assembled gr aee hoste brytons wente london seke allec foude hym slewe hym felowes one called walon deffended hym fyersly fought longe brytons last dyscomfyted brytons tooke hym bonde hys hondes foot regned gouerened londe well nobly noble man well loued amonged brytons pwhan tho rome herde astelepades slayne wonder gladde sente grete prynce romayns yt called costance came ye kyng coill chalege emperour good man gouerned hym wel ondes hym attendaunt vnder gouernaunce pand deuyll ty aun maxence tyme londe gre e herde tydyngs sodeynly became wood sodeynly deyed ended hys lyf pwhan constantyne went thys londe vnto rome tooke wyth hym hys moder eleyne moche wysedome coude th e grete lordes moche loued ye one called hoell another called taberne thyrde morhyn toke alhys londe kepe vnto erle corne wayle called octauyan soo anone thys octauyan wyste hys lorde dwelled rome incotynent seased londe hys honde therwyth dyde hys wyll amonge hyghe lowe hellde hym kynge pwhan tydynges came constantyne emperoure wonder worthee towarde erle octauyan sent taberne wyth xiim men destroye erle hys falsenesse arrayued por tesmouth pand whan octauyan wyst assembled grete power brytons dyscomfyted taberne taberne fledde then scotlonde ordeyned grete power came ayne thys londe another tyme yeue batayll octauian pwhan octauian herde assembled grate power came warde taberne moche myght soo two hostes mette togyders vppon stanesmore strongely smote togyder tho octauian dyscofyted fledde then vnto norwaye taberne seassed londe honde townes castelles moche ther syn octauian came ayen norwaye grete power seased londe hys honde droue romayns tho made kynge regned phow marimian yt emperours cosyn rome spowsed octauians doughter made kynge londe octauian gouerned ye londe well nobly none heyre saue doughter yonge childe loued moche lyfe moche wered syke poynt det myghte lenger regne wold haue made one neuewes haue kynge whyche noble knyght strong man called conan mer edok sholde haue kypte kynges doughter haue maryed whan tyme ben lordes londe wolde suffre yaaf couseyll maryed hygh man grete honour thenne myght haue luste cousell emperour constantyne lorde couseyll accorded chose tho cador cornewaylle go emperour message toke waye wente rome tolde emperoure thys tydynges well wysely emperour sente thys londe wyth hym hys owne cosyn hys vncles sone noble knyght stronge yt called maximian spowsed octauians doughter crowned kynge londe phow maximian themperours cosyn conquered londe armorycam yaaf conan meriedok kynge maximian became soo ryall thougt conquere londe armory cam grete rychesse herde tell yt londe ne lyfe man worthynes knyght squere ne none man ne toke wyth hym grete damage londe lefte home behynde hym noo man kepe londe toke wyth hym fro thys londe xxx thousande knyghtes doughty mennes bodyes wente ouer londe armorycam slewe kynge yt called imball conquered londe whan done called conan sayd moche kynge octauian made kynge brytayne thrugh ye lette dystroubled ye kynge gyue thys londe armorycam make kynge moche ye bryton well londe haue name called armoricam called brytayne londe whens comen shall called moche brytayne soo shall men knowe one brytayne fro thae conan meriedok thaked hym gretly soo made kynge lytell brytayne whan done maximian wente then vnto rome tho made emperour constantyne conan dwelled styll lytell brytayne moche honour lette ordeyne ii thousande plowman londe culture londe harow sowe feffed rychely yt asmoche kyng conan none knyght ne noe othere peple wold take wyues ye nacio frau ce tho sente grete brytayne erle cornewayle called dionothe shold thorugh al londe xim maydens saye viiim meane people iiim grettest lordes sholde spowse whan dyonoth vnderstode made commaundemente thorughout londe brntayne many nombre cam assembldy togyder maydens noo man durste wythstande hys commaundement moche londe take hym warde kepe doo thynge hym good lyked pand whan maydens assembled lete come fore hym atte london lete ordeyne shyppes hastely moche neded vyage tooke owne doughter called vrsula fayrest creature ony man wyst wolde haue sent konge conan sholde haue spowsed made quene londe made pryuely god vowe chastyte fader wyst ne noe man elles lyuynge vpon erthe phow vrsula xi thousande maydens companye wente warde lytell brytayne alle martrde colayne thys vrsula chose vnto company xi thousande maydens lady meystresse wente shyppe one tyme water called tamyse comaunded kynne frendes almyghty god saylled warde lytell brytayne whan come hyghe see stronge tempest arose goddes wyll vrsula wyth shyppes compny dryue hundlonde thrugh temstpe arryued hauen cyte coleyne kynge londe called gowan tho cytee whan wyst tydynges soo many fayre maydens arryued toke elga hys broher hys housholde wyth hym went shyppes see fayre company whan sawe fayre hys company wolde haue ouerlayne take fro ther mayndehode vrsula good mayde coumseylled prayed warned taught theym felowes sholde defende wyth theyr myghte rather suffre deth tha suffre ther body defoyled soo tho maydens became stedfast god defended thrughe hys grace soo none hadde power doo shame wherfore kynge gowan sore anone wrath slewe euerychone anone ryght soo tho maydens martred loue god lyeth coleyne phow kynge gowan came destroy londe man grete power called gracian deifended londe alle thys done kynge gowan sarrasyn called hys brother elga sayde hym sholde go conquere londe alle fayre maydens borne ordened tho grete power pehites denmarke e ay norway came londe brente townes slewe folke caste downe chirches house obbed lond length brede put deth alle tho wolde forsake ryght byleue crystendome moche souerayne myght helpe kyng maximian take hym worthy men whan wente conquere lytell brytayne tyme ye ye telle saynt albon martryd thrugh wo tyr dyoclesyan place abbaye made saynt albon whyles paynym conuerted hym god thrugh predicacyon clerke wyse man called ble rbourghed nyght hys hous thyn carnacyon ihesu cryste ii hondred xxvi yere men shalle vnderstonde saynt albon suffred martyrdom saynt edmonde martryd therfore saynt albon called fyrste martyr englond pthis gowans brother hys folke sarrasyns wet thrugh lode destroyed al thynge foude thynge spared whan tydynges came rome ye kynge gowan begon destroye londe ye emperour come sent stroge greate power called gracian xxiiiim well fyghtynge men caste sarrasyns thys londe arryued portsmouth maximian myght come hymself moche chosen emperour deth constantyne saynt eleyns sone whan gracian arryued hoste lete sapye preuely kyng gowan myght founde sette vpon sodenly laye theyr beddes disco fyted hym slewe ther beddes euerychone none scaped sauff gowan fledde owne countree moche sorowe grete payne psoone befelle maximian slayne atte rome thrughe treason whan gracian wyste tydynge lete crowne hym kynge londe phow gracian made hym kynge whan maximian slayne warde brytons slewe hym wyckednesse gracian whan began regne became wycked soo sterne moche sorowe dyde brytons yt slewe hym amonge ptho whan kynge gowan vnderstode yt gracian slayne done dethe assembled grete power came ayen londe yf fyrste done harme tho dyde moche tho destroyed londe crysten peple moche brytayne man hardy name god dyde anone put strange deth pbut ye bysshop london called gosselim scaped went then rome seke socour helpe dystroy sarrasyns hadde destryed londe romayns sayd ben often enoyed ther sendinge people brytayne helpe brytos wolde nomore soo soo bysshop gosselin wente then wythout ony socoure helpe tho wente kynge lytell brytane called aldroye ye thyrde kynge gowan meryedok sayde pthe bysshop prayed aldroye helpe socoure kynge pyte herte whan herde bysshop fledde crysten men soo slayne grete brytayne thrugh ye paynyms sarrasyns grauted hym costantyne broder helpe wyth power folke dyde arraye hors armour shyppes al thynges neded vyage wha al thinge redy called ye bysshop hym sayde take costantyne broder vpon couenau yf god gyue hym grace paynems sarrasins destroye yt ye make hym kynge bysshop grauted wyth good wyll pconstantyne bysshop toke leue ye king aldroye betoke god toke men xii thousande went ther shyppes saylled warde grete brytayne arryued totnesse pwhan brytons herde tydyng came socoure strongely holpen ordeyned huge bre people came receyued moche honoure pgowan anone wyst tydynges assebled ye sarrasyns cam ayenst yaue batayle costantyne slewe hym owne ho de sarrasyns dyscomfyted slaine noe escaped couerted vnto almyghty god phow constantyne kynges brother lytell brytayne crowned kyng grete brytayne hys grete vertue hys grete worthynesse anone ye batayll wete lo crowned costantyne made hym kyng lode ye bysshop gosselyn sette crowne heed anoynted hym befalleth kynge tho began crystendome ayen londe anone kyng constantyne crowned anone spowsyd hys wyf thrugh couseyll ye brytos begate thre sone fyrst called costance aurilambros ye thyrde vter co stance elder brother whan cam aege made hym monke atte wynchestre constantyne theyr fader thrugh treason slayne pfor befel time pehite came hym vpon day message yt said wold speke ye king preuely couseyll kyng lete voyde chambre men yt ther abode moo yt kyng pehite made coutenauce though wold haue spoken kynge eere slewe loge knyf wente meruaylously chabre nother chabre ye last man wyst become pwhan kynges wyst theyr lorde deed made moche sorowe wyst moche two sone aurilambros vter yonge myght kynge thyrde moke sayd vortiger erle westsex thoughte preuely hys herte thrugt queyntaunce kyng hymselfe went wynchestre constance monke sayde vnto hym constance sayde fader deed two brethern ben wyth gosselyn ye bysshop london nourysshe yonge ye none may kyng wherfore counsell yt ye forsake habyte come wyth shall make suche meane vnto ye brytons yt ye shall made kynge pof constance kynge consta tyne sone monke wynchestre made kynge faders deth thorugh counseyll vortyger erle westsex moche aurylmabros vter hys two brethern yonge aege vortyger lete slee hym kynge hymselfe thys vortyger couselled thys constance moche tyll forsoke hys abbot wete anone crowned kynge thassent brytons thys kynge constance whan crowned made kyng wyst ne knewe lytell worlde ne cude nothynge knyghthode axed made vortiger chyef mayster couseyller gaf hym power toordeyne moche ye reame aperteyned hymself thynge entermedled bare name kynge whan vortiger sawe londe warde gouernall thought preuy treason slee constance kynge myght hym self crowned made kynge regne lete sende hodred kynghtes pehites worthyest ye londe helde hym dwelle kepers hys body wolde goo thorugh londe ordeyne thinges apperteyned kyng vortiger honoured moche hondred kynghtes soo moche yaue golde syluer ryche iewelles robe horse thynges plente wherfore helde hym lorde dyde kynge vortyger tolde yf myght kynge ye thrugh treason wolde make rychest londe soo laste thrugh grete gyftes gyuen largely cryed thrugh courte vortyger beter worthy kynge constance wherfore vortiger made semblaunt ben wrothe departed then courte sayde must goo elles thynges hadde soo traytour sayde cause sholde slee hym y saye constance pwhan thys vortyger gone yt befell soone yt tho hondred kynghtes pehyces brake doores kynges chambre hym slewe smote hys heed ad bare vortiger dwelled soo whan vortiger sawe heed wepte full tenderly eyen neuer theles som deale glad hys berte deth pand anone vortiger sholde put deth thrugh treason falsenesse done brother therfore ladde ouer lytell brytayn kyng receyued moche honour lete nourysshe dwelled tyll became fayre knyght stronge fyers thourght auenged vpon constaunce theyr brother whan sawe theyr tyme dyde ye shalle telle warde pit longe warde ye tydynges came ouersee ye kynred hondred knyght pehites dampned put deth thrugh vortiger thys londe therfore wonderly wrothe swore wolde auenged theyr kynnes men deth came londe greate power robbed many place slewe dyde ye sorowe myght whan vortiger wyst made moche sorowe sore anoyed place also tydynges came hym aurilambros vter brother assembled grete hoste came moche brytayne saye thys londe auenged vpon constance theyr brother deth soo one half brougho moche sorowe ne wyst whether go phow engist xi thousande came londe vortiger yaue place callde thongcastell soone sorowe tydinges came vortyger grete nauy straugers arryued ye coutree cent wyst whes ne wherfore come londe pthe kynge sent anone messager thyder sholde come speke wyth hym wyte folke wert axed coutree wolde pthere two brethern maysters prynces stronge company one called engist horne engist wente kynge tolde hym cause wherfore come londe sayde syrewe ben countree called saxonne ye londe germayne wheryn y moche sorowe people ben soo many londe maye susteynes maysters prynces haue ye londe gouerne rule made come men wymmen boldest ben amonge theym fyghte beste maye trauayll dyuerse londes soo sholde yeue horse harnes armour thynge nedeth shall saye go countree mowelyue theyr cetrees dyde pand therfore syr kynge yf ye haue ought doo wyth company ben comen youre londe wyth good wylle wolde serue londe kepe helpe defende enmyes yf ye nede pwhan vortyger herde tydynges sayde gladly wolde theym wyth holde vppon suche couenanuce yf myghte delyuer hys londe hys enmyes wolde yeue theym resonable lode sholde dwelle euer pengyst thanked hym goodly thys maner co pany xi thousande sholde dwelle wyth kynge vortiger moche dyde thrugh theyr boldenesse delyuered hys londe enmyes clene ptho prayed engyst kynge moche londe myghte make hym cyte hys meyne pthe kynge answered doo wythoute coancell brytons pengist prayed hym eftsones moche plyce myghte compace thonge skyne wherupon myghte make mancer hym dwelle kynge hym graunted freely ptho toke engist bulles skynne kytte sma e myghte oo thonge roude ther compaced moche londe myght thene make vpon fayre castell whan castell made lett calle thongcastell moche ye place marked thonge pof ronowen engistes douhter kynge voreiger spowsed beaute whan castell made full well arayed engist pryuely dyd sende letter ye coutree cam fro c shyppes fylled men ye strong also well fyghtynge bataylles ye sholde also brynge wyth ronowen hys doughter fayrest creture man myghte see pand whan people come hadde sente tooke castell wyth moche ioye hymself vpon daye went vnto kynge prayed hym worthely wolde come see hys newe maneer made place yt compassed wyth thonge skynne kynge anone graunted hym frely hym went thyder well apayed wyth castell wyth fayr werke togyder ete dranke wyth moche ioye whan nyght came kyng vortiger sholde go hys chambre take hys nyghtes reste ronowen yt engistes doughter came wyth cuppe golde honde kneled kynge sayd hym wassaylle kynge knewe meane ne shold answere vpon moche hymself ne none brytons coude noo englysshe spese ne vnderstonde spake langage brytons done yet neuertheles latiner tolde kynge full vnderstandynge therof wassayll sholde drynke hayll fyrste tyme wasshayll drynkhall came vp londe frome ye tyme vnto thys tyme well kyng sholde yeue coutree kent myghte dwelle hys people kynge hym graunted pryuely wyth good wylle anone spowsed ye damoysell moche confusyon hymselfe therfore alle brytons became soo wrothe cause spowsed woman mysbyleue wherfore wente frome hym noo thynge hym tooke ne halpe hym thynge done phow vortimer vortigers sone made kynge engist dryuen vortimer slayne engist wente kente seased ye londe honde hym men bycame lytyll whyle soo grete power moche people hadde men wyste lytell tyme whyche kyng men whyche engistes men wherfore brytons hadde hym dredde sayd amoges theym yf ne toke counseyll bytwene londe sholde bytrayed thrugh engist people pvortiger kyng begoten fyrst wyf thre sone fyrst called vortimer seconde catagien thyrde passent pthe brytons euerychont one assent chose vortimer theyr lod souerayne counseyler euery batayll crowned hym made hym kynge wolde suffre vortiger lenger regne cause alyaunce betwixt engist hym pthe brytons ordeyned grete host dryue engist company londe yaue hym thre bataylles fyrste kente lorde seconde tetforde thyrde shyre thys half colchestre batayll theym mette catagien horne engistes brother eche thym slewe moche countree yeuen longe befor horne thrugh vortiger tho e spowsed cosyn made fayr castell called horne castell owne name vortiger anoyed brother dethe anone lete fell downe castell grounde ne lefte nyght ne daye tyll dryuen engist people londe thene ronowen doughter made sorow ynogh quen ely spake nexte kyng vortimer pryuyest hym moche gaue hym gyftes enpoysoned deyed london fourth yere hys regne lyeth phow brytons chose tyme vortiger theyr kynge engist came londe fought togyders vortimers dethe brytons theyr comyn asset eft sone made vortiger theyr kynge vpon couenaunt sholde neuer suffre engist ne none eft sone come londe wha done ronowen quene pryuely sente letter engist hadde en poysoned vortimer vortiger lorde bare ayen ye crowne regned sholde come ayen londe well arayed wyth moche people auenge hym vppon brytons wynne londe ayen pand whan engist herde tydynges made grete ioy appareylled hym hastely xv thousande men yt deughty euery batayll came londe whan vortyger herde telle engyst come ayen wyth grete power thys londe assembled hys brytons tho went ayenst engyst yeue hym batayll hys folke engist dradde hym sore brytons dryuen hym discomfyted hym stregth wherfore engist prayed hym loue daye sayd comen londe fyght haue hys lond ayen yf myght accorde brytons haue loue grace kynge vortiger thrugh counseyll hys brytons grauted hym loue daye thus ordeyned thrugh brytons yt daye sholde holden fast besyde salysbury vpon hylle engyst sholde come thyder four hordred kdnghtes without moo kyng many wysest men hys londe daye kynge came couseyll ordeyned engist warned hys knyghtes pryuely conmaunded euery one shold put longe knyf hys hose whan sayde fayre syres y tyme speke loue pea euery man anone shold drawe hys kynue slee bryton slewe mlxi knyghtes wyth moche sorowe many escaped kyng vortyger hymself tho taken ladde thongcastell put pryson engystes men wolde kynge brente alle quycke vortiger tho haue hys lyf grauted moche wolde yaue vp londe townes castelles cytees borughs engist folke brytons fledde thes waiys helde styll engyst wente thorugh londe seased londe wyth fraunchyles euery place lete cast downe chyrches house relygyon wasted destroyed crystendome thrughout phow vortyger wente walys beganne castell yt wolde stande wyth morter tempred wyth blood engist departed lond thys maner bytwene hys men lyuerde vortyger pryson suffred hym freely go whyther wolde toke waye wente walys brytons dwelled moche ye londe stronge wycked wynne engyst neuer came therene neuer knew londe pvortiger helde hym wyth hys bratons axed counseyll hym best yaue hym counseyll make stronge castell hym myghte hymself kepe defende yf nede e son haste tho fette began werke vpon ye hylle breigh certes thus befell werke mason made daye downe felle nyght wyste myght ther kynge sore anoyed chaunce wyste werfore lette sende wysest clerkes also lerned men thorugh walys myght foude sholde tell wherfore ye foudament fayled vnder werke sholde hym tell best doo whan wyse men longe tyme studyed sayde kynge sholde doo seke chylde borne woman neuer man chylde sholde slayne tempred blood morter werke soo sholde werke euer endure withouten ende phow kynge lette seke merlyn thorugh walys speke wyth hym kynge herde commaunded messagers anone go thrugh walys seke chylde yf myghte hym fynde sholde hym brynge forthe vnto hym recorde wytnesse thys kynge hadde take letter ne distroubled man ne lette tho messenger wente then spedde soo faste came towne called carmardyne passed theyr waye founde two chyldern xxiiii yere aege thydynge togyder hasty wordes one sayde donebat sayde ye wronge chyde stryue ye haue wytte ne reason haue certes merlyn sayde wytte ne youre reson make force men telle comynly ye haue thynge god myghty syth ye neuer fader euery man knoweth youre moder pthe messenger kynge vortiger whan herde stryue betwixt two gromes axed stode besyde whens marlyn borne also hym nourysshed folke tolde greate gentyll woman hym bare carmadyne called adhanr neuer myght noth man wyte fader pwhan kynges messenger herde tydynges wente anone hym wardeyne towne tolde hym kyng wyll shewed hym leter wherfore come thyder pmerlyn moder fetched wardeyne towne commaunded sholde go kynge ordeyned messagers merlyn moder wente then came vnto ye kynge receyued moche honour kynge axed lady yf ye chylde sone whome hym gate lady answered full tenderly wepynge sayde neuer hadde company worldly man syr sayde yonge mayden faders chambre greate lygnage company oftentymes wente place solace belefte alone chambre wolde goo orthe bernnynge sonne tyme came fayre bacheler entred chambre alone came wyst neuer ne yet knowe doores fast barred dyde game loue ne myght ne power hym defen often came vnto ye forsayd maner begate childe neuer myght wyte pof answere merlyn wherfore kynge axed castel myght stonde begonne ne proue whan merlyn hadde herde moder hadde sayd spake kynge maner psyre begoten axe ye falleth ne none wyte telle cause wherfore brought wherfore ye haue sente ptruely sayd kyng wyse couseyllers haue done vnderstode yt ye morter werke haue begonne behouety thempred blood foundament shall fayle euer psyr sayd merlyn wyll ye slee blood tempre morter ye sayd kyng elles castell shall neuer stande couseyllers vnderstonde tho answerd merlyn kyng syr sayd sayd lete come wyse cou seylles woll preu saye well ne truly whan ye wyse men comen merlyn axed yf blod ye cause make werke stode endure tho wyse men abasshed coude answere merlyn tho sayd kynge syr shall tell ye cause wherfore werke thus fayleth may stande vnder moutayne yt ye haue buylded youre toure grete ponde water ye botome ye ponde vnder ye water ben two dragon ye one whyte ye reede ye fyght togyd ayest werke ye myne depe eyll men come ye pond cause men take way ye water thenne ye shall see ye dragans haue tolde ye togyder fyght ayest werke cause wherfor foudament fayleth kynge anone lete dygge vnder men came ponde lette doo waye water founde two dragon merlyn tolde egerly fought togyder whyte dragon egerly assayled reede lyadde hym strongely myght endure withdrewe hym rested caue wha whyle rested hym wente assayled reede dragon angerly helde hym soo sore yt myght ayenste hym endure withdrewe hym rested came ayen ye whyte dragon strongly fought wyth reede dragon bote hym euyl ouercame fledde then nomore came agayne pof sygnycacyon two dragon botome ponde fought togyder kynge vortyger hys men sawe thys batayll grete meruaysle prayed merlyn tell myght betoken syr quod merlyn shall telle reede dragon betokeneth yourselfe whyte betokeneth folke saxon fyrste ye toke helde londe fyght ayenst haue dryuen enchaced pbut brytons ynure lygnage ouercame droue waye sythen ye comynge ayen saxon recouered londe helde euer droue brytons dyde wyth londe wyll destroyed crystedom thrugh thys londe ye fyrste grete ioye wyth theyr comynge yt y torned grete damage sorowe tho brethern constance kynge whiche ye lete slee shal come quizeme passed grete power lytell brytayne shall auenge deth theyr brother shal brenne fyrst wyth sorowe shall slee grete parte saxon shall dryue remenaut londe therfore abyde ye noo lenger make castell werke anone goo elles youre lyues alle saue god betake trouthe haue sayde thynges shalle befalle pand vnderstande ye welle aurilambros shalle kynge shalle enpoysoned lytell tyme shall regne pof kynge aurilambros pursued vortiger engist deyed merlyn hys moder departed frome kynge torned agayne carmardyn soone tydynges came ye brytons aurilambros vter brother arryued totnesse wyth greate hoste anone brytons assembled wente receyue aurylambros vter wyth grete noblesse vnto london crowned aurylambros made hym kynge dyde vnto hym homage anone axed vortyger kynge myght founde wolde auenged brother dethe wolde warre vpon paynems tolde hym vortyger walys soo ladde hym thyther warde pvortiger wyste welle tho brethern came hym conquere fledde then castell called gerneth stode vppon hyght mountayne hym helde aurilambros vter hys brother theyr folke besyeged castell full long tyme cagell stronge well arrayed pso laste casted wylde fyre brente howses men theyr araye moche wythin castell soo vortiger brente amonge soo deyde wyth moche sorowe ptho engist kente regned ane herde thys tydynges anone fledde wolde haue gone scotlonde haue socoure aurilambros men mette hym north cou tre yane hym batayl engist men defended whyles myghte folke discomfyted slayne octa sone fledde vnto yorke aurilambros hym folowed egerly octa lytell whyle withstode hym warde put hym mercy aurilambros receyued hym hym hys men gaafthe countree galewaye scotlonde dwelled pthe kyng aurilambros wente thorugh londe put awaye name englonde engist hys name called befoere tho lete calle agayne grete brytayne lete make ayen kynge harde stone ben londe irlonde psoth sayde merlyn londe ben none suche gautes sette grete good themself atte euery tyme woude ony maner hurte wysshe stone hote water thenne wysshe ther anone irlonde soo thye dyde whan kynge irlonde culled guillomer herde tell straungers arryued londe asse bled grete power fought ayenst folke dyscomfyted pthe brytons went tyll came mount kyan clymmed vp vnto mounte whan sawe stone maner stode grete meruaylle sayde bytwene themself noo man sholde remeue noo strengthe ne engyne soo grete soo longe merlyn thrugh crafte remeued broughte theyr shyppes came ayen thys londe merlyn sette stone kyng wolde haue sette manner stode irlonde whan ye kynge sawe made thanked merlyn rychely hym rewarded owne wyll place lete calle stonhenge euer phow passent vortigers sone kynge guillomer came thys londe traytour called cappa enpoysoned ye kynge aurilambros men shall vnderstonde passent vortigers sone lyued ye tyme came thys londe wyth grete power arryued north coutre wolde aueged faders deth vortiger strongely trusted vpon company brought wyth hym londe germayne conquered north countree vnto yorke pand whan kynge aurilambros herde assemled grete power brytons went fyght passet dyscomfyted passent peple passent escaped then men fledde then irlonde come kynge guillomer prayed hym helpe socour kynge grauted hym good wyll sayde wolde helpe hym vppon couenaunt selfe muste go power brytayne wolde aduenge vpon broytons rather came londe toke stone strength called gyauntes karoll pthe kyng guillomer lete ordeyne shippes went see xv thousade men arryued walys began robbe moche sorowe dyde pit befell kynge aurilambros laye syke wynchestre myghte helpe hym self sente name vter brother power helpe walys thyther warde went moche myght pthe kynge irlonde passente herde telle aurilambros syke hym came sarrasyn called cappa sayde syre dwelle ye pea host behyght thorugh quayntesye ye shall slee kynge aurilambros syke thenne sayd passent yf ye doo shall rychely auaunce traytour cappa put vpon hym habyte relygyon lete shaue hym brode crowne came vnto kynges courte sayde wolde help kynge malady tho sayd traytour cappa vnto kyng syr good comforte shall yeue suche medicyne ye shalle swete anoe ryght lyste slepe haue good reste traytour yaaf hym suche poyson slepe anone ryghte deyed hys slepynge ye traytour sayd yt wolde go felde tyll awaked escaped awaye man hym suspeccyon cause habyte clothed also hys brode shauen crowne whan kynges men wyste deed became wonder sory faste soughte traytoure myghte fynde hym ye cappa torned ayen vnto hoste frem whes yt came pwhan aurilambbros deyed sterre morne seen wyth clere lyght bought beeme sene heed horryble drago whan kyng aurilambros deed enpoysoned winchestre morne dede aboute tyme pryme sene sterre grete clere beeme sterre brygheter tha ye sonne bought ye beeme apperyd dragon heed hys mouth came two huge lyghtes bryght ony fyre brennynge one beeme warde fraunce streyght ouer see thyther warde beeme came vii beemes full clere longe lyghte fyre pthis erre seen many man none wyste tokened pvter kynges brother walys wyth hys hoste brytons sawe sterre grete lyght yaue wondred ther gretly myghte betoken lete calle merlyn prayed hym telle yt myhght betoken pof betokenynge sterre merlyn sawe ye sterre behelde yt longe tyme sythen quoke wepte tenderly sayde ala ala soo noble kyng worthy y deed iou vnderstande aurilambros brotherds poysoned see well thys sterre yourselfe y betokened heed dragon seen bought beeme y self shall kynge regne beeme stondeth warde eest y vnderstonde ye shall gete sone shall conquere fraunce londes belongeth crowne fraunce shalle wrothyer kynge honoure euer ony auncetours pand beeme stretched towarde irlonde betokened ye shalle gete doughter shalle quene irlonde pand seuen beemes betoken ye shall haue vii sone euery one shall kyng regne wyth moche honoure abyde ye lenger goo yeue batayll enmyes fyghte wyth booldely ye shalle ouercome haue victory pvter thanked hertely merlyn toke men wente warde hys enmyes fought togyder mortally soo dyscomfyted enmyes destroyed hym self slewe passet vortigers sone brytons slewe guillomer kyng irlonde men pand vter anone batayll toke hys waye warde wynchestre doo entyere aurilambros kynge brother tho body borne vnto stonhenge moche honour done make remembrau ce brytons slayne thrugh treason engist day sholde haue ben accorded place entyered aurelambros seconde yere hys regne wyth ye worshyp ye myght belonge suche kynge whoos soule god haue mercy amen pof vter pendragon therfore called ye shall fre de hys kynne os hys brother taken londe humbre vnto yorke yorke helde strongely agaynst wolde suffre come cytee neyther yelde cytee besyeged towne anone ryght yaue therto stronge assawte cyte kept well strongely pand whan vter herd therof came thyther wyth grete stronge power helpe rescowe ye towne put way syege yaue stronge batayll octa company defended well myght ye laste dyscofyted partye slayne octa os taken put pryson london pand vter hymfelf dwelled whyle atte yorke wente london eester wold vere crowne holde solempne feest lette somone erle baron sholde come feest hadde wyues sholde brynge also feest seygnoury came kynges co maundemente commaunded pthe feest rychely arayed holden worthely sette meete astate soo erle gorloys cornewaylle igreyne wyf sate nexte vnto kynge whan kyng sawe fayrnesse lady beaute anone rauysshed beaute often made nyce countenaunce lokynge laughynge laste erle perceyued preuy lokynge laughynge loue bytwene roso vp table wrathe toke wyf nd called hym hys knyghtes wente then wrath wythout takynge leue ye kynge pthe kynge anone sente hym sholde come agayne goo then dyspyte hym erle wolde come agayne maner wyse pwherfore kynge wrothe wrathe hym defyed deedly enmye pand erle wente then cornewaylle wyfe castell tyntagyll pand kynge lete ordeyne grete host came cornewaylle destroye erle yf myghte hadde put hym suche castell stronge welle arayed called tyntagyll wollde yelde hym kynge pand kynge anone besyeged called dwelled xv dayes neuer myghte spede euer thought vppon igreyne vpon layde moche loue wyste doo pso laste called hym knyght called vlfin preuy wyth hym tolde hym hys counseyll axed hym wha best done psyr sayde sende merlyn anone came telle beste counseyll ony man lyuynge merlyn anone sente came kynge kynge tolde hym counseyll wyll syr sayd merlyn shall doo moche thrugh crafte shalle make come nyght castell tyntagyll shall haue yo wyll lady vter begate igreyne erles wyf cornewaylle arthur merlyn thrugh craft yt co kynges fygure erle vlfin garlois fygure iorda erles chambrelayne ec transfygured others lyke merlyn soo done sayde syr sayd ye may goo castell tyntagyll axe ene wyll kynge toke pry gouerne lede knyght moche loued tooke waye towarde castell hym toke vlfin chambrelayne merlyn whan came thyder porter demyd ben hys owne lorde whan tyme came go bedde kynge went bedde igreyne erles wyf dyde alle wyll begate vpon sone called arthur vppon kynge tooke leue lady wente ayen hys hoste nyghte kynge laye igreyne bedde erles wyf kynges men gaaf grete assawte vnto castell erle hys men manly defended laste befell assawte erle hym self slayne castell taken pand kynge anone torned againe tyntagill spowsed greyne moche honour made quene pand soone tyme came sholde lyuered bare chylde sonne yt called arthur gate doughter called amya whan came aege noble baron lorde lyon weded pwhan vter longe tyme regned ther came vpon hym grete sykenesse sorowe pand ye meane tyme kepe octa yt engistes sone os brother thene pryson lete go grete yeftes yaue went wyth whan tho two brethern escaped theyr owne countree agayne thenne ordeynede gret power folke began warre ayen vpon kynge phow kyng vter loth kepe londe brytayne whyle seke moche might syknesse moche kynge vter syke myght helpe hym self aloth sone eleyne tho cho wardeyne chyeftayne alle soo anone hys bry mbled grete hoste yaue bataylle folke octa last pit befell thus warde ytons dedignacion aloth othe hym attendaut wherfore anoyed wonder sore lete put hoste amonges folke de hym vereloyne yt tho fayre cyte saynt albon martred cytee destroyed wyth paynems thrugh warre thyther hadde sente octauian os ther people entered towne lete make sure ye yates helde kynge came besyeged made stroge assawte within manly theym deffended pthe kyng lete ordeyne gunnes engynes breke walles walles soo stronge man myghte mysdo pocta people grete despyte kynge lyenge letere ym besyeged toke counseyll among stande vp morowe erly come yeue batayll kynge soo dyde batayle octa os slayne ye escaped lyue fledde scotlonde made colegyn theyr chyeftayne saxon yt lyue escaped fro batayll brougth ayen grete stregth amoge sayd kyng vt deed sholde well conquere londe thought enpoysen kynge ordeyned men dede yaue yef ti grete plente thynge ordeyned thyderwarde ye kynge dwellyng clothed poore wede better spede theyr fals purpose neuertheles theyr falsenes subtylte myght neuer come nygh ye kyng last aspyed kynge dranke noo lycoure water clere wel tha nyghe besyde ye fals traytours vpon daye preuely wente welle put therin poyson soo water enpoysoned anone kynge dronke water began swelle soone deyed many dranke water deyed also anone thys aspyed folke towne lette stoppe welle euermore pwhan ye kynge deed folke bare hym stonhenge wyth grete solempnyte bysshops baron hym burye besyde aurilambros hys bro torned ayen tho euerychone sent sone made kyng londe moche reuerence faders deth xvii yere regne phow kynge arthur sone vter crowned faders deth droue colegryn saxon cheldri mayne londe arthur made kyng londe yonge aege xv yere fayr bolde doughty body meke folke good curteys large spendinge made hym welle beloued amonge yt nede whan began regne heswore truely ye saxon neuer shold haue reste ne pea tyll hadde dryuen londe asse bled greate hoste fought wyth colegryn whyche ye tyme octa deed saxon mayntened thys colegryn dyscomfyted fledde vnto yorke tooke towne hym helde kyng besyeged hym myght thynge spede cyte strong wythin towne kept cyte well orpedly pand mene tyme colegryn lette towne bladulf f ledde hymselfe cheldryk yt kynge almayne haue hym socour kynge assembled grette power came arryued scotlonde xv hondred shyppes wha arthur wyst tydynges power strength ynough fyght ayenst cheldrik lete syege went london sent anone letter ye kynge lytell brytayne wy called howell hys neuewe hys systers sone sholde come hym power myghte assembled grete hoste arryued southampton whan kynge arthur wyst gladde ynough wente ayenste receyued wyth moche honour soo two host mette assembled tooke theyr waye euen vnto nycholl cheldryk besyeged taken came vpon cheldrik people wyst egerly assaylled pthe kynge cheldrik men defended hym manly theyr power kyng arthur hys men slewe many saxon hat neuer seen suche slaughter cheldrik hys men left alyue fledde waye kynge arthur pursewed droue wood tha myghte ferder passe pcheldrik hys sawe well brought moche dysease yelded kynge arthur thys manner wy sholde take theyr horse theyr armour must go foot theyr shyppes wolde goo home theyr owne londe neuer come ayen londe pand vpon assuraunce thys thynge yaue hym good hostage pand arthur counseyll men graunted thynge receyued ye hostage therupon yt wente theyr shyppes whan ye hyghe see wynnde chaunged deuyll wolde torned theyr nauy cam ayen scotlonde ouer see arryued fast kynge arthur hoste none wyst therof went warde hym yaue hym bataylle ouercame hym anone ryght guillomer fledde wyth hys agayne irlond whan thys done dyscomfyted hym arthur torned hym ayen place lefte scottes wolde haue slayne bysshopes abbottes folke ye countree ladyes open heeded came kynge arthur cryed hym mercy sayde syre gentyll kynge myghty haue mercy pyte vpon v ryght lawe holde mayntene crystendome full grete dyshoudur yt shold slee hym byleueth almyghty god ye goddes loue haue mercy pyte v suffre v haue hadde moche sorowe payne saxon haue many tymes passed thrugh londe ynough often tymes haue done v sorowe dysease castelles haue taken beestes slayne eten moche harme haue v done yf ye wolde v slee none honour kynge slee crye hym mercy ynough ye dyspended theyr vytayle wythin grete hungre became amonge deyed wenderly thycke within cyte ho gre came vnto froll prayed hym accorded kynge arthur haue pea wolde yelde theym vnto hym cyte also pfroll yt wolde none hys people vndertoke batayle hym pand vpon morne came wel arayed without parys sholde fyght anone smote togyders fyersly wel fough sydes man demed better soo befell ye froll yaue arthur suche stroke yt kneled grounde wolde nolde froll wounded kynge arthur forhede yt blode felle downe eyen face arthur anone sterre vp hertely whan felte hym hurte man yt semed almoost wood toke taburne hys good swerde drewe vpon hyghe yaaf froll suche astroke thyr claue hede downe sholders helme myght warraunt fel downe deed place thenne tho cytye made grete sorowe froll euerychone yelded kynge hys noble knyghthode hadde also hys owne worthynes man neuer grete lorde durste meue warre ayenst hym nother aryse make londe frau ce inquyete pea dwelled ix yere dyde many greate wonder repreued many proude men euyll tyrautes theym chastysed theyr demerytes phow kynge arthur auaunced men trauaylled seruyce warde yt befel thus ester helde feest para rychely gan auauce knyghtes ye seruyce hym holpen hys coquest yaue hys stewarde called kay augien angoers yaue bed butler normandye tho called neustrye holde hys chambrelayn yaue flaunders mance dorell hys cosyn yaue bolayne rycharde hys enewe yaue pountyf yaue large londes fee estate whan arthur thus knyghtes feoffed aperyll next suynge came ayen brytayne hys owne londe wytsontyde sewynge counseyll baron wolde crowned kynge glomergon helde moo ryche lordes brytons came moo saye dippon donande gennes many named atte feest many fayre feest kynge arthur hadde holde neuer none suche ne soo solempne lasted xv dayes wyth moche honoure myrthe pof letter yt set fro rome pryde kynge arthur thyrde daye kynge arthur satte meet amonge knyghtes amonge satte feste cam xii men age rychely arayed curteusly salewed kynge sayde came fro rome sente massengers fro emperoure toke hym letter thus moche vnderstad pgretely v maruaylleth arthur thou art one hardy thyn eyen thy heed make open warre contake ayenst v rome owne worlde redeme thou haste neuer yet thys tyme proued ne assayed strengthe roma therfore though shall lytell tyme iulyus cezar conquered londe brytayne ayd toke therof truage folke haue longe nowe throughe thy pryde thou holde countree soo bolde ne hardy durste fyght hym ne come nye place yt gyaunt dwelled tha called dinabus moche sorowe dyde countree pwhan kynge arthur heede tydynges called kay bedwere comaunded go pryuely oswalde soo peanda came northumberlonde yaue batayll vnto oswalde batayll oswalde slayne heed smyten entered abbay berdenay whiche place god hadde wrought hym many fayre myracle bothe elles pand anone oswy brother seased londe honde oswaldis folke northumberlonde loued wonderly well helde hym theyr lorde men kynne worthy ynough wolde haue departed londe warred togyed well asmoche stronge ynoughe came peanda prayed hym helpe socour behyght hym ye lode largely vpo couenat wold gouerne helpe counseyl ppeanda herde theyr prayer spake cadwalyn sholde ordayne grete host faste ordeyned hym northumberlonde teyght oswy oswy meke man moche loued pea charyte prayed peanda loue pea profe ede hym golde syluer grete plentye pand peanda proude yt nolde graunt hym pea fo maner thynge thynge wolde hym fyght laste sette daye batayll oswy euer trusted vpon god peanda trusted tomoche vpon pryde vpon hoste gyder smote egerly peanda anone dyscomforted slayne incarnacyon oure lorde ihesu cryste vclv yere oswy regned xxviii yere kynge called oswyne peandaes cosyn warred vpon hym togyder fought oswy hadde victory oswyne oswyn dyscomforted slalyne lyeth tynnemouth phow kynge cadwaldre cadwalins sone regned fader laste kynge brytons deth cadwelin regned hys sone cudwaldre well nobly moder ye syster peanda whan regned xii yere felle grete sykenesse thenne greate dyscorde bytwene lordes londe euery warred vpon yet tyme fell grete derth scarsyte corn viteylles londe man myghte go iii iiii dayes fro towne towne yt sholde fynde bye golde ne syluer brede wyne ne none vitayle wich man myght lyue onely people lyued rotis herbes lyuynge none moche faylled aboute fysshes wylde bestes thynge soo yet mysauenture felle soo greate mortalyte pestelens amonge people corrupcyon ayre ye lyuynge people suffysed burye deed bodyes deyed soo sodenly bothe grete smalle lorde seruaunt etynge goynge spekynge fell downe deyed neuer herde sodeyne deth amonge people wente burye deed body deed body noman trauayle tylthe londe londe barayne corne fruytes defawte tyllyers mysauenture dured xi yere noman myght ere ne sowe phow cadwaldre wente londe lytell brytayne cadwaldre sawe grete hungre mortalyte pestylence londe poore faylynge cornes ad vytaylles folke perysshed sawe also mooste partye londe wasted voyde people apparelled hym folke lefte alyue passede ouer lytell brytayne lytell nauy vnto kynge alayne moche loued cosyn fader hadde moche loued tyme sayled see made moche lamentacyon dyde alle tho hym sayde dedisti no domine tanquan oues escaru et gentibus dispersisti no thenne pof kynge alured danys tyme prayed hym mercy myght goo londe pthys tyme came danys englonde deth eldred regned hys broder alured dolfynes called ptho wente danys assembled wente seke alured yt tho kyng newe made southsex fou de hym atte wylton wyth lytell people neuerthelesse faught laste fledde then felde wente westsex ordeyned moche people owne reame also tyll stronge hoste soo danys hadde power ayenst hym withstande came london hoste danys soionrned wolde haue foughten ye danys durste hym fyght prayed hym pea myghte goo ayen theyr owne countree neuer come englonde ayen saye ony harme vppon thys couenaunt sholde gyue hym pledge good hosta e suche englysshmen wolde phow hubba hungar slayne atte chyppenham danys brought theyr kynge kynge daye danys departed frome london soo faste rode bothe nyghe daye neuer tooke rest goynge tyll came vnto excestre tooke tho towne helde pwhan kynge alured herde rydynges anone lette take hostage wente then vnto excestre wyth power hadde whan danys herde telle hys comynge wente frome then unto westsix came vnto chyppenham dyde moche harme countree robbed folke brough theym pryson kynge alured pursewed came vpon ryght soone fyersely theym assayled slayne bothe hubba hugar broder buerne bocader bataylle moche folke slayne one gre felde bode danys moche kyng came fewe folke pthe kynge hasted hym moche myghte goo agayne whan danys founde hubbaes body lyeng deed buryed layd vpon grete logge lete calle hubeslowe soo called vnto thys daye place deuenshyre baron somerset wyltshyre dorset herde tell theyr kyng dyscomfyted ordeyned power myghte haue came kyng thanked god hym yet founde alyue wende ye danys hadde hym slayne tho toke counseyll kynge baros wolde go seke danys fyght rode nyght theim seke came morowe aboute pryme abyndon danys kyng alured baron assembled assaylled danys egerly yaue stonge batayll danys put longe tyme noo man wyst whether parte people slayne thys befell god wolde kyng alured victory moche honoure danys soo dryuen ne wyst whyther torne xv dayes yng pursewed wyll gladly ayne speke pea accorde toke hym good hostage sayd wolde neuer vpon hym warre ne debate arere pand ouer behyght vnto kyng alured wolde go b ynhe theyr owne kynge vnto hym theyr kynge shold baptysed vpon condycyon kynge alured graunte lyf lymme sayd vnto theym sholde gone theyr kyng seke certayne daye come ayen yt theym sette wente forth fast came ayen daye assygned ye danys brought theyr kynge pthe kyng alured anone lette e baptysed theyr name chaunged soo kynge denmark called athelstone xxx felowes name chaunged also baptysed ryght byleue pand done atte westmestre kynge alured helde wyth hym kynge athelstone hys danys xii dayes soiourne moche solempnyte yaue th grete yeftes baptysed soo departed tho kynge alured ease whan hadde enmyes ouer comen torned ye ryght leue god almyghty phow danys came fraunce gurmonde came agayne englonde deth kynge alured thus befell warde danys northumberlonde yt paynems came grete strength huge hoste frauce vnderstode went frauce gurmonde affyke whan conquered englonde yaue vnto ye saxon tho yt came fro frauce arryued kent sent northumberlonde shold come whan two host come assembled anone yede destroye alle crysten people englonde place place dyde moche sorowe befelle thus almyghty god wolde harde chaunce englonde good kyng alured yt wonte abate ye danys deyed n meane tyme thys kynge alured regned xxx yere good kyng welle coude chastyse enmyes also good clerke lete make many bokes boke made englysshe aduentures kynges bataylles ben done londe many bookes gestes lete wryte greate wysdome good lernynge thrugh whyche bookes many man may hym amende woll rede vpon loke vpon whose soule almyghty god haue marcy pand thys kynge alured lyeth wynchestre iohanes viii pope adryan viii yere iohannes anoynted karolus emperour suffred grete wronge ye romayns fauoured ye sayd emperour therfore put sayd pope kepyng also degarded bysshop portuense whyche ye occasyon sorowe karol ye seconde empour ludouicus karolus brother whyche called ludouicus kyng germayne ordeyned batayll agaynst brother karolus faughte poysened made many monasterye pmartynus pope ioha ne one yere martynus sone wha regned foure yere helde batayll ayenst danys droue kynge gaufride kyng danys hoste vnto see ested scotlonde toke strongely al countree hoole yere yt tho comberlonde settes westmerlonde begane adelstone sone edmode worthy man doughty knyghte body noble also thyrde yere kynge wente ouer homber countree whiche coutree fonude two kynges danys one called enelaf renant kynge edmonde droue bothe fro londe wente toke grete proye comberlonde edmonde regned vii yere lyeth glastenbury pof kynge eldred edmode regned eldred broder auenged edwarde fader enmyes dyde hym slee seased northumberlonde whoos goodnes saynt dunstane preched kynge eldred regned xi yere lyeth whynchester pof kynge edwyn eldred regned edwyn sone edmonde symple man warde god people hated folke owne londe loued honoured brother man moche loued god pea ryght hooly chyrche also worthy man grete lord blood myghty maycened well londe pea edgar lorde kynge aboue kynge scotlonde walys fro tyme arthur gone neuer sythen kynge power pand edgar saynt edwardes fader whan edgar wyf deed yt saynt edwardes moder entryd herde speke fayrnesse estrylde orgarus doughter baron deuenshyre fayre woman men dyde speke called one hys knyhhtes moche loued trusted vpon tolde hym go sayde noble baron orgarus deuenshyre see yf hys doughter fayre men speke yf sothe wyll haue vnto wyfe pthis knyght called edelwolde wente forthe waye kynge hym sayd came lady whan sawe fayre thought haue hymself wyfe therof spake grgarus fader fader olde man man chyldern oonly sawe yt edelwode fayre yonge knyght kyng thought doughter sholde well maryed sette vpon hym graunted hym doughter yf good lorde ye kynge wolde consente therto pand thenne thys edel wolde came ayen vnto kynge colde hym fayre ynough vpon see wonder lothly ptho answerede kynge sayd toke lytell charge syr sayd edelwolde faders heyre ryche londes yf ye wolde consente graunte myght haue thenne sholde ryche ynough goddes name sayde kynge consente therto edel wolde tho thanked kynge ryght mothe wente ayen deuenshyre spowsed damoysell coutree dwelled pand thus befell vpon tyme tolde couseyll thynge vnto wyf maner begyled lord kynge wolde haue hadde wyfe anone wyst loued neuer warde dyde pthys lady conceyued hym sone whan tyme wan chylde sholde borne edelwolde came kynge prayed hym haue sone fonte stone kynge hym graunted lete calle hym edgar owne name whan done thought alle syker ynough kynge wolde take hys wyf moche hys lord ioly man amerous phow kynge edgar wedded estrylde deth edel wolde thus befell men kynge edgar courte thene spake sayd yt edel wolde rychely auaunced thrugh forsayd maryage wyf yet sayd auaunced hondred folde spowsed moost fayrest creature yt euer seen ye kyng herde speke moche beaute yt thought wolde haue hym dysceyued begyled thought pryuely herte wolde goo deuenshyre hunte harte ye hynde wylde beestes thene sholde see lady departed then lady dwellynge manere place besyde forest kynge wolde hunte manere borowed nyghte whan tyme came kynge sholde suppe sonne shone kyng asked gossyppe hys godsone edelwolde made come kynge neuerthelesse yf wyse myght haue sholde haue come hys syght hys wyll pthe lady welcome kynge swetely hym kyssed toke ye honde nexte hym sa te souped togyder pand custome vsage londe tyme whan drake drynker sholde saye wassayll sholde answere saye drynke hayll thys dyde kynge lady kyste many tymes supper whan tyme go bedde kynge wente bedde kynge hertely ayrnesse lady thene ouer come loue hym thought sholde deye yf hadde wyll pvppon morowe kynge aroos foreest wente hym dysporte wyth harte hyndes wylde beestes hertes grete plente sence ye lady thryes went solace speke wyth lady whyles dwelled countree pand kyng remeued then thought hym myghte best delyuer edelwod fro hys wyf hym fyrste desceyued kynge anone viii dayes ordeyned parlyament salysbury baronage counseyll haue ordeyne countree northumberlonde sholde best kepte danys came londe destroye thys edelwode came vnto kyng peter helpe meruellously saynte peter delyuered hym wyf doughter ye emperour constantynopolytan roman bloode man crowned benedictus pope pof saynte edwarde martyr escrylde hys stepmoder lete kylle hym make eldred owne sone kynge edgar regned edwarde sone begate vpon hys fyrste wyfe wyll nobly gouerned londe full maner goodnes ledde full holy lyf aboue thynge loued god holy chyrche quene escrylde stepmoder lete slee hym cause make owne sone eldred kynge daye slayne ye shalle afterwarde pit befell thus vpon day tha kynge edwarde wente woode playe southe coutree syde towne called warham yt whiche foreste grete pleyntye harte hyndes whan ben whyle hym playe thought vpon broder eldrede hys moder quene place waste nygh foreste thought goo thyder vysyte see hys brother toke hym lytell meyne wente hym towarde hys stepmoders hous tyme soiourned castell corfe rede ye thyckensse wood speye hys game befell wente amysse loste hys meyne hym came laste came wood lo hym sawe fast besydes e hys stepmoder dwelled thyder warde wente alone anone tolde quene kyng comen alone wyth ony company therfore made ioy ynough thought myght slayne pryuely myght called one knyghtes whome tolde moche counseyll bytwene bothe came kynge curteysly hym receyued pand kynge tolde come vysyte also speke eldred broder quene many tymes hym thankyd hym prayed alyght borugh al yt nyght pthe kynge sayd myght agayne wold goo vnto hys folke yf myghte theym fynde pand whan quene sawe wolde abyde prayed hym wolde one drynke graunted anone drynke come quene dranke vnto kynge kynge tooke cuppe sette mouth meane whyle dranke false knyght yt ye quene knyfe smote kyng vnto herte fell downe deed vnto erthe palfroy quene dede gaue knyght golde syluer greate plente ryches ynough knyght anone thys done wente hym ouer see escaped oute londe pwhan kyng edwarde thus martred yere incarnacyon lorde ihesu cryste ixclxxx regned xii yere halfe lyeth glastenbury pof kynge eldred kynge swyne denmake helde englonde grete payne thys fygure sayd trusted thynge mercy god thyng profyted hym yt done hym goten extorcyon vniustely thenne bysshop left bysshopryche dred thys syght went monastery lyued vertuously hys dayes piohanes x pope hym xi yere lytell profyted pof kynge knoght dane dethe eldred knoght dane began regne edmonde irensyde kyng eldredes sone fyrste wyf ordeyned grete power men began warre kyng knoghte dyde many tymes often warre stronge harde ye wonder wyte pand quene emme dwelled tho westmestre grete drede two sone warre alured edwarde lest sholde defoyled mysdone thorugh warre wherfore sente theym ouer ye see normandy ye duke rycharde theyr vncle dwelled saufte pea longe tyme pthis edmonde irensyde knoght dane warred strongely gyder last accorded manere yt sholde departe ye reame betwixt soo dyde became good frendes well loued gyder ben brethern goten one fader one moder borne phow kynge edmonde irensyde traytoursly slayne thorugh traytour ralled eldred strotton tho regned kynge irensyde knoght dane thus befel afterwarde yere accorded moche loued gyder wherfore fals traytour hadde enuytee loue betwixt theym frendshyp whoos name edrith stratton yt grete lord edmonde irensydes man hym helde londe neuertheles thought lord betray make knoght kynge londe entente rychely auauced hym well beloued wherfore prayed hys lord edmonde irensyde vppon daye wyth hym ete kynge hym curteysly graunted hym came prayer mete ye kynge ryally serued wyth dyuers meete drynkes whan nyght came yt sholde go vnto bedde kynge toke owne meyne went vnto chambre yt sholde take nyghtes reste loked hym sawe fayre ymyge well made semblaut archer boowe boowe fyne arowe pkynge edmonde wente tho nere beholde better myght anon arowe smote hym thrughe body slewe kynge engyne made slee owne lorde traytoursly pand soo whan kynge edmode thus deed slayne regned x yere peple hym made moche sorowe body ba e vnto glastenbury theym hym en yred pand fals traytour edrith anone went unto quene kynge edmondes wyf wyst lordes dethe anone toke frome tow sone fayre yonge lorde vpon goten one called edward edwyn lawe theym hym londen toke vnto kynge knoght yt sholde wyth wyll tolde hym subtylly slayne kyng edmonde cause loue hym kynge knoght englonde power hooly myghte haue po thou fals traytoure haste thou true brother soo true thus slayne loued ye world heed shall thy traueyll well rewarde thou hast deserued anone lett hym take bounde honde foot maner traytour lete cast hym tamyse thys maner fals traytour ended lyf kynge toke two childern put unto abbot westmestre warde kepe tyll wyst best phow kynge knoght sente kynge edmondes sone demarke slayne saued befell soone kynge knoghte londe honde spowsed quene emme thorughe consente baronage fayre woman whiche eldredes wyf duke syster normandye lyued togyder moche loue reason wolde kynge axed vpon daye counseyll quene best sonnes edmonde irensydes syre sayd ben ryght heyres ye londe yf lyue wyll moche sorowe warre therfore lete sende strange londe ferre man maye defoyle destroy kynge anone lete calle dane called walgar commaunded hym sholde lede tho two childern denmarke soo doo ordeyne sholde neuer theym syr sayde walgar gladly commaundement shall done anone tho two chyldern toke ladde denmarke moche sawe chyldern wonder fayr also meke grete pyte ruthe wolde slee ladde kynge hungry noursshe walgar well knowen kynge well beloued anone kynge axed whens childern walgar tolde hym sayde ryght heyres englonde therfore men wolde destroye therfore syr vnto come mercy helpe seke sothe yf may lyue men shal become shall holde theyr londe kynge hungry receyued wyth moche honour lete worthely kepte pand thus befell warde edwyne ye yonger brother deyed edwarde ye elder brother lyued fayre man stronge large body gentyll curteys condycyons yt men hym loued edwarde cronycles called amonge englysshmen edwarde ye outlawe pand whan made knyght kynges doughter hugry hym moche loued hys goodnes hys fayrnes called derlyng kynge fader perceyued well loue betwixt two heyre doughter kyng vowche sauf doughter man well dyde hym loued soo well yaue vnto hym good wyll edwarde spowsed moche honour kynge hungry sente hys baronage made solempne feest ryche weddynge made vnderstande edwarde sholde kynge londe decesse hym tydynges full gladde edward begate vppon lady sone called edgar helynge afterwarde doughter called margarete afterwarde quene scotlonde kynge scotlonde yt called mancolin doughter called maude yt quene afterwarde englonde thrugh kynge henry fyrste sone conquerour wedded begate doughter called maude afterwarde empresse almayn maude came ye kynge englonde vnto thys daye called henry empresse sone yet hadde thys edwarde doughter hys wyfe called crysten nonne phow kynge knoght proude man conquered normandy became afterwarde meke mylde haue herde edmonde irensydes sone kynge knoght wende ben slayne commaunded walgar kynge knoght hadde honde reame englonde denmarke wente vnto norwaye londe conquere kynge lond called elat came people wende londe haue well kepte defended soo faught wyth hym tyll laste slayne batayll tho knoght toke londe hys honde whan conquered norway taken feaute homage came ayen englonde helde hym self grete lord hym thought world hys pere noo man came soo proude hauteyne grete wonder pand befell vpon daye herde masse westmestre wolde haue gone hys palays wayes tamyse swyftely ayenst hym came almoost touched foot tho sayd kynge proude herte comaunde water torne ayen elles shall make wawes comaundemente wolde spare flowed euer heyght pthe kynge proude herte wolde flee water bete rodde hys honde comaunded water sholde go ferder comaundemet water wolde cesse euer wexed hygh kyng wete stode depe water whan sawe abyden longe water wolde thynge comaundemet tho soone drewe hym tho stode vpon stone helde hondes hyghe sayde wordes herynge alle people pthis god maketh see thus aryse kynge kyng myghtes moost catyf man deedly maye neuer deye thynge dothe hys commaundement hym obedyent pto god praye warraunt knowlege caytyf feble power therfore wyll goo vnto rome without ony longe lettynge wyckednesse punysshe amende god clayme londe holde none anon made redy heyre hym selfe wente rome withoute ony lettynge waye dyde many almesse dedes whan came rome also whan hadde synnes doo penaunce came ayen englonde became good man holy lyued lefte alle manere pryde stoutenes lyued hooly lyfe made two abbayes af saynt benet one englonde normandye moche loued saynte benet specyally thanne sayntes moche loued saynt edmonde kynge ofte yaue greate yeftes se wherfore made ryche pand whan hadde regned xx yere deyed lyeth wynchestre panno dm mxviii benedictus ix pope iohannes grete lechour therfore dampned apperyd certayne man vnder meruaylous fygure horryble heed tayle lyke asse parte body lyke bere sayd man apperyd aferde man ye apeyre lyued vnhappely olde tyme lyke beest whan pope mannes tyme grete dyuysyon sclauder ye chirche put two tymes pand tholomeus noteth pryde bysshops hadde euer euyll ende euer occasyon moche vnrest batayll pconradu ye fyrst emperour henricus xx yere man made many lawes commaunded pea kepte moost straytly ony man erle ludolf accused fledde frome londe desyred lyue lyke churle lyke gentyll man yet meruayllously sone made emperour comaundemente god ayenst wyll conradus laste accorded toke corodis doughter wyf pof kynge harold leuer goo foot ryde hors knoght haue spoken hadde two sone wyf emme one called hardyknoght harold lyght foot men called hym moost comynly harolde hare foot harold thynge condycyons maners kyng noghte fader sette lytell pryce chyualrye ne noo curteyse nother worshyp hys owne wyll became soo wycked exyled hys moder emme went ye lode flau dres dwelled erle wherfore neuer good loue betwixt hym broder broder hated hym deedly whan regned two yere lytell deyed lyeth westmestre pof kynge kariknoght haroldes brother harold hare foot regned brother hardiknoght noble knyghte worthy man moche loued chyualry maner goodnes whan thys hardiknoght regned lytell whyle lette vncouere hys brother harold smote heed brother att westmestre lete cast heed gonge body tamyse came fysshers toke body theyr nettes nyght bare hym saynt clementes chyrche hym caryed maner auenged hym hardiknoght hys broder none maner myght auengeb kyng hardiknoght large yeuer meete drynke table sete euery daye thre tymes full ryall meetes drynkes owne meyne came vnto hys courte rychely serued ryall meetes thys kynge hardiknoght sent emme moder made come ayen englonde dryuen englonde whyle harold hare f ot regned thrugh counseyll erle godewin yt tho grettest lorde englonde next kyng moost myght thrugh oute englonde wolde hys comaudement moche hys spoused doughter ye good kyng knoght dane whiche doughter hys fyrste wyfe pand whan quene dryuen englonde come erle flaundres called balde wyne cosyn founde thynge neded vnto tyme went ayen englonde kynge hardiknoght sente sone made come ayen moche honour kynge hardyknoght whan regned fyue yere deyed lyeth westmestre pof vylany dany dyde ye englysshmen wherfore fro ye tyme dane made kynge londe deth kynge hardyknoght moche hadde noo thynge hys body begoten erles baron assembled made cousell neuer noo man ye dane though neuer grete man amonges sholde neuer kynge englonde despyte dane hadde done englysshmen euermoore yf englysshmen danys hapened mete vpon brydge englysshmen sholde hardy meue ne styre foot stande styll tyll dane passed ouer yf ye englysshmen bowed downe theyr heedes doo reuerence vnto danys sholde haue ben beten defoylled suche maner despytes vylany dyde danys englysshmen wherfore dryuen ye londe tyme kynge hardyknoght deed lord ye theym myght mayntene pand maner auoyded danys englonde neuer came ayen pthe erles baron theyr comyn assent theyr counselles sent unto normandy seke two brethern alured edwarde yt dwellyng duke richharde theyr came entente crowne alured elder brother hym make kynge englonde kynge make ende erles baron made theyr othe erle godewin westsex falsely traytoursly thought slee se two brethern anone sholde come englonde entent make hys sone harolde kynge whyche sone begote vp wyf whiche kynge knoghtes doughter dane godewin pryuely hym wente south hampton mete two brethern whan sholde come vnto london pand thus befell messenger went normandy foude oonly alured elder brother edwarde hys brother gone hugry speke cosyn edwarde outlawe yt edmonde sone irensyde messenger tolde sayde alured erles baron englonde sente hym boldely sholde come englonde receyue reame kynge hardiknoght deed dane dryuen londe phow godewin fals traytour toke alured vppon gyldesdowne whan came normandy kynge englonde caused hym martyred yle ely alured herde tydynges tha ked god shyppe went hast yt myght passed see arryued southhampton godewin fals traytour whan traytour sawe come welcomed hym receyued hym moche ioye sayd wolde lede hym london ye baron englonde hym abode make hym kynge went theyr waye warde london whan came gyldesdowne tho sayd traytour godewin vnto alured take kepe aboute left syde ryght syde ye shall kynge suche hondred forsothe sayd alured behyght yf kynge shall ordeyne make suche lawes wherfore god man shal ell pleased traytour com al men yt hym wh come vpon gyldesdowne lee aluredes copany hym fro normandy take alured lede hym yle ely put hys eyen heed afterwarde brynge hym ye deth dyde slewe al ye copany ye nobre xii gentylmen come hym fro normady toke alured ye yle ely put eyen rent hys wombe toke chyef bowel put steke groude ende ye bowel ther fastened nedles eylesse yren prycked good chylde made hym go ye stake tyll yt al bowel drawe body dyed alured thrugh treason erle godewin pwhan lordes englond herde wyst alured shold haue theyr kyng put deth thrugh fals traytour godewin wonder wroth swore bytwene god sholde deye wors deth dyde edrith stratto yt betrayed lord edmonde irensyde wolde haue pute hym deth ye theyf traytour fledde then denmark helde hym foure yere lost londe englonde siluester thyrde pope benedictus pthys siluester chose benedictus expulsyd warde expulsyd benedictus put vp ayen put gregorius made pope pand symple lettred man therfore chose man consecrate hym whan many men dyspleased wyth thys godynge two pope thyrde brought whyche sholde occupye place bothe tow stroue amonge themself henry emperour came thenne rome deposyd made clement seconde pope made anone crowne hym sayde romayns sholde neuer chese pope wythout assente soo fyue beynge pope sixte put many men saye gregorius holy man pdamasius seco de clemente xx dayes man vsurper popeheed deyed sodenly anone romayns asked haue pope almayns sholde haue none harde herted myhht enclyne entence emperour whiche sayd sholde pope chosen yf wolde counseyl eleccyon put holy man leo conscyence refused anone chosyn comyn assent leo put cryste fourme laser owne bedde ye morowe founde thynge pof saynt edwarde confessour aluredes brother kynge englonde whan done al baron englonde sente tyme normandy edw rde sholde come englond moche honour edwarde hys chyldehode loued almyghty god hym dradde honeste clennesse hadde lyf hated synne dethe whan crowned anoynted wyth ryall power forgate good maners condycyons fyrste vsed forgate alle good customes maner honour ne ryches ne manere hyghnes euermore yaue hym goodnesse loued god hooly chyrche passynge manere thynge pand poore men also loued theym helde hadde ben hys owne brethern ofte yaue greate almesse full good wyll pof fyrste specyall loue god saynt edwarde lyuynge befell daye went chyrche westmestre hadde herde masse saynt iohan euangelyst moche loued saynt iohn euangelyst specially god hour lady dyde ony saynt came hym pelgryme prayed hym loue god lady saynt iohan euangelyst good hym yeue kynge pryuely toke rynge fynder man perceyued yaue pelgryme receyued wente then pthis kynge edwarde made good lawas englonde yet ben moost vsed holden mercyable ful pyte noo man myght phow erle godewyn came ayen englonde ayen londe afterwarde saynt edwarde weded doughter erle godewin dwellynge denmarke moche herde godnesse kyng edwarde yt full mercy pyte thought yt wolde go ayen englonde seke haue grace good kynge edwarde soo mercy full myght haue ayen hys londe pea arayed hym moche myght put hym warde see came englonde london kynge tyme lordes englonde helde parlyament godewin sente hym yt frendes moost grettest lordes londe prayed beseche kynges graet hym wolde hys pea londe graunte hym lordes ledde hym kyng seke grade anone kynge hym sawe apeled hym treason deth alured brother wordes vnto hym sayde traytour godewin sayd kynge appele yt thou hast betrayed slayn brother alured certes syr sayde godewin sauynge grace pea lordshyp hym neuer betrayed ne yet hym slewe therfore put rewarde ye courte fayr lordes sayd kynge ye yt ben lyeges erles baron londe assembled fulle welle ye herde appele answere also godewin therfore woll ye warde dooth ryght erles barones tho gadred togyder warde themself spake dyuersely amu ge sayd neuer alyaunce homage seriment seruyce ne lordshyp bytwene godewin alured whyche thynge myght hym drawe att laste deuysyd demed sholde put hym ye kynges mercy togyder tho spake ye erle leuerik couentree good god worlde tolde hys reason manere sayd erle godewin best fended man englonde kynge well myght agayne sayd ye wythout counsell godwin alured neuer put dethe wherfore warde towchynge parte hymself hys sone euery v xii erles ben hys frendes goo kynge charged moche golde syluer maye bere betwyxt hondes praynge ye kyng forgyue euyll wyll erle godewin receyue hys homage londe yelde ayen accorded vnto warde came thys maner abouesayd euery holde syluer moche myght bere bytwene hondes kynge sayd fourme maner accorde theyr warde kyng wolde theym agayne saye moche ordeyned graunted confermed ye erle godewin accorded kynge ayen londe afterwarde bare hym well wysely kynge loued hym wonder moche hym fulle preuy within lytell tyme loued moche kynge spowsed godewyns doughter made quene neuerthelesse though kyngge wyf yet lyued euer chastyce cle nesse body without ony flesshely dede doynge wyf quene also halfe ladde holy lyf two yere deyed afterwarde kyng lyued hys lyf without ony wyf pthe kynge yaue erledome oxenforde harolde godewyns sone made hym erle well beloued bothe fader pryue kyng fader sone myghte doo ryght thynge wolde ayenst ryght wolde nothynge doo noo maner man soo good true conscyence therfore oure lorde ihesu cryste greate specyall loue vnto hym shewed phow kyng edwarde sawe swyne kynge denmark drowned see tyme sacrament stode herde masse befelle vppon wytsondaye kynge edwarde herde masse greate chyrche westmestre nyghe att leuacyon ihesu crystis body alle men gadred chyrche came nyght awter see sacrynge kyng hondes lyfe vp hygher grete laughter toke vp wherfore aboute hym stode gretely ganne wonder masse axed kynges laughter fayre lorde sayd kyng edwarde sawe swyne yonger kynge denmarke come see hys power haue come englonde vpon v warre sawe hym hys folke drowned see thys sawe leuacyon crystis body bytwene ye preestes hondes therfore grete ioye myght laughter withholde pand erle leueryk besyde hym stode leuacyon openly sawe ye fourme brede torne lykenesse yonge chylde tooke vp hys ryght honde blessyd kynge erle erle anone torned hym ward ye kyge make hym see ye hooly syght saide ye kynge psyre erle sayde see welle yt ye see tha ked god haue honoured god sauoyour vysybly ihesu cryst fourme man whoos name blessyd worldes phow rynge saynt edwarde gyuen poore pelgryme loue god saynt iohan euangelyst came ayen kynge edwarde thys noble man saynt edwarde regned xiii yere thus befelle vpon tyme deyed two men englonde gone holy londe done theyr pelgrymage goynge ayen theyr owne countree came fro went ye waye mette pylgryme curtely theym saluwed axed londe countree borne sayd englonde tho axed kynge englonde answered sayd good kyng edwarde pfayre frendes sayd tho pelgryme whan yt ye come countres ayen praye yt ye wyll go vnto kynge edwarde oftentymes grete hym myn name oftentymes hym thanke hys grete curteysy hath done namely rynge ye haue whan hadde herde masse westmestre saynt iohans loue euangelyst toke ye pelgremes sayd pray go bere rynge take vnto king edwarde tel hym sende hym full ryche yefte wyll hym yeue vpon x daye shall come unto euermore dwelle blesse without ony ende psyr sayde ye pelgremes ye countree dwellynge pfayr frendes sayd iohn euagelyste dwellynge almyghty god kynge edwarde frende loue hym specyal chause hath euermore lyued clennesse clene mayde praye message fulfyll haue sayd whan ye saynt iohan euangelyst thus charged sodenly voyded theyr syghtes bothe pelgrymes tho thanked almyghty god wene forth theyr waye whan hadde gone two thre myle bega waxe wery sette downe rest felle one slepe whan slepte well one woke lyfe vp hys heed loked sayd felowe aryse vp walke way sayd one felowe vnto certes sayde semeth yt coutree layde v downe rest slepe ierusalem thre myle toke vp theyr hondes blessyd went forth theyr way went theyr waye sawe shep goynge wyth theyr shepe ye spake none langage englysshe pgood frendes sayd one pelgrymes countree lorde therof pand one sheperdes answered sayd ye coutree kent englonde whiche good kyng edwarde lorde pelgrymes anked tho almyghty god saynt iohn euangelyst wente forthe theyr waye came caunterbury fro then vnto london founde kyng tolde hym frome begynnynge vnto ye endynge asmoche saynt iohn charged al thynges hadsped waye tooke rynge kynge edwarde tooke thanked almyghty god saynt iohn euangelyst tho made hym redy euery daye fro daye daye departe thys lyf whan god wolde hym sende phow saynt edward dyed ye twelfth day befell thus crystmasse euen holy man edwarde goodes seruyce matyns hereof hyghe solempne feest became full lyke morowe endured moche payne masse masse lette hym ladde chambre reste hym hys halle amonge hys baron knyghtes myght come theym comforte solace wonte ye worthy feest wherfore theyr myrth comforte amonge halle torned care sorowe cause dradde lese good lorde ye kynge pand vpon saynt iohn daye euangelyste came nexte kynge receyued hys ryghtes hooly chirche yt befaylleth euery cristen man abode mercy wyll god ye two pylgrymes lete hym come yaue theym ryche yeftes betoke theym god also abbot westemestre lette hym come tooke hym rynge honour god saynt mary saynt iohan euangelyst abbot toke put amonge rekyles westmestre euer shall laye kyng syke tyll twelfth eue tho deyed good kynge edwarde att wehmestre lyeth whoos loue god hathe inquyete man many time troubled hooly man gregorius vii fyrst axed foryeuenesse assoyled perceyuered longe brought pope ayenst hym sayd heretyke gregori cursyd hym chesers emperoure duke baxon emperour thys henry batayll ouercame thene came rome pope pursewed pope gregorius cardynalles also pand thene anone robert ye kyng naples droue hym thes delyuered pope cardynalles neuerthelesse yet man grete almesse iii tymes faught batayll ye last deyed wrytchedly put owne sone dyde men done vnto pnichola ye seconde pope benedict two yere nicola called couseyll ayenst yt archedeken turonoseus ye whiche heretyk taught ayenst ye fayth erred ye sacramet couerted holy man coude neuer conuerte dyscyples pnota palexander ye secode pope hym xii yere alexander holy man ordeyned yt vnder payne cursynge yt noo man sholde preest masse men knewe lemman vt p xxxii pcer hoc stryue one codulo expulsyd hym vsurper put hym symonyer phow harolde good wyns sone made kynge escape duke normandy saynt edwarde gone oute worlde passed god worthely enteryd suche grete lorde oughte baron londe wolde haue edwarde elygus sone edwarde outlawe edmonde irensydes sone kynge moche moost kyndest kynges blood reame pbut harolde sone thrugh erle godewyn ye strengthe fader godewyn thrugh grete lordes reame yt kynne vnto hym sybbe seased englode hys honde anone lette crowne hym kynge enterement saynt edware harolde godewynes sone seconde yere afore saynt edwarde deed wolde haue gone flaundres dryuen thrugh tempest coutree pountyse taken brought duke wyllyam harolde wende yt tho thys duke wyllyam wolde haue auenged vpon hym cause yt erle godewyn yt roldes fader lete slee alured saynt edward brother pryncipally cause alured quene emmes sone ye rychardes moder duke normandy aienll duke wyllyam neuertheles whan duke wyllyam harolde pryson vnder hys power asmoche harolde noble wyse knyght worthy body hys fader accorded good kynge edwarde therfore wolde mysdo hym manere thynges betwext spoken ordeyned harolde hys good wyll swore vpon boke vpon oly sayntes sholde spouse wedde duke wyllyams doughter deth saynt edwarde sholde besely doo deuour kepe saue reame englonde vnto profyte auantage duke wyllyam pand whan harolde hadde thus made othe vnto duke wyllyam lette hym goo yaue hym many ryche yeftes tho wente then came englonde anone dyde manere whan saynte edwarde deed man falsly sworne lette crowne hym kynge englonde falsely brake coue name yt hadde made wyth duke wyllyam wherfore wonder wroth wyth hym swore wolde vppon hym auenged euer hym befell pand anone duke wyllyam lette assemble grete hoste came englonde aueng hym vppon harolde conquere londe yf myght pand yere harolde crowned haralde herestynge kynge denmarke arryued scotlo de thought haue kynge englonde came englonde robbed destroyed myght tyll came yorke slewe many men armes thousande hondred preestes wha tydynges came kynge assembled grete power wente fyght haralde denmarke wyth hys owne hondes de hym slewe dane dyscomfyted tho lefte lyue wyth moche sorowe fledde theyr shyppes thus kynge harolde englonde slewe kynge haralde denmarke panno dm mlxvi phow wyllyam bastarde duke normandy came englonde slewe kyng harolde phere come norman expulsyd harolde saxon annd wha bataylle done harolde came proude wolde thynge parte people thynge goten helde hym self wherfore moost parte people wrothe frome hym departed soo oonly hym abode moo soldyurs vpon daye sate atte meete messager came hym sayde wyllyam bastarde duke normandy arryued englonde greate hoste take londe hastynge also myned castell wha kynge herde tydynges wente thyther lytell power hast myght fewe people wyth hym lefte whan come thyder ordeyned yeue batayll duke wyllyam duke axed thre thynges yf wolde haue doughter wyf made swore othe behyght wolde holde londe hym truage wolde determyne thys thynge batayll harolde proude man stronge trusted wonder moche vpon strength faught duke wyllyam people harolde men batayll dysco fyted hymselfe slayne thys batayll ended tombryge seconde yere regne vpon sanyt calixt daye buryed waltham pof kynge william bastarde gouerned hym well wysely grete warre bytwene hym kynge fraunce willi bastarde duke norma dy conquered londe vpon crystmasse daye nexte lete crowne hym kynge westmestre worthy kyng yaue vnto englyshmen largely londes hys knyghtes warde wene hym ouer see came normandy dwelled whyle seconde yere regne came ayen englonde brought hym maude wyf lette crowne quene englonde oon wytsondaye pand tho anone kynge scotlonde thoe called malcolin began stryue warre kyng wylyam ordeined hym towarde scotlonde men lo de see destroye kynge malcolin accorded kynge scotlonde became hys man helde hys londe hym kynge wyllyam receyued hym homage came ayen englonde kynge wyllyam brent thys norma company spared nother chirches ne house relygyon brente obbed bare way l myght take londe destroyed one syde pthe baron lordes englonge ordeyned amonge theym beste spekers wysest men sente ouer see kynge phylyp frauce prayed hym wolde sende lowys hys sone englonde kynge englonde receyue crowne phow lowys knges sone fraunce came englonde stronge power people kynge englonde anone kynge phylyp fraunce herde tydynges made certayne alyaunce bytwene theym theyr comune eleccyon lowys kynge phylyps sone fraunce sholde go theym englonde dryue kynge iohan londe presence lowes made
