alle castels englonde alyens hondes pand tho came lowwys besyeged rochestre castell tooke yt wyth strength thursdaye wytson weke lete hange alyens therin ye thursdaye nexte se wynge came london receyued moche honur lordes abode hym hym made homage pand warde tewysdaye nexte trynyte sondaye toke castel reigate morowe castell gilforde frydaye nexte castell farneham mondaye nexte cyte wynchestre hym yolde morowe saynt iohans daye maner wu ueseye hym yelden tewysdaye vtas saynt peter poule toke castell odyham mondaye saynt margaretes day ordeyned hym warde bawmore syege castell dwelled xv dayes myghte gete castell thenne wente then came london toure hym yolden ye pope sete englonde legate yt called swalo ye deth kynge iohan tyme pope sente englond legate called swalo preest cardynall rome mayntene kynge iohans cause ayenst baron englond baron huge parte helpe thorugh lowys kynges sone frauce kyng iohn wyst orne ne go befell wolde haue gone nycholl went thyder warde came abbaye swynes hede abode two dayes sate mete axed monke ye hous moche loof wroth sette hym vpo table monke sayd hat loof wroth half peny sayd kynge tho greate chepe brede sayde tho may leue ony whyle suche loof shall wrothe xx shelynges half yere gone whan sayd worde moche thought often syghed toke ete brede sayd god ye worde haue spoken shall sothe pthe moke stode kyng worde full sory hys herte thought rather wolde hym self suffre deth thought yf myght ordeyne therfore maner remedy anone monke wente vnto hys abbot shryuen hym tolde abbot kynge sayd prayed hys abbot assoyle hym wolde yeue kynge suche drynke englond sholde glad therof ioyfull tho yede monke gardeine foude grete tode therin toke vp put cuppe prycked tode thorugh broche many tymes tyll venym came euery syde cuppe tho tooke cuppe fyllyed good ale brought kyng knelynge sayenge syr sayd wassayll euer dayes lyf dronke ye good cuppe pbegyne monke sayd kynge pand monke dranke greate draught toke kynge cuppe ye kynge dranke also greate draught sette downe cuppe monke anon ryght wente farmere deyed anone whoos soule god haue mercy amen fyue monkes synge soule specyally shall whyle abbaye standeth kynge rose vp anone full euyll ease commauded remeue table axed monke men tolde hym deed wombe broken sondre pwhan ye kyng herde comaunded trusse nought bely began swelle drynke yt droke within two dayes deyed ye fyue por e wyth viii shyppes tho mette ye hyghe see assaylled egerly ouer came strength smote eustace monkes heed toke also x grete lordes fraunce put theym pryson slewe almoost men came theym anone northumberlonde surrey also yt sholde go take theyr vyage vpon ye traytours lewelyn dauyd wonder herde warre tho wynter walys whan coutres somer lewelyn lete ordeyne well arayed vytayll hys good castell swandon ther huge nombre people plente vytaylles kynge edwarde wyst wher entre whan kynges men perceyuer also strenth walys lete come see bargee botes grete plankys many myght ordeyne haue go sayd castell swandon wyth men foot also hors walsshmen moche people stronge draue englysshmen ayen yt ther moche presse people ye tornynge ayen ye charge burden men made ye bargee botes synke drowned many good kynght yt say syr robert clyfford syr wyllyam lyndeseye yt syre iohns sone fitz robert syr rychard tanny huge nombre thrugh owne foly yf good espyes harmyd whan kynge edwarde herde tell hys people drowned made sorowe ynough tho came syr iohan vessy frome kynge aragon brought wyth hym moche people bachelers gascoynes souldyurs dwelled sayde iohn vessy receyued hym wage hym witholde noble men fyght brente many townes slewe moche people walsshmen myght take tho wyth strenth myght made assawte vnto castell swandon gate castell whan dauyd prence brother herde tydynges ordeyned hym flyght lewelyn prynce sawe broder fledde sore abasshed power warre mayntene soo lewelyn gan flee wynde well haue scapedde morowe syre roger mortymer mette wyth hym oonly wyth x knyghtes sette hym rounde aboute hym went smote hys heed presented ye heed vnto kynge edwarde thys manere lewelyn prynce walys taken hys heed smyten also alle hys heyres dysheryted euermore thrugh ryght full dome lordes reame phow dauyd lewelyns broder prynce walys put dethe dauid prynces broder walys thrugh pryde wende haue prynce walys brother dethe vpon sent walsshemen hys parleament dynbygh folysshely made walys aryse ayenst kynge began meue warre ayenst kynge edwarde dyde sorowe dysease myghte hys power whan kynge edwarde herde thys thynge ordeyned men pursewe vppon hym dauyd fyersly hym defended tyll ye came towned saynt morice dauyd take fledde ladde kynge kynge comaunded sholde hangyd drawen smyte hys heed quarter hym sende hede london foure quarter sende foure chyef townes walys sholde take ensample therof beware afterwarde kynge edwarde lete crye pea thrugh walles seased londe honde grete lordes left alyue came feaute homage kynge edwarde theyr kynde lorde tho lete kyng edwarde amende lawes walys defectyue sent ye lordes walys letter patentes sholde come parlament whan come yu kyng sayd full curteysly lordynges ye welcome behoueth counseyll helpe go vnto gascoyne amende trespasse yt done whan entreate pea bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey ye kynges lyege men erles baron cosented grau ted therto tho made hym kynge edwarde redy went gascoyne lete amende trespass yt hym done gascoyne debate yt bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey sessyd made theym accorded whyle good kyng edwarde elynore wyf gascoyne good erle cornewayll made wardeyn englonde tyll kynge edwarde came ayen tho enquered hys traytours yt coniected falsenesse agaynst hym eche receyued ther dome deserue meane tyme good kynge edwarde beyonde see doo make amendes ayenst hym trespassyd ther false yf traytoure called rysap merydok began make werre ayenst kyng edwarde yt cause syr payne typtot wrongfully greued dysceased forsayde rysap meradok whan kyng edwarde herde matere well vnderstode anone sente hys letter pryue seale forsayd rebellyo rysap merydok sholde begynne maner wyse make reyse werre yt sholde pea loue whan came ayen englonde wolde vnder take quarell amende al yt mysdon forsayd rysap merydok dyspysed kynges commaundement spared doo sorowe myght kynges men englond anon take ladde yorke drawen hangyd felonye pof dressyng kynge edwarde made iustic clerkes done ther falsnes draue iewes englonde ther vsury mysbyleue kynge edwarde dwelled thre yere gascoyne desyre came goo englonde ayen whan come ayen foude many playntes made hym iustyces clerkes done many wronges falsnesse yt wonder whiche falsnesse syre thomas waylond ye kynges iustyce swore englonde toure london falsnesse put vpon hym wherfore atteynt proued fals anone whan kyng done wyll iustices tho lete enquere espye iewes dysceyued begyled people thorugh synne falsnesse vsury lete ordeyne preuy parlement amonge lordes ordeyned amonge theym iewes sholde voyde englonde theyr mysbyleue also theyr fals vsury dyde vnto crysten men spedde make ende thynge comyn alte englonde yaue vnto kynge xv peny theyr goodes meuable soo iewes dryuen oute englonde tho went iewes fraunce dwellyd thorugh leue kynge phylyp tho kynge fraunce phow kynge edwarde seased alle londe scotlonde cosente graunte lordes scotlonde longe alexandre kynge scotlonde dede dauyd erle huntyngdon kynges brother scotlonde axed claymed kyngdom scotlond brother deed cause yt ryghtfull heyre many grete lordes sayd nay wherfore greate debate arose bytwene theym fredes asmoche wolde consente hys coronacyon meane tyme forsayd dauyd deyed befell ye sayd dauyd thre doughters yt worthyly maryed fyrst doughter maryed bayloll seconde brus thyrde hastynges forsayd bayloll brus chalenged ye londe scotlonde greate debate stryf arose bytwene cause eche wolde haue kynge whan lordes scotlonde saw debate bytwene came kynge edwarde englonde seased hym londe scotlond chyef lord wha kyng seased ye forsayd lordes ye forsayd baylol brus hastinges came kynges courte axyd kyng whyche shold kynge scotlonde kyng edwarde ye full gentyll true lete enquyre cronycles scotlonde gretest lordes scotlonde whiche eldest blood foude baylol eldest ye kyng scotlond sholde holde kynge englonde hym frauce homage done baylol went scotlode crowyed kynge scotlonde pand ye tyme vpon see grete warre bytwene englysshemen norman vpo tyme norman arryued douer ther martred holy called thomas douer afterwarde norma slayne escaped one pand afterwarde kynge edwarde sholde lete duchye gascoyne thrugh kynge phylyp frauce thrugh fals castynge dousepers londe wherfore syr edmond kynge edwardes brother yaue vp domage vnto kynge frauce pand tyme clerkes englond graunted kynge edwarde half eale holy chirche goodes helpynge recouer londe agayne gascoyne kyng sent thether noble company hys bachelers hymself wolde haue gone portelmouth let thrughe one maddok walys yt seased castell swandon honde cause kynge torned walys cristmasse cause noble lord englond yt sent gascoyne comforth lorde kynge take syr charlys frauce yt say syr iohn brytayne syr robert tiptot syr raufe tanny syr hugh bardolfe syr adam cretynge yet att assensyon maddok take walys nother called morgan sent tour london byheded phow syre iohan baylol kyng scotlonde sayde homage whan syre iohn baylol kynge scotlonde vnderstande ye kynge edwarde werred gascoyne ye reame scotlond delyuerd falsly tho ayenst othe sayd homage thrugh procurynge folke sent vnto ye court rome thrugh fals suggestyon assoylled othe yt swore vnto kyng englonde soo letter enbulled ptho chose scotlonde dousepers brnyge edward ryght pand ye tyme came two cardynalles ye cource rome fro pope celestme trete acorde bytwene ye kyng englod tho cardinalles spake accorde tha turbeluyll take lyon made homage warde parys put sone hostage thought go englonde aspye countre tell whan came englond broken kynges pryson fraunce ryght said wolde yt englysshmen walshemen sholde aboute kynge brynge ende swore vpon thys couenaunt dedes made bytwene sholde haue yere thousand poudes worth londe byrnge thynge ende fals traytour toke leue wente then came englonde vnto kynge seyd broke oute pryson yt put hym suche peryll loue wherfore kyng cowde hym moche thanke full gladde comynge pand fals traytoure fro daye aspyed doynge kynge also counselle kyng loued hym full welle hym full preuy clerke englonde kynges hows fraunce herde treason falsnesse wrote another clerke tho dwellynge edwarde kynge englonde thomas turbeluyll hadde done fals c niectynge counselle englonde wryte haue sende vnto kynge fraunce pand thoruhhe forsayde letter clerke hadde sente fro fraunce founde vppon wherfore ledde london hangyd drawe treason hys two sone hadde put fraunce hostage thenne beheeded pof conquest berwyke whan twoo cardynalles gone agayne fraunce trete pea cambroy kynge sent thether erles baron saye syr edmonde broder erle lancastre lecetre syr henry lacy erle nychol wyllyam vessy baron baronettes aboute xiii best wysest englonde pand tyme kynge edwarde toke vyage scotlonde werre vpon iohn baylol kynge scotlonde pand syr robert roos berwyk sledde fro ye englysshmen wente scottes kyng edwarde wente hym towarde berwyk besegyd towne tho within manly defended sette fyre brente two kynge edwardes shyppes sayde dyspyte reprey hym wenyth kynge edwarde longe shankys haue gete berewyk vnthankes gas pykes hym whan doon gas dyke hym whan kyng edwarde thys scorne anone thorugh hys myghtenesse passed ouer dyches assaylled towne came yates gate conquered towne thrughe hys gracyous power slewe xxv thousande vii hondred scottes kynge edwarde loste man renoune saufe syr rycharde cornewayle hym kylled flemynge redde halle quarell forsayd rycharde dyde hys helme comaunded theym yelde put kynges grace ye scottes wolde wherfore halle brent cast downe tho therin brente kynge edwarde loste noo moo men vyage symple estate xxvii englysshemen wardeyn castell yaue vp keyes ye castell wythout ony assawte taken syre wyllyam douglas symonde frysell erle patryk yelded pea ingham humbresmylle robert brus kynge edwarde forsoke kynge edwarde helde scottes afterward taken put pryson tho lete kynhe edwarde close berwyk wyth walles dyches robert rous went tyndale sette wuyerbrydge fyre exham lamerstok slewe robbyd folke countree wente fro then dunbarre fyrste wenesdaye marche kynge sent erle garenne syr hugh percy syre hugh spenser wyth fayre company besege castell one called syre rycharde sywarde traytoure fals man ymagyned begyle englysshme sente englysshmen theym deseeyue sayd wolde yelde theym ye castell yf wolde graunt viii dayes respyce myhht sende telle syr iohan bayloll kynge scotlonde men fared within castell pand hym worde yf wolde remeue sege englysse men wolde yelde castell vnto englysshe men pthe messenger tho came syr iohan baylol tho kynge scotlode wyth hooste messenger tolde hym caas syr iohan toke hoste came morowe erly towarde castell syr rycharde sywarde sawe hym come yt mayster counseyll keper castell sayd vnto englyssgmen sayde see fayre company well apparelled wyll goo ayenste theym wyth mete theym assaylle syr hughe spenser sawe falsnesse hym ye treson sayd hym traytour take proue falsnesse shalle auaylle hughe spenser commaunded anone bynde hym hast wente ayenst ther enmyes slewe scottes xxii thousand scottes tyme man wyth honour saufe patryke graham manly foughte longe laste slayne tho sayde englysshmen repreyf scottes thyse scaterande scottes holde sottes wrench vn ware erly mornynge euyll tymynge wente ye fro dubare pa tho ware within castell sawe scomfyture yelded vp castell vnto englysshmen bounde theyr bodyes godes castels kynge edwarde soo take castell thre erles vii baron xxxviii knyghtes xi clerkes vii pycardys presentyd kynge edwarde sente towre london kepte phow kynge edwarde greate grace delyuered ayen scottes oute pryson cheyftayns londe drewe frensshemen thrugh counseyll wyllyam waleys kynge edwarde made tho ende ye werre taken chey eyns scotlonde tho came syr iohan baylol yelded hym vnto kynge edwarde put hym grace ledde london whan kyng edwarde come thether brough hym kynge axed howe wolde make amendes trespaas losse doon hym put theym mercy lordynges sayde kynge wyll londes ne goodes wyll ye make othe vpo goddys body true neuer tyme ayenst bere army consentyd kynges wyl swore vpon goddys body saye syr iohn comyn erle scra hron erle carryk also foure bysshops vndertoke clergye kynge delyuered yaue sauf conduyce go ther owne londe longe afterwarde ne aryse ayenst kynge edwarde cause wyst well kynge edwardes folke take gascoyne sayd syr iohn bayloll kynge scotlonde wyste well londe sholde haue sorowe shame theyr falsnesse hast wete hym ouer see owne londes helde hym came neuer ayen wherfore scottes chose vnto theyr kynge wyllyam waleys rybaude harlot comen vp nought moche harme dyde englysshmen kyng edwarde thoughte myght haue delyueraunce peple take gascoyne hast wente hym ouer see flaunders werre vpon kyng frauce erle flaunders receyued hym wyth moche honour grayntyd hym londys hys owne wyll whan kynge fraunce herde telle kyng englonde aryued flaundres came wyth greate power hym dystroye prayed hym trewes two yere englysshe marchauntes also frenche myght saufly go come bothe sydes kynge edwarde grauted muste haue men pryson gascoyne kynge fraunce anone graunted delyuerd pand ye tyme scottes sente ye bysshop saynt andrewes frauce kynge syr charles brother ye syr charles sholde come wyth hys power scotlode wolde come theyr power sholde go englonde loude dystroye scotlonde vnto came ente scottes trustyd moche vpon fresshmen ye thyng maner graut neuertheles ye scottes beg robbe kylle northuberlond dyd moche harme phow wyllyam waleys lete reyse ye londe scotlonde cheyf lorde syr hugh cressynham batayll fonkyrke tydynges come kynge edwarde wyllyam walys ordeyned suche stronge power also alle scotlonde hym attendaunt redy slee englysshmen dystroye londe sore anoyed sente anone letter therle garrenne syr henry percy wyllyam latomer syr hughe cressynham tresoroer sholde take power go northumberlonde soo forth scotlode kepe countres whan wyllyam waleys herde theyr co mynge began flee englysshmen hym folowed dr ue hym tyll cam stryuelyn helde hym castell walsshmen euery daye escryed menacyed dyde dyspyte myghte soo englysshmen vpon tyme mornynge went fro castell moutenaunce x myles passed ouer brydge william waleys came strog power droue abak englysshmen ayenst hym noo power tho fledde myght take brydge scaped syr hughe kyngs tresorer slayne many also wherfore made moche sorowe ptho kynge edwarde sped hys mater flaudres come ayen englonde haste toke waye scotlonde came theder ascencyon tyde founde sette fyre brente poore people scotlonde came hym wonder thyck prayed hym goddys loue wold haue mercy pyte tho kynge comaunded yt man sholde doo harme yt yolden hym ne man ordre ne hous relygyon ne manere chyrche lete espye myght yt myght fynde ony enmyes tho came spye vnto kynge tolde ye scottes assembled abyde bataylle saynt mary mawdelyns daye ye kynge came fonkyrk yaue bataylle scottes bataylle slayne xxx thousande scottes englysshemen xviii mo whyche worthy knyght slayne yt knyghte hospytelere callyd frery bryan iay whan wyllyam waleys fledde batayll frery bryan hym pursewed fyersly hors ranne stert mire mary vp bely wyllyam waleys estreuelyn welle vytaylled stored vii yere phow castell estrefelyn seged wonne kynge edward came ye castell estreuelyn huge power beseged castell lytell auaylled myhht doo scoctes harme castell soo parlement shode stonde ordynance phow troylebaston fyrste ordened kynge edwarde went then london wende haue rest pea hys warre whiche werre occupyed xx yere saye gascoyne walys scotlonde thought myght recouer hys tresour yt spended aboute hys werre lette enquere thrugh reame alle tyme oute hys reame men called troylebaston ordeyned therto iustyces thys manere recouered tresoure without nombre hys purpose haue goon hooly londe haue werred vpon goddes enmyes cause crossyd loge tye neuertheles ye law ordeyned dyd moche good thrugh englonde mysbode tho ye trespassed well chastysed meke better ye pore comyns reste pea tyme kynge edwarde prysoned owne sone edwarde cause walter lanton bysshop chestre kynges tresorer complayned hym sayd forsayd edwarde thrughe cousell entysynge one ganasto asquyre gascoyne broke park forsayd bysshop thys peer counselyd ladde edwarde cause kynge e yled sone englonde pof dethe wyllyam waleys fals traytoure whan thys kynge edwarde hys enemyes ouercome walys gascoyne scotlonde dystroyed hys traytours rybaude wyllyam le neuer kynge wolde hym yelde towne saynt dominyk yere kynge edwarde regne xxxiii ye fals traytour take presentyd kynge kyng wolde see hym sent hym london receyue iugement vpon saynt barthylmewes eue hangyd drawe hede smyte bowelles take body brente hys body quartered sent vnto four best townes scotlonde hys heed put vpon spere lete hym whan herde masse toke soope dranke warde bestrode hys palfroy rode dumfris whan roberte brus sawe hym come wyndow chambre made ioye ynoygh came ayenst hym collyd hym ye necke made hym gode semblaut whan erles baron scotlonde present robert ye brus sayd syrs ye wote well ye cause comynge wherfore yf ye wyl graut ibe kyng scotlonde ryght heyre ye londe lordes sayd one voys h sholde crownede kynge scotlond yt wolde hym helpe mayntene ayenst maner men lyue hym yf nede deye gityll knyght tho iohn comyn answerd certes neuer forme ne haue asmoche helpe value baton oth haue made vnto kynge edwarde englonde shall holde whyle lyfe woll laste worde wente copany wolde lyght vpon palfroy roberte brus pursewed hym drawenswerde bare hym thrugh body syr iohn comyn felle downe vnto erth robert comyn slayne hewen peces robert brus torned ayen yt syr iohn comyn ye noble baro lay wounded pyned warde deth besyde hygh awter chyrche graey freres sayde vnto syr iohan comyn traytoure thou shalt dede neuer lete myn auauncement shoke swerde hygh awter smote hym hede ye brayne felle downe vpon groude blood storte hygh vpon walles yet vnto thys daye blood seen water maye wasshe waye deyed fore syknes batayll take ye bysshop baston bysshop saynt andrewes abbot scone armyd yren men armes fals traytours fals prelate ayenst theyr othe brought kynge kynge sente vnto pope rome shold theym wyll phow iohan therle alethes taken put dethe bataylle fledde syre iohan erle alethes wente chyrche hydde hym drede myghte haue noo refute cause chyrche enterdyted thrugh generall sentence chyrche taken syr iohan went well haue scaped fro ye deth cause yt claymed kynred kynge edwarde kynge wolde lenger bytrayed traytours sent hym london hast hangyd hys head smyten body brent asshes prayer quene margerete cause claymed kynge edward kynred drawynge yeuen hym phow iohan wyllyam waleys brother put dethe grettest mayster scotlonde thus doon euyll deth destroyed theyr falsnesse iohan wyllyam waleys brother take doon vnto dethe syr iohan erle alethes phow robert brus fledde scotlonde norway ye tyme robert ye brus moche hated amonge peple scotlonde yt wyste best hyde hym wente norway kynge spowsyd syster helde hym socour haue robert brus myght foude scotlonde sokynge edward tho lete crye hys pea thrught londe lawas vsyd hys mynystrys serued thrugh londe phow kynge edwarde deyed kynge edwarde abatyd hys enemy turned south warde sykened atte burgh vpon sande marche scotlonde callyd hym henry lacy erle nichell syr guy erle warwyk syr aylmer erle penbroke syr robert clyfforde baron prayed theim vpon fayth hym oughte sholde make edwarde carnaruan kynge englonde assone myght shold suffre peer ganaston come agayne englonde make hys sone ryot graunted hym good wyll kynge toke hys sacramente hooly chyrche good crysten man sholde deyed repentaunce whan hadde ben kynge xxxv yere deyed buryed westmestre moche solempnyte vpon whose soule god haue mercy pof merlyns prophecyes declared kynge edwarde kynge henry sone kyng edward prophecyce merlyn called hym dragon seconde vi kynges sholde regne englonde sayd sholde medled mercy also strenthe fyernesse sholde kepe englonde frome colde hete sholde opene hys mouthe towarde walys sholde sette foot wyk sholde close walwes sholde doo moche harme sede sayde sothe good kynge edwarde medled mercye fyernesse mercy ayenst enmyes walys scotlonde fyernesse whan put dethe ther falsnesse traytourily hadde deserued welle keped englond frome colde heet sythe kepte frome alle manere enmyes ranne vppon hym doo hym ony wronge pand welle opened mouthe warde walys made quake thrughe hydour hys mouthe whan conqueryd thruoghe dynte swerde prynce lewelyn dauyd hys brother ri morgan put dethe thrughe theyr falsnesse theyr foly sette hys foot wyk conquered berwyk whiche conquest slayne xxv thousande vii hondred take suche brente redde halle pand walles yt lete make shall noyous vnto sede men shall inthe lyf syre edwarde carnaruan hys sone yet sayd merlyn sholde make ryuers ren blood wyth brayne ye semyd well hys warres ye maystry yet merlyn sayd yt ther sholde come people ye nortwest durynge regne forsayd dragon yt shold ladde yll greyhoude yt shold dragon crowne kynge afterward sholde fle ouer ye see drede dragon without comynge ayen proued syr iohn baylol ye kynge edwarde made kynge scotlonde ye falsly aroyse ayenst hym fled owne londes frauce neuer came ayen scotlond drede kyng edward yet sayd merly peple yt shold lede ye sayd greyhoud sholde faderles vnto certayne tyme soth sayd peple scotlonde gretly dysesyd syr iohan baylol fled merlyn sayd sone shold become hys tyme redde ony blood tokenynge grete mortalyte people knowe wel wha scottes slayne syth sayd merlyn ye dragon shold nouryshe fox sholde meue grete werre ayenst hym yt sholde hys tyme ended semed well robert brus kynge edwarde nourysshed hys chambre sythen stale way meued grett werre ayenst hym whiche werre ended tyme yet sayd merlyn dragon sholde deye ye marche londe hys londe sholde long without good keper men shold dethe yle shephey vnto yle mercyll wherfore ala shall ther songe amonge comyn people faderles londe wastyd prophecie anone good kynge edwarde deed syr edwarde hys sone kyng englonde sent pers ganaston gascoyne moche louyd hym yt callyd hym brother anone yaue vnto hym lordshyp walyngforde longe yt yaue hym therldom cornewaylle ayenst lordes wyll englonde pand tho brought syr walter langton bysshop chestre pryson durauce toure london wyth two knaues alonely hym serue kynge wrothe wyth hym fore cause syre water made complaynt hym hys fader wherfore put pryson tyme troylebaston sayde pers ganaston made grete maystreys wente kynges tresory ye abbay westmestre toke table golde ye trestls ye many ryche iewels yt somtyme noble good kyng arthur toke marchaut called ameri friscobande sholde bere ouer ye see gascoyne went then came neuer ayen wherfore grete losse londe whan pers rychely auausyd became proude stowte wherfore ye grete lordes reame hym idyspyte grete berynge wherfore syr henry lacy erle nicholl syr guy erle warwyk ye whyche grete lordes good kynge edwarde syr edwardes fader kyng englonde chargyd pers ganaston sholde come englonde brynge sone edwarde ryot lordes englonde assembled certayn day att frere prechers london spake dyshonour ye kynge edwarde dyde hys reame crowne assentyd alle bothe erles baron comyns sayd peer ganaston sholde exyled englonde euer done swore englonde went irlonde kyng made hym cheyfteyne gouernour londe hys commyscyon pers cheyfteyne londe dyd hym lykyd hadde power wolde tyme wer templers exyled thrugh cristiantee cause myn put vppon theym sholde thynges ayenst fayth good byleue kyng edwarde louyd peer ganaston moche myght bere copany moche kynge yaue behyght people englonde exylyge forsayd peer shold reuokyd atte stamforde thrugh yt hym exyled wherfore pers ganaston cam ayen englond whan come ayen londe dyspysed ye grettest lordes londe called syr robert clare erle gloucetre horesone erle nycholl syr henry lacy brustenbely syr guy erle warwyk blacke hound arderne also callyd ye noble erle thomas lancastre churle many scornes shamys sayde many grete lordes inglonde wherfore warde hym full angry wroth ryght sore anoyed tyme deyed erle nycholl chargyed yt deed thomas lancastre erle sone lawe sholde mayntene hys quarell ayenst peer ganaston vpon blessynge pand befell thorugh helpe erle thomas lancastre erle warwyk forsayd syr peer heeded att gauersich besyde warwyk xx day iune yere grace mccc xii wherfore kyng sore anoyed prayed god myght se daye auenged vpon deth forsayde peer pand befell afterwarde ye shall ala ye tyme forsayd erle lancastre many grete baron put pyteous dethe martred cause forsayde quarell kynge att london yere regne yere oure lorde mccc xiiii ala sorowe losse ther done slayne noble erle gylbert clare syr robert clefford baron kynge edwarde scomfyted edmonde maule ye kynges stewarde drede wente drowned hymself fresshe ryuer called bannokysborne wherfore sayd repreyf kynge edwarde asmoche louyd go water also dyscomfyted banosborne therfore ye maydens made songe therof ye countree kynge edwarde manere soge maydes englonde sore may ye morne tyyt haue lost lemans banokysborne heuelogh wenyth kyng englonde haue gote scotlond rombylogh kynge edmonde dyscomfyted woder sore faste fledde folke left aliue wet vnto berwyk helde hym toke hostage ii chyldern rychesse towne kynge went london toke couseyl thynges nedefull ye reame englode pand ye tyme befel tho englonde rybaude called iohan taner yede sayd sondaye yere lorde mcccxvi berwyke loste thorugh false treson oon pers spaldynge whyche pers kynge put helpe towne many burgeyses towne wherfore chyldren put hostage thrughe burgeyses berwyk folowed tymes masse shold songe holy chyrche thrugh soctlonde yf scottes wolde make restitucyon harmes hadde made vnto holy chyrche wherfore many good prest holy men therfore slayne thrugh ye reame scotlonde bycause wolde synge masse ayenst ye popys comaundemet ayenst wyll fulfyll tyrauntes wyll phow syre hughe spenser sone made kynges chamberlayne bataylle mitone longe warde kynge ordeyned parlemente atte yorke syr spenser sone made chambrelayne meane tyme whyle werre lasted kynge wente ayen scotlonde wonder wytte beseged towne berwyk scottes wente ouer water sole wath thre myle frome kynges hoste pryuely stole way nyght came englo de robbyd dystroyed myght sparde manere thynge tyll came vnto yorke whan englysshmen left home herde thyse tydiges tho myghte traueyll well monk prestes freres chanons seculers came mette wyth scotes myton vp swale xii day octobre ala sorowe englysshe husbonde men coude thynge yt werre kyllyd drowned arme see cheyftyenes syre wyllyam melton arche bysshop yorke abbot selby wyth stedes fledde came yorke theyr owne foly myschaunce passed water swale scottes sette fyre sta kes hey smote ther huge ye englysshmen myght se ye scottes wha englisshmen gone ouer water tho came ye scottes wyth theyr wynge maner shelde came warde englyssme araye englysshemen fledde neth hadde ony men army kynge hadde almoost lost syege berwyk scottes hobylers went bytwene brydge englysshmen whan grete host mett englysshemen fled bytwene hobylers gret hoste englysshmen almoost slayne myght go ouer water saued many drowned ala slayne many men relygyon seculers preestes clerkes moche sorowe tharchebysshop escaped therfore scottes callyd batayll whyte batayll phow kynge edwarde dyde alle manere thynge syr hugh spenser wolde kynge edwarde herde tydynges remeued sege berwyk came agayn englond syr hugh spenser kynges chamberlayne kept kynges chambre myghte speke kynge made hym fret alle nede ouer mesure hugh bare hym stowte men hym scorne dyspyte kynge hymself wolde gouerned ne rulyd manere man fader hym yf ony knyghte englonde hadde wodes maneyrs londes wolde coueyte anone kyng must yeue elles man ought sholde falsly endyted forfeyt felony thrugh suche doynge dysheryted many bachelere moche londe gate grete wonder whan lordes enlonde sawe grete couetyse falsnesse syr hugh spenser fader syr hugh sone come gentyll erle lancastre axyd hym counseyll dysese reame though syr hugh spenser sone hast one assente made pryue asseble shirburne elmede made othe breke dystouble ye doinge bytwene kynge syr hugh spenser sone vpon theyr power went marche walys dystroyed londe forsayd syr hughes phow syr hugh spenser fader exyled englonde whan kyng edwarde sawe ye grete harme dystruccyo tho baros englonde dyde vnto syre hugh spenser londe sone euery place came vpon kynge tho thrugh hys counseyl yll exyled syr monbraye syr roger clyfforde syr gosselyn dauyll many lordes yt theym consente wherfore baron dyde tho harme dyde wha kynge sawe ye baron wolde sesse theyr cruelte kyng sore adradde lest wolde dystroy hym reame mayntenauce yf assented sente hys letter sholde come london hys parlement certaine daye letter conteyned came thre bataylles well armyd al poyntes euery batayl cotarmours grete clothe therof ryght quarter yelowe wyth whyte bendes wherfore ye parlemente callyd parlement whyte bende ye company syr hunfrey de bohoune erle tidynges syr roger mortymer many lordes toke towne brugge wroth wyth strenth wherfore kyng wonder wrothe lete outlawe thomas lancastre vmfroy de bohoune erle herforde alle tho assentynge quarel kyng assebled huge host came ayenst lordes englond wherfore mortymers put kynges grace anone sente toure london kept pryson wha baron herd thys thyng came poutfert ye erle thomas soiourned tolde hym mortymers yelde kynge put hys grace pof syege tykhyll whan thomas erle lancastre herde thys wonder wrothe company greatly dyscomfyted ordeyned power togyder besyeged castell tykhyll tho wyth manly defended barnos myght gete castel whan kyng herde yt castell beseged swore god name lege sholde remeued assembled huge power people wente theder ward rescowe castell power encresyd fro daye daye whan syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke iohan erle araundell theyr power wente ouer water dyscomfyted therle thomas company fled castell tetbury then went pountfret yage deyed syr roger daumore thabbay thebury tyme erle thomas traytour wyth hyme yt callyd robert holonde knyght erle brought vp nought nourysshed hym hys butrye yeue hym thousade marke londe yere moche erle louyd hym myght erles court hym lyked bothe amonge hyghe lowe craftly theyf bare hym ayenste lorde trustyd vpon hym ony man lyue erle ordeyned letter goo erledome lancastre make men aryse kepe hym vyage saye v hu dred men army fals traytour came manere men warne ne make arayse helpe lord whan fals traytour herde tell yt hys lord dycomfyted burton vpon trent fals traytour theyf stele way robbyd rauesdele lordes men came fro scomfyture toke hors harneys al slewe myghte take came yeldyd hym kynge pwhan good erle thomas wyste bytrayed abasshed sayde hymself almyghty good myght robert holonde fynde hys herteme betray sythe louyd hym moche god well maye nowe man se hym yt man maye dysceyue nother rathar yt trustyth moost vpon hath full euyll yelded goodnes worshyp yt haue hym done thrugh kyndnesse haue hym auaucyd made hym hyghe yt lowe makyth go hyghe vnto lowe yet shall deye euyll dethe pof scomfyture brurbrygge good erle thomas lancaste humfroy de bohoune ele herford baron yt theym toke counsell bytwene ye frre prechers poutfret tho thought thomas vpon traytour roberte holonde sayde repreyf ala robert holonde hath betrayed red euyll shred comyn assent sholde goo castell dunstanbrughe whiche perteyned therldome lancastre yt sholde abyde ther tyll kynge yeue male talente pbut whan good erle thomas herde answered manere sayd lordes sayd yf go wade north northen men woll saye go warde ye scottes shall holden traytours cause dystauce bytwene kynge edwarde robert ye brus made hym kynge scotlonde therfore say touchyng self wyll go ferder northe myn owne castell poutfret pand whan syre roger clyfford herde arose vp anone wrathe drawe swerde hye swore god almyghty holy name yf yt wolde go sholde hym slee noble gentyll erle thomas lancastre sore ferde sayd fayr syres wyll go whether euer ye bydde tho went togyder north wyth hadde viic men army came burbryg whan syr andrew herkela north countre thrugh ordynauce kynge kepe ye countree scotlonde herde tell yt thomas lancastre scomfyted hys company burton vpon trent ordened hym stronge power syr symonde warde also shyref yorke mette baron burburgge anone brake brydge made tree pand whan syr thomas lancastre herde ye syr andrewe herkela broughte wyth hym suche power sore adradde sente syr andrewe herkela wyth hym spake sayde hym thys manere syr andrewe sayde ye may wel vnderstode lorde ye kyng ladde mysgouerned moche fals counsel thrugh syr hugh spenser fader syr hughe sone syr iohan erle arudel thrugh mayster robert baldok fals pylled clerke yt kynges courte dwellynge wherfore praye ye wyll come wyth v alle youre power ye haue ordeyned helpe dystroie venym englond ye traytours ben therin wyll yeue vnto best parte fyue erldoms haue holde wyll make vnto othe wyll neuer doo thynge wythout counsell soo ye shalbe left well euer robert holande tho answered syr andrew herkela sayd syr thomas yt wolde ne consent therto manere thynge wythout wyll comaundement lorde kynge shold holden traytour euermore whan ye noble erle thomas lacastre sawe wolde consent hym maner thyng syr andrew sayd wyll ye consent dystroy venym reame consente one worde syr andrewe tel yere begoo ye shall take holde traytour ony hold v worse dethe ye shall deye euer dyde ony knyght englonde vnderstonde wel ye dyd neuer thynge sorer ye shall repente go doo good lykyth wyll put mercy god went fals traytour tyrau ce fals forsworne man thrugh noble erle thomas lancastre receyued army chyualrye thrughe hym made knyght tho myghte men se archer drawe one syde knyghtes also foughte tho togyder wonder sore also amonge humfroy de boughon erle herforde worthy knyght renoune thrugh crystendom stode fought enmyes vppon ye brydge noble lord stode foughte vpon brydge theyf rybaude sculkyd vnder brydge fyersly spere smote noble knyght ye fudement yt bowellys came aboute fete ther ala sorowe pyte slayne floure solace comforth also curteysye pand syr roger clyfforde noble worthy knyghte stode euer fought well worthyly hym defended noble baron last sore woundyd heed syr wyllyam sullaynde syr roger benfeelde slayne batayll whan syr andrewe herkela sawe syr thomas la castre lassed slakyd anone hys company came vnto gentyll knyght syr thomas layd vnto hym hyghe voyce yelde traytour yelde gentyll erle thomas lancastre answered thenne sayde nay lordes traitours ben none wyll neuer v yelde whyle oure lyues last leuer slayne thruth yelde v vnto syre andrewe en gardyd vppon syr thomas hys company yellynge cryenge lyke wode wulf yelde traytours taken yelde sayde wyth hyghe voys beware syres yt none hardy vpon lyf lymme mys thomas body lacastre wyth worde good erle thomas yede castell sayd knelynge vpon hys knee torned hys vysage warde crosse sayd almyghty god yelde holy put vnto thy mercy wyth vylaynes rybaudes lept aboute hym euery syde tyrautes wood tormentours dyspoyled hym armoure clothed hym obe ray squyres lyuetay forth ladde hym unto yorke water tho myght men see moche sorowe care gentyl knyghtes sledde euery syde ye rybaudes vyllayns egerly dyscryed cryed hyghe yelde traytours yelde whan yelden robbyd bounden theuys ala shame dyspyte gentyll orde knyghthode batayll londe tho without lawe holy chyrche tho nomore creuereence burdell hous batyall fader ayenst sone vncle ayenst neuewe moche vnkyndenesse neuer seen englonde tyme amonge folkes one nacyon one kynred noo pyte hungry wulf hathe shepe wonder grete lordes englonde alle one nacyon medlyd nacons say brytons saxon danys pehypes frenssemen norman spanyerdes romayns henaude flemynges dyuers nacyons whyche nacyons accordyd kynde blood englonde yf soo grete lordes oonly weddyd englysshe people thenne sholde pea haue ben reste amonge theym without ony enuye batayll roger clyfforde take syr iohn mombray syr wyllyam tuchy syr wyllyam fitz wyllyam many worthy knyghtes take batayll syr hugh dandell nette daye taken put pryson sholde haue doon dethe yf hadde spousyd kynges nece erle gylbertes syster gloucestre anon syr berthylmewe badelesmore taken stow parke maneyr bysshop lyncoln neuewe many baron baronetters wherfore made moche sorowe phow thomas lancastre heedyd pountfret v baron hangyd drawen shall tell noble erle thomas lancastre wha take brought yorke many cyte full glade vpon hym cryed hyght voys syr traytour ye welcome blessyd god ye shall haue rewarde longe ye haue deserued caste vppon hym many snowe balles many repreues dyd hym gentyll erle suffred sayd nother worde pand tyme ye kyng herde thys scofyture ful glad ioyous grete hast came poutfret syr hugh spenser syr hugh sone syr iohn erle arundell syr edmonde wodestoke ye kynges brother erle kent syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke mayster robert baldoke fals pyllyd clerke pryue dwelled kynges court came theder wyth kynge kyng entryd castel syr andrewe herkela fals tyraunte thrugh kynges comaundement toke wyth hym gentyll erle thomas pountfret prysoned owne castell newe made stode ayenste abbaye kynge edwarde pand syr hugh spenser fader sone cast thought maner good erle thomas lancastre sholde deed wythoute iugement hys perys wherfore ordeyned thrugh kynges iusticus kyng sholde put vpon hym poyntes treason befell ledde barre kynges iustices bare heed theyf fayre halle owne castell yt made ther many fayre feste ryche poore pand iustices syr hugh spe ser fader aymer balaunce erle pe broke syr edmonde wodstok erle kent syr iohan brytayne erle rychemonde syr robert malemethrop iustyce syre roberte hym couplyd manere pthomas court excludeth maner answer thomas lorde kynge puttyth vppon ye haue hys londe ryden wyth baner dysplayed ayenst pea traytour pand ye worde gentyll erle thomas hygh voyce sayd nay lordes forsoth saynt thomas neuer traytoure pthe iustyce sayd ayen tho thomas oure lorde kyng putteth vpon ye haue robbyd folke murdred people theyf thomas also kynge puttythe vpon dyscofyted people wyth folke owne reame wherfore ye te fledde woode outlaw thomas traytoure ye shall hangyd reaso ye kynge hathe foryeuen iugement loue quene isabell thomas reson wolde yt ye sholde hangyd ye kynge hath foryue iugemet cause loue lygnage asmoche thomas ye taken fleenge outlawe kynge woll heed shalle smyten anone haue hym oute prees brynge hym iugement pwhan ge tyll knyght thomas herde wordes wyth hygh voyce cryed sore wepynge sayd ala saynt thomas fayr fader ala shall deed thus graunt blessydful god answere auayled hym thynge cursyd gascoyns put hym hyther thyder hym cryed wyth hyghe voys kynge arthur moost terryble dredefull well knowen shewed thyn open traytour euyll deth shalt thou ryght anone deye haste thou ryght well deserued pand thenne thyse cruell folke sette vpon gode knyhht thomas scorne olde chaplet alle rente yt worth halfe peny sette hym vpon whyte palfroy full vnsemely also bare wyth olde brydell wyth horryble noyse draue hym castell warde hys deth cast vpon hym many balles snowe dyspyte traytours lad hym castell tho sayde pyteous wordes hondes helde vp hygh warde heuen kyng heuen yeue u mercy erthly kyng hathe v forsaken frere precher wente hym castell tyll came place endeth lyfe vnto whome shroue hym hys lyfe gentyll erle helde frere wonder fast clothes sayd hym fayr fader abyde v tyll yt deed flesshe quakyth drede dethe pand sothe say gentyll erle sette hym vpon hys knee torned hym warde eest rybaude called hygone mo sette honde vpon gentyll erle sayd dyspyte hym syr traytour torne towarde scottes thy fowle deth receyue torned warde nosth noble erle thomas answered tho wyth mylde voys sayd fayr lordes shall wyll worde ye frere went hym sore wepynge anone rybaude wente hym smote hys heed xi kalendas auerell yere grace mccc xxi palas euer suche gentyll blood sholde deth withouten cause reason traytoursly kynge counseylled whan thrugh fals counseyll spenser suffred syr thomas vncles sone put suche deth beheeded ayenst maner reaso grete pyte also suche noble kynge sholde dysceyued mysgouerned thrugh counsell fals spenser whyche tho mayntened thrughe loselry ayenst honour also proffyte warde fell grete vengaunce englonde cause forsayd thomas dethe whan gentyll erle lyf passyd ye pryour monkys pounfret gate body syr thomas kynge buryed hyghe awter ryght syde pthat daye thys gentyll knyght dede hangyd drawen quarel poutfret syr wyllyam tuchet syr wyllyam fitz wyllyam syr werreyn isell syr henry bradborn syr wyllyam cheyne baron al iohn page esquyrer soone yorke drawen hangyd syr roger clyfforde syre iohan mambray baron syr goselyne deuyll knyght pand brystowe drawe hangyd syr henry wemyngton syr henry moun torde baros pand gloucerre drawe hangyd syr iohn gaffarde syr wyllyam elmebrughe baron londo hangyd drawen syr henry tyes baron pand atte wynchelse syr thomas clepepyr knyght ferthermore telle thys cruell occyon atte wyndsore drawe hangyd syr fraunc waldeham baron caunterbury drawe handyg syr berthylmew badelesmore syr berthylmew asshe bourucham baron cardyf walys syr wylyam flemmynge baron phow kynge edwarde wente scotlonde wyth hundrde thousande army myght spede whan kynge edwarde englonde brought floure cheua vnto theyr deth thrugh counsell con ente syr hugh spenser fader syr hughe sone became woode ony lyon euer spenser wolde haue done well kynge louyd theym yt myght hym thynge lyked wherfore kynge gaaf vnto syr hughe spenser fader ye erldom wynchestre vnto syr andrewe herkela erldome cardoyll preiudyce harmynge hys crowne kyng edwarde tho thrugh counsel spenser dysheryted alle ayenst hym ony quarel thomas l castre many dysheryted also cause spenser coueyted haue theyr londes wold desyre wyth wronge ayenst reason tho made kynge robert baldok fal e pylled clerke chaunceler englond thrugh counsell forsayde spenser pand false rybaude coueytouse counseylled kynge moche kyng lete take hys owne warde gooddes lordes put wrongfully deth hys owne honde aswell toke goodes yt within hooly chyrche e goodes yt wythout lete theym put hys tresoury london lette calle hys feytes cousell ye kynge wrought euer dysheryted godes ought thrugh ther cousell lete arer talegge goodes englonde wherfore rychest kyng yt euer englonde wyllyam bastarde yt comquered englonde yet thrughe cousell hym semyd yt hadde ynough made yet euery towne englonde fynde man army vpon theyr owne costes go werre vpon scottes yt enmyes wherfore kynge went scotlonde houndred thousande men army wytsontyde yere lord ihesu crist mcccxxii scottes wente hyd mouteyns wodes caryed englysshmen fro day day kynge myght manere thynge fynde playne felde wherfor many englysshmen lytyl vytaylles deyed ther hungre wonder fast sodenly goynge comynge namely tho bene ayenst thomas lancastre robbyd men vpon hys londes whan kynge edwarde sawe vytaylles fayled hym wonder sore dyscomfyted bycause also yt hys men deyed myght spede enmyes att last came ayen englonde anone came iames douglas also thomas radulph huge hooste englonde northumberlonde wyth englysshmen dryuen englonde came robbed countree slewe ye people also brente twone yt callyd northallerton many twones yorke whan kynge herde thys tydynges lete mane maner men myght trauyllee englysshmen mette scottes ye abbay beyghelande xv day mygelmas en yere aboue sayd englysshmen dysconfyted dyscomfyture take syr iohan brytayne erle rychmonde helde countree erldome lancastre payed huge raunsonne lete goo wente fraunce came neuer agayne phow syr andrewe herkelay take put deth erle cardoil tyme syr andrew herkela ye new made erle cardoil cause taken good erle thomas lancastre phe hadde ordeyned thrugh kynges comaundement englonde bringe hym power yt myght helpe ayenste scottes abbaye beglonde whan ye fals traytour gadred people myght shold haue come kynge vnto abbaye beyghelande ye fals traytour ladde nother coutre thrughe copelonde thrughe therldome lancastre went thrugh ye cou tree robbed slewe folke yt myght ferthermore fals traytour take grete somme golde syluer syr iames douglas ayenst kyng englonde helpynge holdynge scottes thrugh whose treason kynge englonde scomfyted beyghelande yt came thyder wherfore kyng ward hym wonder wrothe lete pryuely enquere coutre aboute yt men enquered aspeyed laste trough foude sought atteynte take fals traytour ye gode erle thomas lancastre hym tolde yt pute vnto deth hys ta ynge att burbrugge hym sayd ye doon sholde take holde traytour holy sayd pwherfore kyng sent pryuely syr anthony lucy knyght countre cardoil sholde take syr andrew herkela put hym vnto dethe brynge thynge vnto ende kynge sente hys commyssion thys andrewe take cardoill ladde vnto barre maner erle worthyly arayed wyth aswerde gyrde aboute hym hosyd sporyd ptho spake syr anthoyn maner syr andrewe sayd kynge puttyth vpon asmoche thou hast orpyd thy dedys dyde moche honour made erle cardoil traytour thy lorde laddest people hys countere shold haue holpe hym batayll beyghel thou laddest awaye countree copelande thrugh erldom lancastre wherfore lorde kynge dyscomfyted scottes thrugh thy treason falsnesse yf thou haddest come tymes bataylle treason thou dydest ye grete somme golde syluer thou receyued iames douglas scot kynges enmye lorde kynge wyl yt ordre knyghthode whiche thou receyued al thyne honour worshyppe vppon thy body brought nought thyn estate vndoyne knyghtes lower degree mowe beware whyche lorde hathe auaunted hugely dyuerse countrees englonde al may take ensample lorde warde truly serue ptho commaunded anone knaue hew hys spore helys lete breke serde ouer hys heed whiche kynge yaue hym kepe defende hys londe ther wyth whan made hym erle cardoyll lette hym vnclothed hys furred taberde hys hode furryd cote gyrdell pand whanne done syr anthony sayde thenne vnto hym andrewe sayde nowe arte thou noo knyghte knaue thy treason kynge wylle thou shalte hangyd drawen thy heed smyten thy bowel take oute thy body brente thy body quartryd thy heed sente london shall stonde vpon london brydge foure quarter shall sente foure townes englonde yt maye beware chastysed yt anthony sayde done manere thynge laste daye octobre yere grace miiicxxii yere sonne torned blood peple saw dured morne tyll xi cloke pof myracles yt god wrought sayt thomas lancastre wherfore kynge lete close ye chyrche dores ye pryory dremed thre nyghtes sewynge preest lede hym hyll wha came ye place yt martryd deuowtly made prayer prayed god saynt thomas myghte haue hys syght ayen hys prayer layed hys ryght hode vpon gode man martryd drope drye blood smale sonde cleuyd hys honde stryketh eyen anone thrugh myght god saynt thomas lancastre syght ayen thankyd tho almyghty god saynt thomas whan myracle knowen amonge men people came thither euery syde knelyd made theyr prayer tombe pryory pountfret prayed holy martyr socour helpe god herde prayer palso yonge chylde drowned welle towne pountfret deed thre daye thre nyghtes men came layed ye deed chylde sayd thomas tombe holy martyr chylde arose dethe lyfe many man sawe pand also moche peple ther mynde god sent theyr mynde ayen thorough vertue holy man god hathe yeue louyd god saynt thomas euermore good man came englonde toke foure felowes came poutfret ye holy martyr dyd theyr pylgrymage good man syke came thyther nakyd saufe preuye clothes whan done torned home ayen theyr owne coutre tolde myracle wher soo euer came pand also two men haue ben heelyd mormale thrugh helpe ye holy martyr thoughe euyll holde curable whan ye spenser herde yt god dyde suche myracles thys holy man nolde byleue yt noo manere wyse sayde openly grete heresye suche vertue hym byleue whan syr hugh spenser sone sawe doynge anone sente massager pountfret dwelled kyng edwarde yt tho grauen scypton cause yt kynge sholde vndo ye pylgrymage rybaude ye messager went warde kynge message came hylle e good martyr doon dethe place made ordure whan hadde done rode warde kynge stronge flyre came vpon hym came yorke tho shed alle hys bowelles fudment wha syr hugh spenser herde tygynges somdele adradde thoughte vndo thys pylgrymage yf myghte ony manere waye anone wente kynge sayde sholde greate sklaundre thrughe alle crystendome deth thomas lancastre yf yt suffred ye peple pylgrymage poutfret counseled kynge comauded shyt chyrche dores pountfret wyche chyrche ye holy martyr enteryd thus dyd ayenst frauchyses holy chirche ye foure yere myght pylgryme come holy bodye bycause monkes suffred men come honour holy body saynt thomas ye martyr thrugh cousell syr hughe spenser wardeyne gascoyne ordeyned quene isabell came fraunce wente syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke murdred sodenly apreuysege thrugh goddes vengauce one iustycys cosented saynt thomas deth lancastre wolde eldest fraunce quene isabell quater yere dwelled fraunce whan syr edwarde eldest sone axed leue tho go frauce speke moder isabel quene fader kynge grauntyd good wyll sayd hym go fayr sone goddys blyssynge myn thynke come ayen hastely thou may wete ouer see fraunce kynge fraunce hys vncle receyued hym moche honour sayd vnto hym fayr son ye welcome cause father come homage ye duchye guyon thrugh englonde kynge edwarde herde telle ye quen isabell edwarde sone wolde come englonde wyth grete power alyautes yt outlawed englonde rebellyousnesse sore dradde put downe lese kyngdom wherfore ordeyned kepe hys castels walys well englond vytayllers theyr appa ylles lette kepe hys ryuers also ye ye feest decolacio saynt iohn baptyst ye cytezyns london sent kyng prochestre c men army also comauded hys letter ordeyend yt euery hundred wepetake otrye wel men army men foot yt sholde put xx hundred commaunded ye alle tho men redy whan ony shoute crye made purpose take alyauntis yt came englond ben bme hym londe put kyngdon ouer lete crye thorugh patent euery fayre euery market englonde yt quene isabell syr edwarde eldest sone erle kent yt take saufly kepte without ony manere harme vnto doynge manere people yt come anone smyte ther hedys without ony manere raunsom takynge man myght brynge syr rogeres mortymer heed wygmore sholde haue hudred poude money trauall pand ferthermore ordened patrent comaunded make fyre vpon euery hyll besyde ryuers lowe countrees make hyghe bekenesse rymbre yf alyuntes came vnto londe nyght tyme thene inhabycauntys aboute sholde endeuoyr selfe goodly hast lyght fyre ye bekenes countree maye warned come mete enmyes ye tyme deyed syr roger mortymyer vcle toure london phow quene isabell syr edward duke guyhenne sone came london dyde quene isabell syr edwarde sone duke yf guyhenne syr edwarde wodstok erle kente syr iohn erles brother henaude company dradde menace ye kyng ne hys traytours trusted goddys grace came south floke ye xxiii daye septembre yere grace mcccxxvi quene syre edwarde sone sent letter mayre comynalte london requyrynge sholde helpynge quarell cause saye dystroye traytours reame none answeres sent ayen whe fore quene syr edwarde sone sent nother patent letter vnder sea tenour whiche letter folowyth maner pisabell grace god quene englonde lady irlonde coutesse pountyf edwarde eldest sone kynge englond duke guyon erle chestre pauntyf moustroyl mayre comynaltee cytee london sendyth gretynge asmoche haue tyme sent letter come thys londe good arraye good manere maner honour profyte holy chyrche dere lorde ye kyng reame al reame myght power kepe mayntene al good folke forsayd reame holden doo vppon praye ye wolde helpynge v moche ye maye quarell comune profyte forsayd reame haue tyme none answere forsayde letter ne knowe mynde party wherfore sende ayen praye charge chat ye bere ayenste v haue cause greue ye ye ben vnto v helpynge wayes ye maye may knowe wytte ye well certe come v thys reame thynke ony thynge thynge shall comyn profyte reame oonly destroye hugh speser enmye enmye reame ye wel knowe wherfore praye charge ye fayth ye owe vnto lyege lord ye kynge v vpon al ye shall mowe fayre ayen v yf sayd spenser enmye come within power ye hym hastely take saufly kepe vntyll ye haue ordeyned hym wyll ye ye leue maner wyse ye desyre honour profyte v ye reame vnderstondynge ye ryght well yf ye prayer streyghte comaundemet thynke v moche beholdynge vnto also ye shall gete worshyp also profyte yf ye sende hastely answere wyll ayen baldok syxte daye octobre whiche letter dawnynge day saynt denys tackyd vppon newe crosse chepe many topyes letter tackyd vpon wyndowes dores vpon place cyte london men passynge way myght rede se tyme kyng edwarde london toure mete messager came halle sayde quene isabell come londe herewhiche hath brought company syr iohan henande hym armes without nombre worde syr hugh spenser ye fader spake thus vnto kynge sayd moost worshypfull lorde kynge englond make good chere certenly ben oures kynge sawe worde comfortable yet fulle sorowfull pensyf hys herte kynge fully eten came halle nother messager sayde quene isabell arryued whiche besyde ypswytche soutfolke syr hugh spenser fader spake messager sayd tell sothe gode fayth fayre frendes come grete strenth c te sothe saye syr sayd messager ne hath companye v houderd men army worde syr hughe spenser fader cryed hygh voice sayd ala ala ben alle betrayes fortes lytell power neuer come londe yf folke thys lode vnto concente therfore mete toke counsell went warde walys arere walsshmen ayenst quene isabell edwarde sone ryght purpose euery chone phow mayster water stapylton bysshop excetre ye kynges tresorer heedyd london tyme kynge edwarde sore adradde leest men london wolde yelde theym vnto quene isabell sone edwarde wherfore sette mayster walter stapylton tresorer wardeyne keper cyte londo mayre soo came gyldeha e london axed keyes yates cyte thrughe vertu strength hys commyssyon wolde haue kepynge cite ye comuners answered sayd wolde kepe cyte honour kynge edwarde isabell quene ye duke kynges sone without ony bysshop tho sore onoyed swore othes sholde abye anone kynge edward come walyes pand ye comuners anone cyte toke ye bysshop lad hym anone amyddes chepe ther smote heed set heed ryght honde forth comyns cyte london heedyd two squyres yt helde bysshop one callyd wylliam wayle yt bysshops neuew callyd iohn padynto also toke burgeys lodon yt callyd iohn mershall syr hugh spe ser espye fader smote heed also tyme ye bysshop london fayr toure makynge close vpon ryuer temse yt withou temple barre fayled stone make therof ende commauded men go frere carmes toke stone make ther toure moche sonde morter olde robous left dyspyte bysshop done vnto holy chyrche hys two squyres buryed sonde thoughe ben houndes laye xi wekes tyll quene isabell sent letter comuners prayed wolde suffre graunte bysshop myght take place buryed excetre owne chyrche soo hys two squyres buryed saynt clementes chyrche without temple barre wonder thoughe bysshop deyed euyll deth coueytous man wyth hym mercy euyll counseylled kynge soone arnold spayne take assetye lede vmli syluer fyue barelles feryers vnto ye douzepers frau ce helpe haste quene isabell deth edwarde sone also arnold put deth without cyte phow kynge edwarde syr hugh spenser erle arundell taken kynge edwarde sente mayster walter stapylton hys tresorer london kepe cyte vnto hym ayenst quene isabell hys wyf ayenst edwarde sone anone hymself toke hym syr hughe spenser sone syr iohn arundell mayster robert baldok hys chaunceler fals pylled clerke toke theyr waye warde brystowe kynge abode lytyll tyme made syr hugh spenser fader conestable keper castel ane kynge spenser went shyppe saylled warde walys toke noo leue kynges stewarde ne none kyngys housholde went ouer walys arere walsshmen ayenst dame isabell quene duke sone erle kente syr iohn henaude wente pursued theyr power encreacyd euery daye laste kynge taken vpon hyll walys syr hugh spenser sone othersyde ye hylle false pylled clerke mayster robert baldok faste besyde theym broughte ayen englonde almyghty god wolde kyng hymself put sauf kepynge castel kenylworth hym kept syr henry yt saynt thomas brother lancastre syr hugh fader came put hym quenes grace edwarde sone duke guyon syr hugh spenser ye tyme take wolde neuer eete meete ne drynke maner drynke wyste haue mercy sauf deed pand quene counsell ordeyned sholde haue doon deth london soo feble hys moche fastynge yt nygh deed therfore ordeyned yt shold haue iugement forde place toure hys heed take body also fro robert baldok yt fals pylled clerke kynges chaunceler men sette vpon theyr heedys chaplettys sharpe netles two squyres blewe ther eerys two grete bugle horne vpon twoo prysoners men myght ther blowen oute wyth horne myle one symond rydynge ye kynges marshall bare vpon spere ther army reuersyd token sholde vndon euermore vpon morowe syr hughe spenser sone dampned dethe drawen hangyd heedyd hys bowel taken hys body brent yt quartred hys four quarter sent four townes englonde heed sente london brydge symond cause yt dyspysyd quene isabell drawen traytours vndone theyr heyres dysheryted phow kynge edwarde put downe dygnyte take hym anone doone quene isabell edward sone grete lordes englonde one assente sente kynge edwarde castell kenylworth kepyng vnder warde syr iohan hachin bysshop ely syr iohan pereye baron bycause shold ordeyne hys parlement certayne place englond redresse amende state ye reame kynge edwarde answerde sayde lordes sayd ye se ful well lo seale gyue power calle ordeyne parlement ye wyll pand thenne toke theyr leue hym came ayen baron englode whan hadde kynges patent thynge shewed lordes tho ordeyned parlemente sholde westmestre vtas saynt hylary grete lordes englonde lete ordeyned theym ayenst tyme parlement sholde whiche daye ye parlement kynge wolde come maner thynge sete hy self assygned neuertheles baron sent vnto hym oo tyme swore goddys souie wolde come oo fote wherfore ordeyned grete lordes englonde sholde lenger kynge depesed sayd wolde crowne edwarde sone elder ye duke guyhenne sent tydynges vnto kynge warde vnder syr iohan erle garen syr iohn bothun bysshop ely syr henry percy baron syr wyllya trusell knyght ye erle syre thomas lancastre yelde vp homage vnto hym englonde pand syr wyllyam trussell sayd thyse wordes psyr edwarde cause haue trayed people englonde haue vndone many grete lordes englonde without ony cause ye shal deposyd ye stand thankyd god also cause ye wolde myn homage also knyghtes englonde holde seryautre ony thynge thys daye ye shall clamyd kynge nother kyng holde synguler man people pand te then london lordes englonde abode syre edwarde abode pryson good kepynge thys daye conuersyon saynt poule xx yere regne pof prophecye merlyn declared kynge edwarde sone kynge edwarde fyrste kyng edwarde prophecyed merlyn sayd sholde come gote carre sholde haue horne syluer aberde white snowe drope sholde come nosethrylles yt sholde betoken moche harme hungre dethe people grete losse londe begynnynge reyge sholde hauted moche lechery sayd sothe ala ye tyme hys tyme grete hungre amonge poore people stro ge deth amonge ryche yt deyed straunge londe wyth moche sorowe soctlonde loste scotlonde gascoyne whyle hymselfe kynge moche lechery hautyd pand also thrugh therle warwyk pand merlyn tolde tyme sholde seme beer sholde brenne batayll sholde vpon arme see felde arayed lyke shelde sholde deye many whyte hedes sayd sothe brynnynge beer yt betokenyd grete drede thrugh kyttyng swerdes bataylle myton came scottes manere elde maner wynge slewe men relegyon prestes seculers wherfore scottes callyd batayll dyspyce englyssmen whych batayll merlyn sayde forsayde beer sholde gote moche harme sholde vpon south west also vpon hys blode sayde also gote sholde lese moche deale londe tyll tyme ye shame sholde hym ouer come sholde clothe hm lyon skyne sholde wynne ayen lost thrugh people sholde come northwest sholde make hym ferde hym auenge vppon enmyes thrugh counsell two owles ye fyrst sholde pa yll vndone tho two owles shold go ouer see strauge lond sholde dwelle vnto certayne tyme thenne sholde come englonde ayen tho owles sholde doo moche harme vnto many one sholde counsell gote meue warre ayenst forsayd beer gote owles sholde arme see burton trente sholde go ouer drede beer sholde flee swanne companye bury towarde north thrugh vnkynde outpulter swanne thene shall slayne wyth sorowe beer sholde slayne ful nyghe owne nest sholde stonde vppon pounfret vpon sonne shall shede beemes many folke hym shalle seke vertue sayd sothe good erle thomas lancastre borne ye northwest cosyn kynge vncles sone lawe made kynge lese moche londe whiche purchacyd wylfully tyll last kyng toke therof shame hym self slewe cruelte gate ayen lost moche thrugh folke ette asseble ye northwest tha made hym adradde auengyd hym baron thrugh counsell syr hugh spenser fader syr hugh sone outlawed theyr wyckydnesse afterwarde came ayen englonde syr e wer vpon thomas lancast soo yt kynge spenser erle arundell theyr power mette wyth thomas lancastre burton vpon trente hym dyscomfyted syr vmfroy erle forde company fledde ye forsayd thomas humfroy theyr co pany burbrugge metinge syr andrew herkela callyd vnkynde outpulter also syr symonde warde erle yorke came mette thomas lancastre huge power dyscomfyted scomfyture erle herforde slayne vpo brydge cowardly wyth spere foundement erle thomas take ladde vnto poufret tho heedyd besyde owne castell afterwarde many hym sought myracles god dyde hym pand tyme merlyn sayd sorowe harme shold deye people londe wherfore many londes shold vpon hym bolder sayd sothe bycause baron doone dethe sayt thomas quarell lancastre peple many londes became bolder meue werre vpo kyng theyr blood torned many nacyons afterwarde merlyn tolde sayd forsayd owles sholde doo moche harme vnto flour lyf deth shold brynge moche dysese sholde go ouer see fraunce make pea floure delyte sholde abyde tyll time sede sholde come fetche tho sholde abyde bothe tyll tyme sholde clothe wyth grace tho two owles sholde seke put pyteuous deth prophecy full well knowe full sothe syr hugh spenser fader syr hugh sone dyde moche sorowe persecucyon vnto ye quene isabel thrugh theyr procurement lorde kynge ordeyned amonge wagys saye xx shelynges daye wherfore ye kynge frauce brother sore anoyed sente englonde letter vnto kynge edwarde come vnto hys parlement parys fraunce kynge edwarde sore adradde come wende haue arestyd tyll yt made amendes trespase ye syr hugh spenser fader sone done ye harme done vnto quene isabell h syster wherfore thrughe hys ordynaunce consente spenser quene isabell went ouer see fraunce make accorde betwene kynge edwarde kynge fraunce brother ther dwellyd fraunce tyll edwarde eldest sone came seke dwellyd tyll alyaunce made bytwene gentyll erle henaude yf wyth ther vertue myght dystroye ouercome venym falsnesse spenser syr edwarde sholde spowse dome phylyp worshypfull lady erles doughter henaude wherfore quene isabel edwarde sone syr edwarde wodstok kynges brother englonde syr iohn power arryued south folke soone pursewed ye spense tyll take put pyteuous dethe sayd theyr copany also grete falsnes yt dyde kynge edwarde peple pand merlyn sayd also gote sholde put grete distresse
