conqueste kyng edwarde carnariuan regned syr edwarde wyndsore sone whyche crowned kyng anoynted westmestre thrugh cousell consent grete lordes ye reame sondaye candelmasse eue yere grace mcccxxvi aege tyme xv yere cause yt hys fader warde castell kenilworth also put downe ryaltee reame englo de without kyng ye feest saynt katheryn yere aboue sayd feest candelmasse tho manere plees kynges bynche astente tho co mauded shyrefs englonde thrughe wrytte warne partyes defendau tys thrugh somnynge ayen also ferthermore prysoners yt kynges gayolles attachid thrugh shyrefs sholde lete go quyte pthe kynge edwarde hys coronacyon prayer besechynge lyege ye reame grautyd chartre stedfast pea wolde axe syr iohnn henaude hys company toke leue kynge lordes reame tornyd home theyr owne coutre ayen eche hade full ryche yeftes euery men value estate pand tho englond rest pea grete loue bytwene kyng hys lordes comynly englysshmen sayd amonges deuyll dede innumerable tresour kyng fader tresour spenser fader sone erle arundell mayster robert baldok kyng chauceler departyd quene isabelles ordynaunce syr roger mortymers wygmore kynge hadde noo thynge therof wyll delyuerrauce ne theyr lode afterwarde ye shall phow kynge edwarde wete vnto stathop mete ye scottes yet tyme kynge castell kenilworth vnder kepynge syr henry yt erle thomas lancastres broder tho erle leycetre kynge grautyd hym ye erldome lancastre ye kyng fader seasyd honde put thomas lancaster broder erle lancastre leycetre also stywarde englonde hys broder tyme syr edwarde kyng edwardes fader made sorowe wythout ende cause myght speke wyth hys wyf ne sone wherfore moche myscheyf though ledde rulyd fals counseyll yet kyng edward sone callyd edwarde longe shankys came worthyest blood worlde wonte yeue grete yeftes large pryue kyng hys owne sone enmyes bothe nyght daye procured make debate contake bytwene hym hys sone isabell wyf frere prechers hym gode fredes euer cast nyghte daye myghte brynge hym pryson amonge theyr company ye freres priuely brought ther frere yt callyd dunhened ordeyned gadryd grete copany folke kepe att nede ye frere taken put pountfret deyed pryson syr henry erle lancastre hadde ye kynges fader kepynge thrugh comaudemete kynge delyuered edwarde ye kynges fader endeture syr thomas berkelay syr iohn matreuas ladde hym ye castell kenylworth castell berkelay kepte hym saufly pand att ester next coronacyon kynge ordeyned grete huge host fyght ayenst scottes syr iohn erles brother henaue came beyonde see helpe kynge edwarde brought wyth hym viic men army arryued att douer leue go forth tyll came yorke kynge abode scottes came thether ye kynge make pea accorde accordement lasted bytwene bat lytyll tyme tyme ye englysshmen clothed al cote hodes paynted letter floures ful semely longe berdes therfore scottes made byl fastenyd vpon ye chyrche doores saynt petyr towarde stangate thus sayd ye scrypture dyspyte englysshemen longe berdes hertles prynted hodes wytles gay cote graceles makyth englode thryftles trinyte daye next began contak cyte yorke bytwene englysshmen ye henaudes ye debate slayne ye erldom nicholl murdred lxxx men buried saynt clementis chyrche folgate cause henaudes came helpe kyng pea ryed vpon payne lyf lymme halfe founde enquest cytye englysshmen began debate phow englysshme stoppyd scottes parke stanope howe torned ayen scotlonde thys tyme scottes assembled theyr power came englonde slewe robbyd yt myght take brent dystroyed north coutree thrugh tyll came vnto parke ahope weridale ye scottes helde theym bussment wha ye kyng harde thorou spyes ye scottes anone ryght hoste desegyd within forsayd parke ye scottes wyst go vnto ther harmes abode parke xv dayes vytaylles faylled euery syde gretly peyred bodyes syth bruce came fyrst brytayne vnto thys tyme neuer seen fayre hoste englysshmen alyaces men fote whyche ordeyned theym fyght wyth ye scottes thrugh eggynge syr henry lancastre syr iohan henaude yt wolde haue gone ouer water wyth haue fought scottes syr roger mortymer cosentyd therto pryuely taken mede scottes helpe myght go away theyr owne cou tre pand mortymer counseylled somoche thomas brotherton ye erle marshall kynge edwardes vncle ye forsayd thomas shold assemble ye tyme vnto scottes assentyd wyste doynge bytwene scottes forsayd mortymer cause yt marshall englonde hym perteyned euer warde sent hastely erle lancastre syr iohn henaude yt sholde fyght scottes preiudyce harmynge hym fee yf dyde sholde stonde theyr owne paryll forsayd erle marshall arayed batayll att reredoos erle lancastre haue fought hym folke yf go fyght wyth scottes thys manere deceyued wyste thynge treason thus kyng pryncypally dysceyued whan nyghte mortymer yt watche kepe ye host nyght distrobled ye watche yt noo thynge myght done meane whyle scottes stele nyght ward theyr owne coutre fast myght pand kyng fasly betrayed wenyd alle ye traytours londe ben brought ende sayd pnow lordes tratoursly kyng edwarde dysceyued meruayllously boldly scottes dyde werre iames douglas wyth two hudred men army rode thrught host kyng edwarde nyght scottes escaped towarde theyr owne coutree aboue sayd tyl came ye kyng pauylyon slew many men theyr beddes cryed naward naward nother tyme douglas douglas wherfore kyng hys pauylyon moche lke wonder sore frayed blyssyd almyghty god ye kynge taken greto peryll tho reame englonde nyghte mone shone full clere bryghte kynges men scottes scapyd harmeles pand oon morowe whan kynge wyste scottes escapyd theyr owne coutree wonder sory fulle hertely wepte wyth hys yonge eyne yet wyste hadde hym doone treason pbut fals treasone fulle welle knowen good whyle storye makyth mencyon ptho kynge edward came ayen vnto yorke full sorowfull hys host departyd euery man wente owne countree wyth full heuy chere mornynge semblaunt henaudes toke theyr leue went theyr owne countree kynge theyr trauayll hugely rewarde pand bycause vyage kynge dyspended moche tresoure wastyd tyme seen two moones fyrmament ye one clere derke men myghte see thrugh worlde pand grete debate tyme agaynst pope iohan xxii saynt petyr emperour almayn tho made hym emperour ayenst ye popys wyll tho helde hys see auinyon werfore emperour made hys crye rome ordeyned nother pope ye hyght nycholas yt frere mynor ayeng ryght holy chyrche wherfore cursyd power pope soone layed cause suche merueylles seen men sayde worlde nygh ende pof dethe kynge edwarde carnaryuan go ayen syr edwarde carnaryuan yt kynge edwardes fader somtyme kynge englonde put downe hys dygnyte ala trybulacyon sorowe hym befell thrugh fals counsell yt louyd trustyd vpon moche yt warde dystroyed thrughe theyr falsnesse god wolde pand edward carnariuan castel berkelay vnder ye warde kepynge syr moryce herkelay also syr iohn matreues made complaynte hys sorowe dysesee ofte tymes axyed wardeyns trespassyd ayenst dame isabell hys wyf syr edwarde sone yt made newe kyng wolde vysyte hym pand tho answerde one hys wardeyns sayd worthy lord dyspleyse yt shal telle cause doon vnderstonde yf lady youre wyfe came ony thynge nyghe ye wolde strangle slee also ye walde doo lorde sone wyse ptho answerde wyth symple ala ala pryson youre owne wyll god yt wote thought yt neuer wolde dede soo wolde god thenne alle sorowe passyd pit longe ye kynge thrugh counsell roger mortymer grautyd warde kepynge syr edward fader vnto syr thomas toioursy forsayd syr iohan matreuers thrugh kynges letter put holy forsayd syr moryce warde kynge toke ladde kynge vnto castell corf whiche castell kynge hatyd ony dethe kept hym tylle came vnto saynt mathewes daye septembre yere grace mcccxxvii forsayde syr roger mortymer sent maner deth wyse sholde done deth anone forsayd thomas iohan see letter co maundement made kynge edwarde carnariuan good good solace myght soupere nothynge kynge wyst traytory whan tyme go bed kynge went bedde laye slepte faste kynge laye slepte trautours fals forsworne ayenst theyr homage feaute came pryuely kynges chambre theyr company wyth layd huge take vppon wombe wyth men pressyd helde faste downe foure corner table hys body wherwyth good mane woke wonder sore adradde deed slayne torned hys body vp tho downe tho tooke fals traytours tynauntes horne put hys foundemente depe myghte spyt copre brennynge putte thrughe horne hys bodye soo slewe theyr lorde noo thynge perceyued enteryd atte gloucetree phow kynge edward spowsyd phylyp ye erles doughter henaude yorke crystmasse tho next sewynge syr iohan henaude brought hym phylyp brother doughter yt erle henaude hys nece englonde kynge spowsyd atte yorke moche honour syr iohan bothum bysshop ely syr wyllyam melton archebysshop yorke sange masse sondaye euen conuersyon saynt poule yere grace mcccxxvii bycause kyng yonge tender aege whan crowned full many wornges doon whyle fader lyued bycause trowed counserllers fals aboute hy cousyelled hym doo wise tha reason wold wherfore grete harme ye reame ye kynge dyrected kynges dede almyghty god wote wherfore ordeyned att kynges crownynge ye kynge tender aege sholde gouerned xii grettest lordes englonde wythout whome thynge sholde doon say tharchebysshop caunterbury tarchebysshop yorke bysshop wynchestre bysshop herforde erle lancastre therle marchall erle kent ye kynges vncles erle garenne syr thomas wake syr henry percy syr olyuer yngham iohan rous baron thyse sworne truly counseyll kynge shold answer euery yere parlement shold done tyme theyr gouernall ordynaunce sone vndoon moche harme englonde kyng ye lordes sholde gouerne hym gouerned rulyd quene moder dame isabell syr roger mortymer wolde thynge done bothe amonge hygh lowe toke vnto theym castels townes londes rent grete harme losse crowne estate mesure phowe pea made bytwene englyssheme scottes also iustyfyenge troylesbaston kynge edwarde wytsontyde seconde yere regne thrughe cou seyll moder syr roger mortymer ordeyned parlemet northampton parlement ye kyng thrughe hys cousell none ye londe within aege grauntyd accordyd ye scottes manere ye f autees homage ye scottes sholde crowne englonde foryaue theym euermore hys chartre ensealed ferder endenture made scottes vnto kynge edwarde kynge heries sone whiche endenture calle regman ye whyche conteyned homage feautees fyrst kyng scotlond prelate erles baron ye reame scotlonde wyth theyr seales set theron chartres remebraucis kynge edwarde baron theyr ryght ye forsayd reame scotlonde foryeue ayen holy chyrche also blake crosse scotlond ye whiche good kynge edwarde coquered scotlode brought ye abbay scone full precyous relyque also ferthermore relacyd fully forgaue londe noble baron tye ye ream scotlond olde conquest ferthermore yt thys pea holden cotynuelly last scottes bounde vnto ye kynge xxx thousande poude syluer payed wythin thre yere euery yere xm poude eue procyon pand ferthermore aboue spake bytwene partyes aboue sayd ye dauyd drytonautyer kynge roberte brus sone ye fals tyraunt fals forsworne ayenst othe yt arose ayenst hys leyge lord ye noble good kynge edward falsly made hym kynge scotlonde yt aege v yere thys cursyd couseyll dauid spoused berewyk dame iohn ye toure kynge edwardes syster gestes tellyth vpon mary mawdeleyns day yere grace mcccxxviii greate harme empayrynge kynges blode wherof gentyll lady came ala tyme wonder moche ye fayer daoysell dysperagyd syth maryed ayenst al comyns wyl assent englonde frome tyme brute conquered albyon named londe owne name brytayne callyd englonde name engyst reame scotlonde holde reame englond ye crowne feaute homgae brute conquered londe yaue albanak yt seconde sone callyd ye londe albayn hys owne name soo hys heyres yt came hym shold holde brute heyres yt say kynges brytayn feaute homage frome tyme vnto thys tyme kynge edwarde tame scotlond holde reame englonde feaute seruyce aboue y sayd cronycles englonde scotlonde berythe wytnesse playnely accursyd ye tyme parlement holden northampton fals councyll kyng falsly dysheryted yet aege pand yet whan kyng edward put hys ryalte englonde yet men put feautes seruyse scotlonde ne fraunchyses dysheryted hym euer pand neuertheles grete lordes englonde ayenst conferme pea rwes abouesayd sa f quene isabell yt tho kynges moder edwarde bysshop ely lorde mortimer reason lawe wolde fynalle pea sholde made bytwene without comyn assente englonde pof debate bytwene quene isabell syr henry erle lancastre leycetre rydynge bedforde sayde dauyd spowsyd dame iohane toure ye towne berwyk sayde scottes dyspyte ye englysshmen called dame iohanne countesse make pea cowardly pea yt tho ordeyned ye kynges persone bare wyte blame wyth wronge makynge accorde alle done thrugh quene roger mortymer longe quene isabell ne toke hond lordshyp pountfret almoste londes ony value apperteyned crowne englonde soo kynge dyspendede hys v hys escheker quene isabell mortymer hadde grete mayne retenewe yt folowed ye kynges courte euer went toke kynges pryces peny worthes good ch pe wherfore countre came fullsore addrade almoost dystroyed theym ptho began comyna te englonde haue enuye isabell quene yt somoche louyd whan came ayen pursue ye fals traytours ye spenser fro fraunce tyme fals traytour roberte holonde bytrayed hys lorde syr thomas lancastre tho delyuerde pryson wonder preuy witth quene isabell also roger mortymer auaylld hym lytyll taken myghelmasse yt tho cam nexte rode warde quene isabell london syr thomas whyther smote heed besydes towne saynt albons thys syr thomas dwelled syr henry erle lancastre put hym asyde drede quene quene loued hym wonder moche prayed vnto kyng hym ye thomas might exyled englonde noble erle syr henry lancastre often tymes herde comyn claymore ye enghysshmen ye dysease doon englond also dyuers wro ge done comyn people whyche kyng bare blame wronge fulle yonge tender aege thought good man awaye slake sklauder ye kynges persone yf myght ony manere wyse kynge therof nothynge gylty wherfore inperyll lyf lymme pand assebled retenuwe wente spake kynges honoure also amende estate syr thomas brotherton erle marchall syr edmond wodstok kynges vncles also men london made theyr othe hym fo mayntene ye quarell theyr cause kynge sholde holde house hys meyne kyng ought haue ryalt e quene isabell sholde delyuer hondes kynges honde alle manere lordshyps rentys townes castels apperteyneth vnto crowne englonde quenes haue done medle none thynge pand also syr roger mortymer sholde abyde dwelle vpon londes moche people moche comyn people dystroyed gretely domaged thoroughe suche wrongfulle takynge pand also enquere howe whome kynge betrayed falsly dysceyued att stanhope thrughe whose counseyll scottes went awaye nyght kynge also thrugh whoos counseyll ordynauce made kynges coronacyon put downe saye kynge amendement helpynge reame honour hym sholde gouerned rulyd xii grettest wysest lordes reame wythout sholde thynge grauntyd ne done sayd whiche couenauntes malicyously put downe fro kynge many harmes shamys repreues haue falle kyng hys reame vnderstonde asmoche edwarde kynge englonde tyme ordeyned assent playne parlement vnder warde gouernaunce henry erle lancastre cosyn saluacyon hys dody take castell kenilworth warde thrugh colour quene isabell mortymer without consent ony parlement tooke ladde hym neuer none kynred myght wyth hym speke ne see tratorursly toke morored hym whose deth arose sklaudre thrugh crystendom whan done also tresore ye syre edwarde kernaruian left many place englonde walys wastyd borne awaye wythout wyll kynge edwarde sone dystruccyo hym al folke palso thrughe whose counseyll ye kynge yaue vp kyngdom scotlond whiche reame kynges aucetours full sore traueiled dyd many noble theyr ryght delyuered vnto dauyd robert brus sone ye ryght yt ryght reame world wyst also chartres remebraunces yt ryght scotlond take tresory taken scottes kynges enmyes dysheritynge hym successours grete harme hys lyeges grete repreef englysshemen euer palso wherfore dame iohan toure kynges syster edward dysperagyd maryed vnto dauyd robertbrus sone traytour enmye vnto englonde thrugh whoos counseyl take enmyes hondes englonde pand meane whyle ye good erle henry la castre hys companie toke counseyl poyntes aboue sayd myght amended worshyp kynge hys profyte profyte leyg quene isabel thrughe coniectynge also mortymers lete ordeyne parlement salysburye ye parlement mortymer made erle marche ayenst baron wyll englonde preiudyce ye kyng hys crowne syr iohan eltham kynges brother gyrde swerde corne waylle tho callyd erle corne waylle euer quene isabell procuryd moche ayenst sone ye kyng warde ye forsayde syr edward lode parlemente erle lancastre wolde come ordeyned power ayenst quene isabel mortymer men london ordeyned fyue hudred men army pwhan quene isabel wist doynge swore god hys name full angerly euell tyme thought vppon tho poyntes tho sente quene isabell mortymer theyr retenwe kyngys retenewe soo ordeyned amonge huge hoste counseylled kynge vppon nyght rode xxiii myles bedford erle lancastre company thought haue hym dystroyed nyght rode besyde kynge sone knyght drede dethe done kyng vnderstond erle henry lancastre hys company wolde haue dystroyed kyng hys counseylle euer wherfore kynge somdele wardes hym heuy anoye pwhan erle marshall therle kente kynges brother herde thys tydynges rode soo message bytwene theym kynge grauntyd hym hys pea therle henry lancastre certayne raunsomme leuen thousande pounde neuer payed afterwarde thyse lordes helde syr henry lancastre syr beaumont syr fouk fytz waren syr thomas rocelyn syr wyllyam trusdr ynghtes moo hym consented alle exyled thrughe counseylle quene isabell mortymer ye mortymer wayted haue theyr lode yf myght thrugh ony maner coniectynge coueytous hadde moche wyll grete pyte phow kynge edwarde went ouer see doo homage vnto kynge frau ce duchye guyhenne longe kyng fraunce thrugh counseyll hys donzepers sente kynge edwarde englode sholde come parys homage reason wolde duchye guyon thrughe cousell lordes englonde kynge edwarde went ouer see ascyon tyde came vnto parys thyrde yere regne homage vnto kyng frauce kyng receyued hys homage made hym moche ioy worshyp whan kynge edwarde done hys homage hastyly sent englonde thrugh quen isabell moder anone hastyly came ayen englonde vpon wytsonday without ony takynge leue ye kynge frau ce wherfore wonder wrothe phow syr roger mortymer bare hym proudely soo hyghe shall ye syr roger mortymer wygmore desyred coueted hygh astate kyng grauntyd hym callyd erle marche thorughe hys lordshyp became soo proude hauteyn yt wolde lese forsake name yt elder euer fore ye cause let hym calle erle marche none comnyns englonde durste calle hym name callyd ye kyngys crye men shold calle hym erle marche mortymer bare hym hauteyn proude wonder wyte also dysguysed hym wonder ryche clothes al manere reason shapynge werynge wher englysshmen grete wonder manere myght contryue fynde suche manere pryde yd amonge comynly yt pryde sholde longe endure pand tyme syr gyffray mortymer yonge mortymers sone lete calle hym kynge foly befell warde dede soo full pryde wretchydnesse helde rounde table walys men der came couterfeted doynge manere kyng arthur table openly fayled noble kynge arthur ye moost noble lord renomme worlde hys tyme yet came neuer none suche ye noble knyghtes cryste dom dedys army assayed dwellyd wyth kynge arthur helde hym lorde souerayne well seen conquered bataylle romayne yt callyd froll gate hym reame fraunce slewe hym wyth hys owne hondes also faught gyaunt callyd dynabus slewe hym rauysshed fayre elayne kyng howels ne e kynge lytyll brytayn slewe bataylle emperour rome yt callyd lucye hadde assembled ayenst arthur fyghte wyth hym moche people romayns pebytes sarasyns man cowde nombre dyscomfyted alle story tellyth pand thyme comyn voyce spronge englond thrugh coniectynge ordynaunce frere prechers syr edwarde carnariuan kyng edwardes fader whome geste tellyth sayde alyue castell corf wherof comyns englonde almoost sorowe drede whether soo wist traytoursly mortymer hym done murthred phow edmonde wodstok erle kente kynges brother edwarde carnaryuan heedyd wynchestre vppon tyme befell soo syr edmonde wodstok erle kent spake vnto pope iohan xxii auinion sayde almyghty god ofte tymes done thomas loue lancastre many grete myracles many men wymmen yt thrughe dyuers maladyes vndoone pa vnto worlde thrughe prayer broughte vnto helthe soo syr edmonde prayed pope hertely wolde graunt hym grace forsayde thomas myghte traunslatyd pope sayde naye sholde traunslatyd vnto tyme better certyfyed clergye englond seen theyr obedyence thynge god done loue saynt thomas lacastre suggestio forsayd erle kent hadde vnto hym made whan edmonde saw myght spede purpos touchynge traunslacion prayed hy cousell touchynge syr edwarde carnariuan hys brother sayd longe agon kynge englonde thynge myghte beste done touchynge delyuerauce sythe yt comune fame thrugh englonde yt alyue hole sauf wha ye pope herde hy tell yt syr edwarde alyue comauded ye erle vpo blyssynge sholde helpe power myght deliuered pryson saue body manere myght brynge thynge ende assoyled hym copany pena et culpa delyuerauce tho toke edmond wodstok leue ye pope came ayen englode wha syr edmonde come ye frere prechers came sayd syr edwarde brother yet alyue ye castell corf vnder ye kepynge syr thomas gurnay tho sped hy forsayd edmonde fast myght tyll came ye castel corf acquaynted hym spake fayre iohn dauerel conestable castell yaue hym ryche yeftes haue acquayntaunce hym knowe cousell thus befel forsayd edmonde prayed specyally tel hym pryuely lorde brother syr edward yf lyued deed yf alyue prayed hym one haue syght hym syr iohn daueryl hygh herted ful courage answerde shortly syr edmond sayd syr edwarde hys brother helth vnder hys kepynge durst shewe hym vnto man syth defended kyngys halfe edwarde yt edwardes sone carnuariuan also comaundement quene isabel ye kynges moder syr roger mortymer sholde shewe hys body noo world sauf vpo lyf lyme disherytynge heyres euer fals traytour falsly lyed warde take thes lad castell berkeley syr thomas gurney comaudemente mortymer tyll dede sayd syr edmonde wodstok wyst thynge syr edwarde brother deed wherupon toke letter vnto kyng edward brother worthy lorde receyued ye letter hym behyght hym ryght faythful message without fayll syr edmonde toke leue forsayd iohn yede owne coutre lordshyp kent anone iohan wist syr edmonde gone kent owne lordshyp anone went ye hast myght fro castell corf came vnto syr roger mortymer toke hym letter syr edmond wodstok erle kent taken hym closyd ensealed owne seale whan syr roger mortymer receyued letter vnclosed sawe conteyned therin began rede wherof begynnynge pworshyppes reuerence wyth brother alyegaunce subieccyon syr knyyt worshypfull dere brother yf please praye hertely ye gode co forthe shall soo ordeyn yt ye shall come pryso delyuered dysese ye ben vnderstondyth grete lordshyp haue myn assentynge moost grete lordes englonde wyth theyr apperyll say wyth armour tresour wythout nombre mayntene quarell ferforth ye shall kynge agayn ye haue sworne vpon boke aswell prelate erles baron pwhan syr roger mortymer saw vnderstode myght strenth letter anone hert wrathe began boll euyll herte bare ward syr edmode wodstok erle kent wyth hast myght wente vnto dame isabell quene ye kynges moder shewed syr edmonds letter wyll purpose coniected ordeyned put downe kynge edwarde wyndsore sone ryalte kyngdome nowe certes syr roger sayd hathe syr edmonde done faders soule sayde wyll therof auenged yf god graunte lyf shorte tyme quene isabell wente vnto kynge edwarde sone att parlemente wynchestre haue amende wrongys trespass done amonge people hys reame tho toke shewed hym letter syr edmond wodstok made ensealed hys owne seale badde hym vpon blessynge sholde auengyd vpon syr edmond vpon dedely enmye tho quene sore wrothe warde syr edmonde erle kente sessyd neuer praye vntyll sone tyll sente hast hym vpon kynge sent hys letter syr edmoode wodstok sholde come speke wyth hym att wynchestre manere thinge left whan syr edmond sawe kynge sente hym wyth hys letter ensealed ye hastyd hym alle yt myghte tylle came wynchestre pbut whan quene wyst syr edmonde come wynchestre tho anone prayed faste wende vnto kynge edwarde sone good erle arested anone ladde vnto barre robert hamonde coroner kynges housholde assocyed vnto hym syr roger mortymer tho spake sayd roger sayde syr edmonde erle kent ye shall vndersto de done v wyte pryncypally vnto lyege lorde kynge edwarde englonde almyghty god hym saue kepe ye deedly enmye traytoure also comune enmye reame ye haue ben aboute many day make pryue delyueraunce syr edwarde somtyme kynge englonde broder whiche somtyme put downe hys ryaltee ye comyn assent lordes englond peasynge lorde kynges estate also reame ptho answerd good man sayd soth syr vnderstonde well neuer traytoure kynge ne reame doo god worlde therfore kynges leue shalle preue defende man ought ptho sayde mortymer syr edmonde ferfor knowe may well gaynsayd presence shalle well prouyd fals mortymer letter syr edmonde hadde take syr iohan daueryll castell corf take kynge edwarde hys brother syr edmonde wyst ne supposed thynge syr iohn daueryll fals delyuer letter suche wyse vnto mortymer thought manere thynge letter thenne mortymer sayd syr edmonde shewed letter sealed axed hym yf knewe ye letter ye seale syr edmonde lokyd theron auysed hym longe tyme prynte seale myght see letter wyst well seale thought somme letter bore grete charge thought thinge letter sayd openly herynge ye soth thys seale wyll sake plo sayde mortymer syres ye al hath sayd knowlegyth hym letter hys seale ye shall conteyned therin thenne mortymer openyd letter folde tofore togyder redde openly worde worde herynge theym whan letter redde sayd loo syres ye haue herde alle ye herin wryte hath knowlegyth letter seale may go therfro thenne cryed yaue dome sholde hangyd drawen hys heed smyten manere traytour hys heyres dysheryted euer ladde forth put pryson whan done quene wist dampned way lawe lyf lyme hys heyres dysheryted euermore thrugh open knowlegynge playncourt thought good forsayd syr edmond hastyly slayne wythout wyttynge kyng elles kynge wolde lyghtly foryeue hym hys dethe thenne shode torne theym moche sorowe empechyd anone quene thrugh counseyll mortymer wyth ony counsell sent hast baylyfe wynchestre sholde smyte syr edmondes heed erle kente wythout ony manere abydynge respyte vpon payne lyf lymme sholde haue none execusyon cause caryenge withstandynge iugement tho toke baylyes syr edmonde pryson ladde hym besyde castell wynchestre made gonfermer smyte hys heed none durste doo soo deyed ala whyle say tenth daye octobre thyrde yere kynge edwarde regne pand whan kyng wist therof wonder sory lete entyere hym frere mynors wynchestre pof deth syr roger mortymer erle marche befell tyme syr roger mortymer erle ye marche proude hauteyne helde lorde reame pere tho became coueytous folowed dame isabell quenes courte kynge edward moder beset hys peny worth offycers quenes house holde manere kynges offycers dyde made takynge touchynge vytayle also caryages dyde bycause expencys gadre tresoure dyde without nombre myght ptho made hym wonder preuy wyth quene isabell moche lordshyppe rete grete lordes englonde hym adrad wherfore kyng counseylle warde hym agreued ordeyned amonge vndo hym thoroughe pure reason lawe cause kynge edwarde ye kyges fader traytoursly thrugh hym murdred castel corf sayde playnly parte boke deth pand kynges counseyll louyd mortymer tolde hym preuyte ye kynge counsel aboute daye daye hym dystroye vndo wherfore mortymer sore anoyed angry deuyll ayenst kynges counseyll say wolde auenged euer toke pit longe afterwarde kynge edward dame phylyp wyf dame isabell kynges moder syr roger mortymer ne wente vnto notyngham soiurne befell quene isabel thrugh couseyll mortymer toke keyes yates castell notyngham man myght come nother ne thrugh commaundement mortymer ne kynge ne none couseylle pand tyme fel mortymer deuyll wrath bolled also wrathe ayenst kynges men edward pryncypally ayenst theym hym accusyd kynge deth syr edwarde fader pand pryuely cou seyll take bytwene quene isabell mortymer bysshop lyncoln syre symode bedford syr hugh trompyngton preuy theyr counseyll vndo theym mortymer accusyd vnto kynge faders deth treason felonye pwherfore tho kynges couseyll whan wist mortymers castynge pryuely came kynge edwarde sayd mortymer wold theym dystroye bycause hym accusyd kynge edwardes dethe fader prayed hym wolde mayntene theyr ryght pand thyse lordes pursued quarell syr wyllyam mountagu syr wyllyam de bohum syr wyllyam broder syr rauf stafforde syr robert herforde syr wyllyam clynton syr iohan neuell hornby many theyr co sent thyse swore vpon boke mayntene quarell moche myghte befell syr wyllyam mountagu ne none kynges frendes muste herberowed castell mortyme went toke theyr herberowe dyuerse place twone nothyngham tho sore ferde leest mortymer sholde theym dystroye haste came vnto kyng edward syr wyllyam mauntagu castell pryuely hym tolde ne none hys copany sholde take mortymer without counseyll helpe wyllyam elande constable castell pnow truelye sayd kynge loue well therfore counseyl ye go forsayd conestable commaude hym name frende youre helpe take mortymer al thynge yleft vpon peryll lyf lyme ptho sayd mountagu syr lorde graunt mercy ptho wente forthe forsayd mountagu came conestable castell tolde hym kynges wyll pand answerde sayde kynges wyll sholde doone moche myghte wolde spare manere dethe swore made othe ptho sayde syr wyllyam mou tagu constable herynge alle helpynge quarell certes dere frende v behouyth werke aduys take mortymer syth ye keper castell hath keyes warde psyr sayd constable wyll ye vnderstonde castell yates ben lockyd keyes dame isabell sent hyther nyght hath keyes ther layeth vnder lursell bedde vnto morowe ye maye come castell yates manere wyse knowe aleye stretchythoute warde vnder erthe sayde castell gothe weste whiche aleye dame isabel quene ne none men ne mortymer ne none company knowith shall lede thrugh ye aley ye shall come castell withoute aspyenge ony man yt enmyes nyghe syr wyllyam mountagu lordes quarell constable also went theym hors made semblaut go mortymers syght anone mortymer harde thys tydynges wende yt wolde haue gone ouer see fere hym pand anone ryght copanye toke couseyll amonge theym lete theyr passage snetelletters anone porter none grete lordes sholde go home theyr owned coutrees yf arested take amonge thynges wyllyam elande conestable sayd castell pryuely ladde syre wyllyam mountagu hys company sayd waye vnder erth tyll came castell went vp toure mortymer syr hughe trompynton theym ascryed hydously sayd traytours nought ye ben comyn castell ye shall deye yet euell dethe euerychone anone one theim mountages company vp wyth mace smote hugh vpon heed brayne braste fell grounde soo deed euyll deth ptho toke mortymer armyd hym toures dore whan herde noyse theym drede pand whan quene isablell sawe mortymer taken made moche sorowe herte thyse wordes vnto theym sayd fayre syres praye ye doo noo harme body thy knyght welbeloued frende dere cosyn ptho wente then came brought mortymer presentyd hym vnto kynge edwarde commaunded brynge hym saue warde pbut anone consentynge vnto mortymers doynge herde tell taken wente hydde pryuely nyght wente towne eche one waye heuy herte mornynge chere lyued vpon theyr londes well myghte pand yere mortymer take hadde ix score knyghtes without quyres sergau te army fote men thene mortymer ladde london syr edmonde bedforde ladde wyth hym taken ye constable toure kepe pbut warde mortymers lyfe examyned westmestre kynge geate lordes englonde peryll myght falle reame enquer also whiche consentynge syr edwardes dethe kynges fader also thrugh whome scottes escaped fro stanhope scotlonde without leue kynge edwarde also ye chartre ragman delyuered vnto scottes homage feautees lordes scotlode conteyned scottes sholde doo euer englysshe kynge reame scotlond wherfore iugyd drawen hangyd treason myscheyf came vnto hym saynt andrewes euen yere incarnacyon lorde ihesu cryste mcccxxx phowe kynge edwarde gate ayen vnto hym gracyously homage feautees scotlonde wherof put oute thrughe ye false counseyll quene isabell moder syre roger mortymer newely made erle matche haue ye herde iohan bayllol tyme pea chosen kynge scotlonde cause came eldest doughter erle dauyd huntyngton kynge alysanders broder scotlond deyed without heyre hys body begoten iohan made feaute homage kynge edwarde henryes sone thyrde londes scotlonde afterwarde sayd hys homage thrugh counseyll scottes yere lorde mcclxxiiii sente vnto pope thrugh fals suggestyo made hys othe vnto forsayd kynge edwarde ouer hys estate wil whyche othe pope hym assoyled thrughe hys bully hym ysent pand anone kynge edwarde wyst therof ordeyne anone hys baron came vnto berwyk coquered towne whyche conquest slayne xxv thousande vii hundred bayllol kyng scotlond came yeldyd hym gode kynge edwarde ye kyng delyuered hym toure london grete lordes hym yt tho taken berwyk yaue theym saufconduyte goo scotlonde scottes sythe thrugh theyr falsnesse warred vpon good kynge edwarde whan syr iohan bayloll kynge scotlonde sawe wente ouer see vnto dunpier lyued vpon hys londes well myght tyll ye scottes wolde amende theym theyr mysdedys trespaas ladde hym syr edwarde sone wherfore scottes dyspyte hym callyd hym syr iohan turnlabard bycause wolde ne offend ne trespaas ayenst good kynge edwarde englonde soo soke hys reame scotlonde sette therof lytyll pryce syr iohan dwellyd longe tyme fraunce tyll deyed syr edward sone receyued hys herytage dyde homage kynge fraunce londes dunpier befell afterwarde edward iohan bayllols sone hym squyre englond yt yorke shyre callyd iohan barnaby edwarde bayllol louyd hym moche nyghe hym full preuy iohn barnaby debate frenche man towne dunpier slewe hym wente hys way haste myghte castell haue socoure helpe hys lorde anone came offycers towne take iohn barnaby felon syr edward lorde holpe hym rescowed hym nyght made hym go castell went hys waye came englonde withoute ony harme pand whan kyng fraunce saw syr edwarde rescowed felon became wonder wrothe ayenst syr edward anone lete hym arestyd toke hys hondes londes tho dwellyd syr edward pryson vnto tyme syr henry beaumount came fraunce whiche henry somtyme erle anguysshe scotlonde put therof whan chacordement bytwene englonde scotlond thrugh quene isabell syr roger mortymer theyr company ye moryage made bytwene dauyd roberte brus sone dame iohanne tour kynge edward syster englond well vnderstonde thys att ende sholde come ryght yf syre edwarde baylloll ryght heyre reame scotlonde pand kyng fraunce lowys louyd moche syr henry wyth hym full preuy thought make delyueraunce syr edward baylloll yf myghte ony maner wyse ptho prayed kynge wolde grace gaut hym syre edwarde bayllols body vnto nexte parlement myght lyue hys owne rente meane tyme myghte stonde iugyd perys att parlement kynge grauntyd hym prayer made forsayde edwarde delyuered pryson manere aboue sayd anone pryson syr henry toke hym forth hym ladde hym englonde made hym dwelle pryuely att manere sandhall vpon ouse yorke shyre lady vescy soo ordeyned hym huge retenewe englysshmen also alyuntes conquere ayen herytage yaue moche syluer vnto ye souldyours alyauntes helpe hym behyght helpe hym myght faylled hym att hys moost nede pand tyme dauyd erle moryf herde tell syr edward bayloll pryuely come englond came hym made wyth hym gerte ioye comynge sayd vnto hym behyght hym greate lordes englonde sholde hym entendaunte sholde hym holde kynge ryght heyre scotlode dyd hym feaute ptho came syr henry beaumonte kynge edwarde englonde prayed hym waye charyte wolde graunt greate vnto syr edwarde baylloll myghte sau ly goo londe frome sandhall vnto scotlonde conquere hys ryght herytaunce scotlond pthe kynge answerde sayde yf suffre bayllol go thrugh londe scotlonde thenne people wolde saye yt shold assentynge vnto company pnow syr praye yt ye wolde yeue hym leue take hym souldyours englysshmen myght saufly lede hym thrugh londe scotlonde syr vpno thys couenaunte yf befall god bydde dyscomfyted bytayll thrugh scottes also al lordes holde bayllol ben euer rente haue englonde kynge vppon couenaunte grauntyd theyr bone towchynge hym tho quarell whiche claymed haue londes rente reame englonde thyse name tho lordes pursued sayd matere quarell pthat saye syr edwarde bayllol whiche chalengyd reame scotlonde syr henry beaumonte erle angusshe syr dauyd stroboly erle theles syr geffray mombraye walter comyn many put theyr herytage sctlonde whan pea made bytwene englonde scotlonde sayde ye shall vnderstonde thyse lordes tooke theym fyue houndred men armes two thousande archer fote men tho wente shyppe rauen pore sayled see tylle came vnto scotlond came londe kynkehorne xii myle fro saynt iohannes towne anone sent shyppes agayne shold hurte ne empeyred neyther taht man sholde go shyppes agayne thoughe nede abybe perylles flee stonde rather suffre deth flee mayntene true quarell whan erle fyffe fyers man sterne harde bayllol come taste londe scotlond came hast kynke horne iii thousand scottes dystroye hym shold come londe syr edwarde bayllol company hym dyscomfyted whiche dyscomfyture syr alysader seton slayne many erle fyffe th sore full euyll ashamyd lytyll co pany hym dyscomfyted shamefully put hym company alyue flee ptho came syr edwarde bayllol toke coo tree aboute hym tyll came vnto abbay dufermlin ther founde vytaylles hym folke amonge thynge founde chambre aboute fyue houndred grete staues fyne oke longe prykes yren stele toke delyuerd moste strogest men companye anone yede fro then lodged hym felde ii myles saynt iohanes towne whan burgeys towne herde erle fyffe dyscomfyted thrughe baylloll brake ye brydges made ouer water erne bayllol myght go ouer wherfore lodged hym nyght lytyll hede toke reste sayde vnto people dere lordes ye know full well ben lodged bytwene enmyes maye v hampre noo bote dethe wherfore yf abyde stylle nyght wene shall torne v moche harme power scotlonde may euery wexe encrece maye doo ben lytylle people ayenste theym wherfore praye loue almyghty god make v bolde hardy may myghtely take scottes nyght boldly werre vpon theym lete v pursue theym thys nyghte yf trauaylled thorugh v see hardynesse scottes see traueylled wery sorer woll adradde v fyght fyersly thenne shall fyght pursue soo thrughe grace god worlde shall speke doughtynes chyualry pand syres vnderstondeth wel companye came syr robert baylloll graunted well vnto counseyll therof ryght gladde anone pursued vppon scottes became wonder wery baylloll company sore folowed dyde moche harme sorowe thrugh ther assente thy myght feblynesse theym helpe lytyl people pbut tho sayd scottes amonge nowe befall lytyll people baylloll hath wynge doth v moche traueyll sorowe certes semyth v werketh grace wonder gracyous hys quarell certes shall dede maye come hym v yelde sith fader sete v pryce pand amonge alle hys thynges baylloll people passed water erne robert swynerton sone fyers angrye wente forthe sawe people army full well arayed forth wente vnto wyth faught slewe toke many wolde abyde neuertheles assewte wende grete hoste scotlond whan came morowe gadred theym togyder restyd theym whyle pand whyle englysshemen rested noble baron thomas vescy noble baro stafforde pryckyd theyr hors vp downe hylles kepe estrees countree pryckyd vp downe saw grete host gode araye ordeyned theyr wynge helmes sheldes shynynge comynge vpon thene came tho two baros ayen vnto bayllols folke sayd loue god almyghty good coforth ye shall haue batayll one ryght pand tho spake syr fouk sone garenne baran greate renowne dedys army syres vnderstonde wyll saye haue seen many dyuers wynges well amonge sarasyns iewes amonge scottes yet sawe neuer fourthe parte wynge fyght therfore yf ye wyl abyde enmyes ben ynough yf gode herte good courage loste therfore loue god take v gode herte lette v bolde ad thynke neuer wyues ne oure chyldren co quere enmyes batayll pand thrugh helpe lorde shall ouercome wyth came hoste scottes warde theym full serely ayenst syr edwarde baylloll thre bataylles well arayed armoure pand wonder fyersly came warde bayllols company whan syr donald erle marcell scottes sawe sayd vnto roberte brus sone robert brus thyse wordes syr robert sayd full fore thynkyth att herte thyse people baylloll hathe brought wyth hym sholde deye wyth dy te scottes swerdes sythe ben crysten men ben therfore thynkyth grete charyte sende vnto theym yelde theym vnto mercy raunsomme theym vnto greuous raunsomme moche haue taken oure londes done yll certes sayd syr roberte brus haue well rerceyued thou arte enmye traytour vnto scotlonde sythe thou wylte consente saue dedely enmyes haue done v moche sorowe shame semyth wel ye theyr assente certes robert sayde syr donald falsly ye lye theyr company ne theyr consent yt hastyly ye shall se wyll fyz e wyth rather ony thys company certes syr robert sayd shall mauger thy hede assayll thou wyth yt pryckyd theyr stedys fye sly vpon gaskemore theyr wynge theym folowed reng tho came mette wyth baylloll hys copany hangynge bough strayte passage fast hastyd vnto ye englysshmen ye thousand felle vnto grounde echone ouer vpon hepe hors man bayllol men myghtyly stode ayenst theym fast slewe scottes grounde many wounded soo longe tyll stode vpon theym foyned theym wyth theyr swerdes speres thrughe theyr bodyes fulle sore trauaylled vppon theym tylle became wonder wery wyste doo scottes lete alyue fledde awaye saue selfe beste manere myght tho pursued theym syre edwarde baylloll hys men slewe theym tyll nyght fro thes wente saynt iohannes towne toke helde vytaylled self owne wyll foude ynough wherwith make mery tho made baylloll men yt wonded goo shyp sayll englonde hele ther woundes ye tyme flemynge see stonge theyf robber callyd crab flemi ge dryuen flaundres hys wyckydnesse therfore came scotlond holde scottes dyde moche harme englysshmen myght thys crabbe mette bayllols men ye see wouded batayll yt sent ayen englonde hele theyr woundes crabbe yaaf theym gete assawte wold haue slayne theym euery chone englysshmen defended well manly dyscomfyte crabbe company tho gan fle scotlond pand cam towarde saynt iohanes towne foude grete conpany scottes yt come ayen togyder dyscomfyture gaskemore whyche byseyged bayllol hys men towne saynt iohan anone tolde tolde scottes dyscomfyted englysshmen yt woundyd gaskemore went towarde englonde fort hele theyr woundes sayd scottes yt sholde haue nother power ne myghte ne grace ayenst edwarde bayllol cause scomfyted empeyred alle chyualry scotlond handfall men opte ayenst scottes slayne wherfore couseylled remeue sege saynt iohannes towne kepe theym best manere myght pthe scottes vnderstode crabbe sayd sothe soke sege wente then nyghte pwhan thys thynge knowe thrughe scotlonde lordes knyghtes dyscomfyted gaskemore scotlonde thrughe syre edwarde bayllol ye shall vnderstonde yt lordes ladyes gentyls scotlond came wonder faste saynt iohannes towne yeldyd theym vnto bayllol hym dyd homage feaute theyr sondes yelde theym pea theym receyued frely fro then te abbay scone crowned kyng scotlond lete crye hys pea thrughe londe pand tyme befell kynge edwarde helde parlement amonge hys leyges newe castell vpon tyne amende trespaces wronges ben done londe syr edwarde bayllol kynge scotlonde came hym thyther dyde hym homage feautee reame scotlond thys maner kynge edwarde englonde gadred ayen hys homage feautees scotlonde wher put thrughe counseyll assent dame isabell hys moder syr roger mortymer erle marche tho toke bayllol kyng scotlond hys leue kynge edwarde englonde went then owne londe scotlonde set lytyll suche counseylled hym holpen hym hys quarel wherfore wente hym went lyued theyr owne londes renttes scotlond pand befel warde longe kynge scotlonde ne remeued came toure anande tooke hys dwellynge thyder came hym company knyghtes stronge men worthy yelded vnto kynge bare theym fayr dede cou tenauce trustyd moche vpon theym anone traytours sawe trustyd moche vpon theym ordened amonge theym fyfty company wolde haue slayne theyr lorde kynge thrugh grace almyghty god brake thrugh walle hole chambre god wolde scapyd theyr trechery hys men slayne escaped moche dred vnto towne cardoyll helde hym sore anoyed befell vpon ladyes euen ye cocepcyon ptho sent kynge edward baylloll kynge edwarde englonde falsly tratoursly lytyll tyme put shame sorowe thrughe lyege men vppon trustyd wonder moche prayed hym ye loue god wolde mayntene hym helpe hym ayenst hys enmyes kynge englond hym grete pyte behight helpe hym socour hym set hym worde shold hold hym pea styll ye forsayde cyte cardoyll tyll yt gadred power ptho ordeyned kyng edwarde englonde counseyll london lete gadre men diuers shyres englond whan alle redy wente towarde towne berwyk vpon twede theder came hym kyng edward baylloll scotlond powere beseged towne made without towne fayr towne pauylyons dyched theym abowte drede scottes made manye assawte onnes wyth engynnes ye towne wherwyth dystroyed many fayre house chyrches also beten downe ye erthe grete stone spitously came gonne engynes neuertheles ye scottes kept ryght well towne yt tho two kynges myghte come therin longe tyme n theles kynges abode longe tyll tho within ye towne fayled vytaylles also wery wakynge wyst pand ye shall vnderstende tho scottes yt wythin ye towne berwyk thrugh comyn counseyl theyr assent lete crye vpon ye wally twone myght haue pea englysshme therof prayed kyng grace mercy prayed gym trwes viii dayes vpon couenaunte yt yf rescowed syde towne towarde scotlond ye scottes within viii dayes yt wolde yelde theym vnto ye kyng towne also holde couenaunt prouffred kinge xii hostage towne berwyk pwhan hostage delyuerde vnto ye kynge anone tho towne sent vnto ye scottes tolde theym theyr sorowe myscheyf scottes tho came pryuely ouer water twede ye bought abbaye syr wyllya dyket tho stewarde scotlonde many came wyth hym put theym theyr grete peryll themself att tyme ther lyf came ouer brydge yt broke ye stone away many theyr company drowned forsayd wyllyam went ouer company came shyppes englond slew barge hull xvi went towne berwyk water syde wherfore scottes helde tho towne rescowed askyd theyr hostage ayen kynge englonde kynge sente theym worde aye axyd theyr hostage wro ge syth thath came towne enlonde syde couenaunt bytwene theim towne sholde rescowed halfe scotlonde anone tho commauded kynge edwarde yelde towne wolde haue hostage scottes sayd towne rescowed welle ynoughe therto wolde theym holde whan kyng edwarde sawe scottes breke theyr couenauntes made wonder wrothe anone lete syr thomas fytz wyllyam syr alysa der feton warden berewyk whyche thomas person dunbarre lete take fyrste afore hostage cause syr alysanders fader keper towne pand tho commaunded euerye daye two hostage towne tyll deth yf yelded towne sholde teche breke theyr couenauntes whan towne herde thyse tydyng became wonder sory sente kyng wolde graunt viii dayes respyte bytwene two hundre men army xx men armes myght strenthe go bytwene ye towne berwyk theym vytaylle towne must holde rescowed yf soo xxi xxii slayne tho two hundred sayde towsholde holde rescowed thys couenaunte holde sente hym xii forsayd towne hostage kynge englonde grauntyd theym theyr prayer toke hostage saynt margaret eue yere grace mcccxxxiii scottes came fyersly well arayed foure wynges mete kynge edwarde englonde edwarde kynge scotlonde theyr power came faste sharply ayenst euensonge tyme tyme flood atte berwyk water twede man myghte goo ouer hys hors fote water bytwene tho two kynges ye reame englonde tyme abode scottes syde cause englyssgmen sholde haue drowned pthys arraye scottes came batayll ayenst two kynges englonde scotlonde vaunt warde scotlonde thyse lordes therle moryf iamys frysell symond frysell walter stewarde reynolde cheyn patryke greham iohan le graunt iamys cordoyl patryk parkeys roberte caldecottes phylyp melledrum thoms gylbert rauf wyseman adam gurdon iamys gramat roberte boyd huhhe park xl knyght newe dubbyd vic men armes iiim comyns fyrste parte thalfe batayll thyse lordes stewarde scotlonde erle mory iamys vncle wyllya douglas dauyd lyndesey marcolyn flemynge wyllyam keth dnsen cankok xxx bachelers new dubbyd pin seconde parte batayll thyse lordes iamys stewarde corden alein stewarde wyllyam abbrehin wyllya morys iamys fytz wyllyam adam lemost walter fytz gylbert iohn cerleton robert wallam viic men army xviim comyns pin thyrd parte batayll scotlonde thyse lordes erle moref erle ruf therle strahern ye erle soth erlonde william kyrkkelay iohn cabron gylbert hey wyllyam ramsey wylliam predegest kyrston harde wyllyam gurde arnold garde thomas dolphyn wyth xl knyghtes newe dubbyd ixc men army xvm comyns pin fourth warde batayll scotlonde thyse lordes archbalde douglas ye erle lencuax alysander le brus ye erle fyff iohn canbell erle atheles roberte lawether wyllyam vypouynt wyllyam lonston iohnn de label groos de sherenlawe iohan de lyndesey alysander de gray ingram de vmfreuille patryk de polesworthe dauyd de wymes mychell scot wyllyam landy thomas de boy roger mortymer xx bachelers new dubbyd ixc men army xviiim iiiic comyns erle dunbar keper castelle berewyk halpe scottes l men army syr alysander ceton keper ye sayd towne berwyk c men ef army also comyns ye towne wyth iiiic men army viiic fote men pthe somme therles lordes aboue sayd amounteth lxvi pthe bachelers newe dubbyd amouteth clx pthe men army amounteth iiimc pthe sume comnyns amounteth liiim iiic pthe totalle people abouesayd amounteth lxvmviicxlv thyse lx vi gretate lordes ladde greeste lordes abouesayde infonre bataylles tolde beforen allon fote kynge edwarde englonde edwarde bayllol kyng scotlonde hadde well apparelled theyr folke foure bataylles fyghte fote ayenst scottes theyr enmyes pand englys mynstrels blewe theyr trumpetes yr claryons hydously ascryed scottes tho euery englysshe batayll two wynges pryce archer whiche batayll shot arowes faste soo sore scottes myghte helpe themsefle smote scottes thousandes vnto grounde began flee fro englysshmen saue theyr lyues whan scottes knaues saw scomfyture scottes fall fast grounde preckyd faste theyr maysters horse sporis kept theym peryl sete theyr maysters force whan thenglyssmen saw lept theyr horse faste pursued scottes abode slewe downe ryght pthere men myght see doughtinesse noble kynge edward hys men manly pursewed scottes flowe drede men myght see many scottysshman caste downe vnto ye grou de baners dysplayde hackyd peces many gode haberyoyne stele blode bathe many tyme scottes gadred copanyes euer discomfyted pand befell god almyghty wolde scottes day nomore fayson ne myghte ayenst englysshemen xx shepe among v wulues scottes dyscomfyted yet scottees well v men ayenst one englysshmen ye batayll done halydoune hyll besyde towne berwyk whiche batayll slayne scottes xxxv thousande vii houndred xii englysshemen xiii victory befel englysshmen saynt margyretes euen holy virgyn martyr yere lorde ihesu cryste mcccxxxii pand whyle thys doynge lastyd englysshe page toke pylfre scottes slayne euery man myght take wythout ony chalengynge ony man thys gracyous victory kynge torned hym agayne vnto syege berewyk pand whan syeged sawe herde kynge edwarde spede yelded hym towne wyth castell morowe saynt margaretes daye pand englond vnto hys tresorer purueyours golde moneye sholde sete vnto hy nede proctours messyngers cursedly ful slouly serued hym hys nede deceyued hym whoos defaute latch kyng toke trewes bytwene hym kynge frauce thenne kynge edwarde full shame sorowe hys herte wyth drewe hym fro sege come brytayne soo grete stryue batayll loste many peple whan doone come dressyd hym ouer see englond warde pand kynges herte ful sorowe aguysshe welllynge syghynge sayd vnto lady thys wyse po blessyd lady saynt mary cause euer goynge fraunce al thynges wether fallen ioyfull lykynge wold haue alway tornynge people slayne taken prysoners erle ewe lorde thonkeruyll hu dred knyghtes men armes vi hondred foot men nombred towne subbarbes vnto bare walle thynges myghte bere caryen robbyd dyspoyled kynge passed forth ye coutre brede xx myle wastyd manere thynge yt founde whan phylyp valoys perceyued thys alle thought faste hym wyth stronge hoste yet wolde come nygh hym breke brydg beyonde ye water seyn fro royn parys hymself fled vnto cyte parys hast myght pfor sothe noble kyng edwarde whan came parys brydge founde broken within two dayes let make agayne morowe assumpcon lady kynge edwarde passed ouer ye water seyn goyege warde crescy dystroyed way townes peple dwellynge ther feest saynt bartholomewe passed ouer water vnhurt host neuer fonde ony manere way ne passage iim slayne letted theyr passage ouer ptherfore xxvi daye auguste kynge edwarde felde fast frescy hauynge thre batayls englysshmen en coutred mette phylyp valoys hauige hym iiii batayls whyche leest passed gretly nombre englysshe people whan two hostes mette togyder fell vpon hym kyngh beme duke loreyn erles also flaunders dalauson bloys harecourt aumarle neuors many erles baron lordes knyght men armes ye nombre mvcxlii fraude put awaye syege came xxvii daye iuyll yere grete host stronge power neyghed sege calays whiche phylyp last daye iulii sente kynge edwarde worde wolde gyue hym playne batayll ye thyrde daye ye euesonge tyme yf durst come fro sege abyde wha kynge edward herde ony without longe taryenge longe auysentente accept gladly ye daye houre batayll yt philyp assygned whan kynge fraunce herde ye next nyght set hys tentys fyre remeued went waye then cowardly thenne ye towne castell besyeged saw none helpe ne socour ye kynge fraunce ne men also theyr vytayls within spended wastyd faute vytayls refresshynge eten horse houndes cattes myse kepe theyr trouth long myght wha sawe foude amonge last thyng amo ge ete ne lyue ne socour ne rescowe frenssheme syde wist well muste nedes deye defaute el yelde towne anone went toke downe ye baners armes frauce euery syde hange wente ye walles ye forsayd towne dyuerse place naked euer borne sauf theyr shertes theyr pryue clothes helde swerdes naked poynt donward theyr hondes putte rope halter theyr neckes yelded vp key towne castell kynge edward englond grete fere drede theyr liues goodes drede herte kynge edwarde sawe alle thys mercyable kynge lord receyyed grace fewe grettest prysoners estate gouernaunce towne sent englonde abyde theyr raunson kynges grace al comynallte towne kynge lette goo weder wolde pea wyth ony harme lete bere theyr thynges yt myghte bere carye away kepynge ye twone castell hymself thenne thrugh meditacyon cardynales sente pope trewes take twene fraunce englond ix monethes next folowynge aboute myghelmas kynge thynges doynge ye scottes pryuely nyght toke towne berwyk sleynge theym withstode theym man el blessyd god castell saued kept englysshmen therin whan kynge perceyued alle thys torned ayen englonde wrothe myghte wherfore parlemet westmynstre grauntyd kynge euery sacke wulle l shellyng durynge ye terme vi yere myght myghtlyer fyght defende reame ayenste scottes mysdoers whan thynges redy kynge hasted hym warde syege phow kyng edwarde crowned kynge scotlonde howe prynce edwarde toke kynge fraunce syr philyp hys yonger sone batayll peyters xxxi yere hys regne xiii daye ianyuere kynge beynge castell berwyk fewe men hauynge faste greote hoost towne yolden vnto hym without ony maner defence dyffyculte tha kynge scotlond saye syr iohn bayloll consyderynge howe god dyde many meruaylles gracyous thynges kynge edwarde att owne wyll fro daye daye toke gaaf vp reame scotlonde crowne scotlond rokesburgh ye kynges hondes englonde vnder hys patent letter made anone kynge edwarde presence prelate worthy men lordes lette hym crowne kyng scotlond whan thinges done erdeyned countres wyll torned ayen englonde greate worshyppe pand whyle vyage doynge scotlonde syre edwarde prynce wale man enspyred god guyhen cytee burdeux treatynge spekyge chalenge kynges ryght englonde hadde reame frauce wold aueged wyth stronge honde prelateg peres myght men countree consented welle hym syr edwarde prynce wyth greate hooste gadred hym vi daye iuyll wente frome burdeux goynge traueylynge many dyuerse countrees tooke many prysoners moo vi thousande mem armes countree wente tooke towne remorantyne saloygne besyeged castell vi dayes att vi dayes ende yolde castell vnto hym taken lorde crowne syr bursygaude many knyghtes men armes moo lxxx fro then toren peten fast chyneney hys noble men hym hadde stonge batayll frensshmen hundred theyr men armes slayne erle daunce stewarde fraunce taken wyth hondred men armes whyche yere xix daye septembre faste pyeters prynce wyth thousande ix hondred men armes archer ordeyned batayll kynge iohan fraunce comynge tho prynce warde wyth vii thousande chosen men armes moche people greate nombre whyche slayne duke burbon duke athene many noble men ef vyctory somme men taken prysoners theym slayne daye batayll iiiimiiiicxl xxxii yere kynge edwarde v daye maye prynce edwarde kynge iohn fraunce philyp hys sone many worthy prysoners arryued gracyously hauen plumouth xxiiii daye moneth aboute thre none came london lo brydge wente forthe kynges palays atte westmynstre came soo grete multytude presse peple abowte theym beholde se wonder ryall syghte vnnethes fro maddaye tylle nyghte myghte come westmyster kynges raunson fraunce taxed sette thre myllyons scute two sholde worthe nobell ye shall vnderstande myllyon thousande thousande mennys raunson sette att thre thousande thousaynde floreyns one effecte yere made iust solempne smytfende beynge present kynge englonde kyng fraunce kynge scotlonde many worthy noble lordes pthe xxxiii yere regne kynge edwarde wynsore well loue knyght hode ownne worshyppe att reuerence kynge fraunce lordes att tyme held wonder ryal costly feest saynt george passynge ony euer holden afore wherfore kynge fraunce scornynge sayd saw neuer ne herde suche solempne festes ne ryaltes holden ne done wyth taylles wythoute payenge golde syluer pand xxxiii yere hys regne xiiii kalendas iulii syre iohan erle rychmonde ayenst alle wolde come whoos name stede kynge pryuely wyth foure sone edwarde lyonell iohan edmonde xix greate lordes helden felde worshyppe pand yere tolde sayd theym sawe come blood ye combe thomas protestacon wolde neuer ayen englonde tyll endes warre bytwene frauce hym pand soo xxvi yere hys regne wynter come kyng edward trauaylled ryne costes aboute saynt hyllarye tyde departes host went burgon warde wyth met peasybly duke bourgon behyghtynge lxx thousande floreyns sholde spare hys men h peple kynge grauntyd att requeste dwelled vnto xvii daye marche yt whiche tyme come kynge edwardes eere stroge theues see vnder erle saynt poule xv daye marche yggynge wayte vpon townes rastynge rye place vyllages see cost hadden entred enmyes towne wynchelle slewe euer withstode sayd theyr comynge wherfore kynge gretly meued wratthed torned ayen warde parys comauded hoste dystroye sle strench swerde honde spared ye iii daye apryl kyng come parys departed host dyuers batayls iiiic knyghtes newe dubbyd one syde hym syr henry duke lancastre vnder pea trewes went vnto yates cyte proferynge yt wolde abyde batayll felde vnder suche condicyon yt yf kynge englonde ouer comen god forbyd sholde yt sholde neued chalenge kyngdom fraunce theym short scornfull answere came tolde kynge lordes herde sayd thene went forth newe kynghtes many makyng assawte cyte dystroyed subbarbes cyty whyle al thynges doynge englysshmen made redy auenged vpon shame dyspyte done ye yere wynshelse ordeyned nauye lxxx shyppes men london marchauntes xiii thousande men armes archer went serched skumed see manly token helde yle caux wherfore frensshmen say abbot cluyn erle tankeruyll bursygaude yt tho stewarde fraunce wyth many men coutre ye comune assent ye lorde charles yt th regned fraunce hastyd went kyng englond askynge besechynge hym stedfaste pea euerlastynge vpon certayne condycones yt shewed wryten whiche whan ye kyng hys couseyll seen pleased hym neuer deale syth wolde none wyse ye tyme better accorde delyberacyon ye frensshemen besely grete stauce asked trewes see costes kyng grautyd pand morow vtas pasche kynge torned hym wyth host warde orlyauce destroyenge wastynge ye coutre way went theder ward felle vpon theym seche storme tempest yt none nacyon neuer herde ne sawe none suche thrugh whyche thousandes ouer men thryr horse theyr iourney thrugh vengeaunce sodeynly slayne perysshed whiche tempest full grete yet fered ye kyng ne moche peple wente forth theyr vyage yt begone wherfore ye feest phylyp iacob may fast carnocu sayd lordes frauce metynge kyng engelonde apsyble accorde fynall vpon certayne condyons grauts artycularly gadred wryten togyder euermore laste dyscertly made kynges proffytable theyr reames one assente charles regner gouernour frauce parys reame wryten made vnder dare carnocu xv daye may offred ffred ye kyng englod requyring grace thynges wryten yt wolde benyngl admyt holde erme stable theyr heyres euermore then whiche thyng artycles whan kyng edwarde seen grautyd yt partyes sholde sworne goddes body euangelyst yt sayd couenaunt sholde stablysshe accorded graciously therfore ordeyned dressed euery syde two baron two baronettes two kynghtes admitte
