forthe vnto westmynster vnto kynges palays spoused vnto kynge rycharde well worthely abbaye westmynster crowned quene englonde hyr trendes came hyr hadde grete gyftes well cherysshed refresshed longe tyme aboden pand thys yere batayll done kynges palays westmester certayne poyntes treason bytwene syr iohan ansley knyght defendaut carton squyre appellaunt thys syre iohan ansley ouercame carton made hym yelde hym wythin lystes anone carton dyspoyled harneys drawe lystes forth vnto tyburne hangyd falsnesse pand viii yere regne kynge rycharde seconde syr edmonde langley erle canbrydge kynge rychardes vncle wente portyngale fayr company men armes archer strengthynge helpynge kynge portyngale ayenst kynge spayne hys power kynge portyngale victory enemyes thrugh helpe comforth englysshmen whan iourney done erle cambridge come home aye people englonde haste blessed god blessyd gyftes amen pand yere kynge rycharde helde crystemas maner eltam pand yere tyme kyng armony fledde hys owne londe came englond haue helpe socoure kynge ayenst hys enmyes hadde dryuen hym hys owne reame brought vnto kyng eltham kynge helde ryall feest crystmasse pand kynge welcomed hym dyd moche reuerence worshyp commaunded hys lordes make hym chere euer coude besought kynge hys grace helpe comforthe hys nede myghte brought ayen kyngdome londe turkes deuoured destroyed moost parte londe fled drede come hyder socoure helpe thenne kynge hauynge hym pyte compassyon hys grete myscheyf greuous dysease anone tooke hys counseyll asked beste answerde sayde yf lyked hym gyue hym ony good weldone touchynge hys peple trauell ferre londes grete ieoperdye soo kynge gaf hym golde syluer many ryche gyftes iewels betaught hym god passed ayen englonde pand thys yere kynge rycharde wyth ryall power wente scotlonde warre vppon scottes falsnes destruccyon scottes done vnto englysshemen march scottes come downe ye kynge treat wyth hym lordes trewes certayne yeres ouer kynge couseyll gauted theym trewes certayne yeres kynge torned hym ayen englode whan comen vnto yorke abode rested hym syr iohn holonde erle kentes broder slewe erles sone stafforde heyre daggar cytee yorke wherfore kynge sore anoyed greued remeued then came london mayer alderman comyns solempnyte myghte done ryden ayenst kyng brought hym ryally thrught cytye vnto westmynstre owne palays pand ix yere kynge rychardes regne helde parlemet westmynster made two duke marqueys fyue erles fyrste ma made duke kynges vncle syr edmonde langle erle cambridge hym made duke yorke vncle syr thomas wodstok erle bukyngham hym made duke gloucestre syr lyonuer yt erle oxford hym made marqueys deuelyne henry balyngbrok duke sone lancastre hym made erle derby syr edwarde duke sone yorke hym made erle ruttelond syr iohan holonde erle kentes broder hym dyde make erle huntyngdon pand syr thomas mombraye hym made erle notyngham erle marshalle englond syr mychell de lapole knygh hym made erle southfolke chaunceler englonde erle marche parlemet holden westmynster playne parlement amonges lordes comyns proclamed erle marche heyre parente trowne englonde kynge rycharde whiche erle macche wente ouer see irlonde vnto hys lordshyppes londes erle marche erle vlster irlond ryght lyne herytage castell hys laye tyme ther came vpon hym grete multytude busshmentes wylde irysshmen take hym destroy hym come oute fyersly castell wyth people manly faughte man taken wen peces deyed vpon who soule god haue mercy pand x yere kyge rychardes regne erle arundell wente see greate nauye shyppes armed men armes goode archer whan come brode see mette wyth hole flete come wyne lade frome rochell whiche wyne enemyes goodes nauye sete vpon theym toke theym brught theim vnto dyuerse porte hauens englonde london ye myght haue tonne rochel wyne beste xx shellynges sterlynge grete chepe wyne englonde tyme thanked god almyghty phow fyue lorde arosen rattecote brydge regne kyng richarde xi yere thenne fyue lordes arosen atte rattecote brydge destruccyon rebelles ye tyme ye reame pthe fyrste fyue lordes syr thomas wodstoke kynges vncle duke gloucestre seconde syr rycharde erle arundell thyrde syr rycharde erle warwyk fourth syr henry balynbrok erle derby fyft syr thomas monbray erle notyngham v lordes sawe myschyef mysgouernaunce falsnes kynges counseyll wherfore time cheyf kiges counseyl fled londe ouer see syr say alysander neuyll archebysshop yorke syr robert lewe marqueys deuelyne erle oxforde syr mychell de la pole erle southfolke chaunceler englonde thre lordes went ouer see came neuer ayen deyed pand tha fyue lordes aboue sayd made parlemente westmynster toke syr robert tresilyam iustyce syr nycholl brembre knyght cytezeyn lodon syr iohn salysbury knyght ye kynges housholde vske sergeaunt armes many moo peple taken iuged vnto deth counseyll v lordes parlemete westmester treaso put vpon theym drawen ye tour londo thrugh cyte fourth vnto tyburne sholde hanged theyr throtes cutte thus serued deyed th thys parlement westmynster syr symonde beuerle knyghte garter syr iohn beauchap knyght stewarde kynges housholde syr iames berners werefore iuged vnto deth ledde fote toure hylle hedes smyten many moo v lordes pin parlement xii yere kynge rychardes regne lette crye ordeyne generall iustes called turnement lordes knyghtes iustes turnement holden london smythfelde manere straugers londe countree euer thyder ryghte welcome holden ope housholde grete festes also grete gyftes gyuen manere stranges kynge syde one sute theyr cote ther armure sheldes hors trappure whyte hertes cownes abbout theyr neckes chaynes gold hangynge thervpo crowne hangynge lowe hertes body whyche herte kynges leueraye gaafe lordes ladyes knyghtes squyres knowe hys housholde frome people pand feest camen iustes xxiiii ladyes ladde xxiiii lordes garter chaynes gold alle sutes hertes sayde frome toure horsbacke thrughe cytye london smytfelde iustes sholde holden pand feeste iustes holden generalle al tho wolde come theder londe nacyon euer holden durynge xxiiii dayes kynges costes xxiiii lordes answere manere people wolde come thyd theder came erle saynt poule frauce many worthy knyghtes wyth hym dyuerse partyes full worthely arayed holande henaude came lorde ostruaut ye duke sone holande many worthy knyghtes hym holand full well arayed whan feest iustynge ended kynge thanked straungers gaf many ryche gyftes token theyr leue kynge lordes ladyes went home ayen theyr owne coutres grete loue moche thanke pand ye xiii yere kyng rychardes regne batayll done kynges palays att westmynster bytwene squyer nauerne yt wyth kynge rycharde squyre yt called iohn walssh poytes treaso thys nauerne put vppon walsshman nauerne ouercome yelde hym recreaut aduersary anone dyspoyled armure drawe oute palays tyburne haged falsnes xiiii yere kynge rychardes regne syr iohan gaunt duke lancastre wente ouer see spayne chaleng hys ryght wyfes tytle vnto crowne spayne grete host people armes archer hym duchesse hys wyf hys thre doughters ouer see spayne ther grete whyle att last kynge spayne began treate duke lacastre accorded togyder thrugh theyr bothe counseyll maner ye kynge spayne sholde wedde duke doughter lancastre ryght heyre spayne shold gyue vnto ye duke lancastre golde syluer caste grete wegges many iewels moche viii charyetes myght carye euery yere duringe duke lyf lacastre duches wyf x thousande marke golde whyche golde auenture charge sholde theym spayne yerely bryng vnto bayon duke assygnes suerte made also duke maryed hys doughters vnto kyng portyngale tyme wha done come home ayen englonde hys good lady hys wyf also many worthy men deyed vpon flyx pin xv yere kynge rychard regne helde crystmasse manere wodstok erle penbroke yonge lord tendre aege wolde lerne iuste knyghte called syr iohn saynt iohn roden togyder parke wodstoke worthy erle penbroke slayne knyghtes spere caste hym whan coupled thus good erle made ye ende therfore kynge quene made moche sorowe deth pand xvi yere kynge rychardes regne iohan de beyng tyme mayer london iohn wal worth henry vanner beynge shreues london tyme baker man bare basket hors brede fletstrete warde hostre came yonge man bysshop salysbury called romayn toke bors lofe basket ye baker asked hym dyde soo romayn torned ayen brake baker heed neyghbours came wold haue arested thes romayn brake fledde lordes place ye constable wolde haue hym bysshops men shette fast yates kept place yt man myght entre moche people gadred thyder sayd wolde haue hym el wolde brenue vp ye place alle wyth came mayer shreues wyth moche people cessyd malyce comyns made euery man go home hose kepe pea thys romayns lord bysshop salysbury mayster iohan waltham ye tyme tresorer englonde syr thomas arundell archebysshop yorke chaunceler englonde bysshop made hys complaynte vnto chaunceler peple cyte lodon two bysshops grete malyce vengeaunce come vnto kynge wyndesore made greate coplaynt vpon mayer shreues anone cyte warde came kynge counseyll caste vnto cytye greuous herte wonder grete malyce anone sodeynly ye kyng sent ye mayer lodon two shreues came hym vnto castell wyndsore kynge rebuked mayer shreues full foule offence done ayenst hym offycers hys chambre london wherfor deposed put mayer bothe shreues done xiiii dayes afore ye feest saynt iohn baptyst ye kynge called hym knyght called syre edwarde dalyngrygge made hym wardeyne gouernour cyte chambre lo ouer hys people ther kepte offyce foure wekes bycause gentyl tendre cytezens london wherfore kynge deposed hym made syr bunde wyne radyngton knyght conrtrouller kynges houshold wardeyne gouernour chambre people ther chose hym worthy men cyte shreues wyth hym gouerne kepe ye kynges lawes cyte one called gelbert mawefelde thomas ne wenton shreues ye mayer two shreues alderman wyth worthy craftes london wente foot vnto toure london came conestable towre gaaf mayer ye shreues theyr othe charge sholde haue taken escheker westmynster ye kynges court iustyces baron escheker went home ayen kynge hys counseyll grete malyce despyte yt cyte london remeued courtes westmynster vnto cyte yorke yt saye chauceler escheker kynges bynche comune place helde courtes lawe fro mydsomer saye feest saynt iohn baptyst vnto feest crystmasse next comynge kynge hys counseyll sawe proffytale london anone remeued yt ayen lodon soo westmynster grete ease offycers vauntage kyng comunes reame pand whanne people london saw knewe courtes come ayen kynge hys people also mayer alderman chyef comunes cyte gaue grete somme golde comunes cyte ordeyned made grete ryaltees ayen hys comynge london haue hys grace good lordshyp also theyr lybertees fraunchyses geauted vnto aye wonte haue afore tyme thrugh grete instaunce prayer quene lordes ladyes kynge grau ted theym grace done shene sutherey kynge within two dayes came london mayer ye cyte shreues alderme worthy men afterwarde rode ayenst hym good araye vnto hethe hys syde shene mayer submyttynge theym homely mekely maner obeyssaunce vnto hym oughten thus brought ye kynge quene london whan ye kynge came yate london brydge presenttd hym wyth mylke whyte stede sadled brydled trapped wyth cloth golde reed partyed gyder quene palfrey alle whyte ararye trappyd white andreed al conduytes london ranne wyth wyne whyte reed maner people drynke wolde bytwene saynt poules crosse chepe made stage ryall standynge vpon hygh theyn many angelles dyuers melodyes songes angelle came downe frome stage hyghe vyce sete crowne golde pyght wyth ryche perles precyous stone vpon kynges heed vpon quenes heed soo cytezeyns brought kyng quene westmynster theyr palays morne mayer ye shreues alderman london camen vnto kynge hys palays att westmynster presente hym two basyns syluer ouergylted full coyned golde somme xx houdred pounde prayenge hym hygh mercy grace lordshyp specyally grace myght haue good loue lybertees fraunchyses lyke wyse wote haue tymes letter patentes chartre confermed quene worthy lorde ladyes fell ther knee besoughte kynge grace conferme kynge toke vp quene graunted hyr hyr askenge thanked kynge quene wente home ayen pand xvi yere kyng rychardes regne certayn lordes scotlonde came englond gete worshyp foot armes persones erles marre chaleged erle marshall englond iuste hym certayne poyntes horsbak wyth sharpe speres rode togyder two worthy knyghtes lordes certayne course full chalenge scottes erle made calle bothe hors man two hys rybbes broke falle borne thes smythfelde home inne within lytyll tyme caryed home hors lytter att yorke deyed pand syr wayllyam darell knyght kynges banerer scotlonde made chalenge wyth syr peres courtayne knyght kynges banerer englonde certayne course yet horsbacke felde whan ryden certayne cours assayed myghte haue better gaaf ouer wold nomore chalenge syr pers courtayne knyght kyng banerer englonde torned hors rode home vnto hys owne inne one cockeborne squyre scotlonde chalenged syr nycholl haberke knyght certayn course yet wyth sharpe speres roden fyue course togyder euery course scot caste downe hors man thus ouer englysshe lordes thanked god hadde felde pand xvii yere kyng rychardes regne deyde good gracyous quene anne wyt kyng rycharde manere shene shyre surrey vpon wytsondaye broughte london soo westmynster buryed worthely entered besyde saynt edwardes shryne whoos sowle almyghty god haue pyte hys mercy amen phow kynge rycharde spowsed dame isabell kynges doughter fraunce towne calays broughte hyr englond lette hyr crowned quene abbaye saynt peter westmynstre xx yere kynge rychardes regne wente hymselfe ouersee vnto calays wih duke erles lordes baron many worthy squyes wyth grete araye comune people reame good araye longed suche kynge prynce hys noble hys owne persone hym reuerence obseruauce oughte done theyr lyege lorde myghty kynge emperoure hys owne abyde receyue worthy gracyous lady shold hys wyf yonge creature xix yere aege dame isabell kynges doughter frauce worthy lordes greate name bothe baron knyghtes wyth moche people yt camen towne grauenynge tow duke fraunce one duke burgoyn duke barre wolde furtherlesse hadde pledge kynge rycharde delyuered two pledge go sauf come saufe two worthy vncles duke gloucestre duke yorke two wente ouer water grauenynge abode pledge tyme yt maryage done two duke fraunce come ayen vnto grauenynge water two worthy duke came ouer water grauenynge calays worthypfull lady dame isabell kynges doughter fraunce hyr came many worthy lorde eke lady knyghtes squyres beest araye myght brought hyr wne calays receyued sole mpnyte worshyp yt myght done vnto suche lady brought hyr vnto kynge kynge toke hyr welcomed hyr hyr fayre company made solempnyte myghte done pand kynge counseyll asked frensshe lordes whether couenauntes forwardes wyth composycyon wer ordeyned made bothe partyes sholde truely kepte holde bytwene theym saye ye swore toke theyr charge vpon boke made theyr othe well truly holde alle maner poyntes couenauntes wythout contradyccyon delay ony maner wyse brought saynt nycholas chyrche calays worthely wedded wyth moost solempnyte ony kyng quene myght wyth archebysshops bysshoppes mynystres hooly chyrche brought castell sette mete serued delycasye ryall mete drynkes pleteuously al maner strau gers creature warned feest welcome grete halle tentes set vpon grene wythout castell receyue manere people euery offyce redy serue thus worthy maryage soleply done ended ryalte two worthy duke fraun e theyr people token theyr leue kynge quene wente ayen vnto grauenynge water frensshe lordes saye twoo duke theyr menye comen ouer water grauenynge mette wyth two duke euery chone toke leue soo departed lordes camen ayen vnto calays frensshe lordes went ouer water soo home fraunce ayen pand anone kynge made hym redy quene lordes ladyes theyr people theim came ouer see englonde vnto london mayer shreues wyth alle alderman worthy commens roden ayenst vnto blacke kent mette kynge quene welcomed theym good araye euery men clothynge craft theyr mynstrels brought theym vnto saynt george barre south warke token theyr leue kynge quene rode kenyngton peple london torned home ayen tornynge ayen london brydge soo greate presse people bothe hors foot deed brydge xi persones men woman child who soules al myghty god haue mercy pyte amen pand afterwarde quene brought towre london alle nyght morne brought thruge cyte london forthe vnto westmynster crowned quene englond broughte ayen vnto kynges palays holden open ryall feest al hyr coronacyon maner peple heder come thys done sondaye nexte feest saynt clemente xx yere kynge rychardes regne xxv daye august next veyll excytacyon fals counseyll grete wrath malyce kyng olde tyme vnto vncle good duke gloucestre erle arundell erle warwyk anone kynge euuyll excytacyon euyll counseyll malyce late euenynge daye aboue sayd made hym redy wyth strenth rode estsex vnto ye towne chemesforde soo come plasshe sodenly syr thomas wodstok ye good duke gloucestre laye good duke came welcome kynge anone kynge arested good duke hymself wyth owne body ladde downe wa anone put shype anone calays brought capytayns warde kepte holde kynges commaundement englonde ye tyme therle marchall capytayne calays anone commaundement kyng fals counseyl commaunded capytayne put hym deth pand anone certayne yemen good duke kepynge toke theyr counseyl shold put hym vnto deth theyr appoyntemente sholde comen vppon hym whan bedde slepe fetheren bedde anone bounde honde foot charged hym lye styll whan hadde done thus token twoo smale towelles made theym two rydynge knottes caste towelles hys necke tooke fetheren bedde laye vnder hym cast aboute hym drewe theyr welles eche wayes laye vpon ye fetheren bed vpon hym vnto tyme dede bycause shold make noys thus strangled thys worthy duke vnto deth vppon who soule god hygh pyte haue mercy amen pand whan kynge hadde rested thus worthy duke vncle sente hym calays came ayen london haste wyth wonder greate people soone comen sent erle aurundell good erle warwyk anone came arested theym hymself syr iohan cobham syr iohn chyne knyghtes arested theym maner tyll made parlement anone put holde erle arundell went att large vnto parlement tyme founde soffycyent suerte abyde ye lawe answere manere poyntes kynge counseyll wolde put vpon hym pand xxi yere kynge rychardes regne ordeyned hym parlement att westmynster whiche called greate parlemente parlement made iuge thys thre worthy lordes moo lyst tyme iugement kynhe lete make hast loge hous large tybre whiche called halle couered tyles ouer open aboute sydes maner men myght se thrugh dome holden vpon forsayd lordes iugement gyue forsayde parlemente come vnto parlement kynge sent hys wryttes euery lorde baron knyght euery squyre euery shyre thrugh oute englode euery lorde sholde gadre bringe retenue hym shorte beste araye myghte gete maintenynge strengthyng kyng ayenst theym hys enemyes done haste come hym payne deth kynge hymself sent chestreshyre cheyftayns countre gadred brought grete huge company people bothe knyghtes squyres prencypally yome chestreshyre whyche yemen archer kynge tooke hys owne courte gaate bowge court good wage kepers owne body bothe nyght daye aboue persones moste loued beste truste whyche soone afterwarde torned kynge grete losse shame hyndrynge hys vtterly vndoynge destruccyon ye shall afterwarde tyme came syr henry derby grete menye armes archer erle rutlonde came wyth stronge power people bothe men mare archer erle kente brought greate power men armes archer erle marshall came manere lorde spenser manere erle northumberlonde syr henry percy sone syre thomas percy erles brother worthy lordes broughte fayre menye stronge power eche man hys beste araye duke lancastre duke yorke came maner wyth men armes archer folowynge kynge syr wyllyam strop tresourer englond came manere thus thys araye came worthy men londe vnto kynge peple came london one daye moche euery strete lane london subarbes full lodged x xii mylle london euery waye people brought kynge westmynster wente home ayen theyr lodgynge bothe hors mondaye xii daye septembre parlemente began att westmynster whiche called grete parlemet pand frydaye nexte erle arundell broughte parleamente amonge lordes saynte mathewas daye appostle euangelyst iuged vnto dethe thys halle made palays westmynster iugemente sholde go foot wyth hys hondes bounde behynde hym frome place iuged forth thrugh cyte london vnto toure hylle hys heed smyten done dede place vi grettest lordes sate iugemente roden wyth hym vnto ye place done dethe se excucyon done dome kynges comaundemente wyth wente foot men armes archer grete multytude chestreshyre men strenthynge lordes yt broughte thys erle hys dethe dredde leste terle sholde rescowed taken whan come london thus passed forthe cytye vnto dethe tooke full pacyenly whoos soule god haue mercy amen pand come frere austyns tooke vp body hede good erle bare home theyr place buryed hym theyr quyre morne syr rycharde erle warwyk brought parlemente erle arundell iuged gaf erle warwyk iugement ye sayd erle lordes compassyon hym cause getoer age released hym perpetuall pryson put hym ylonde man thenne mondaye nexte lord iohanne cobham kent syr iohan cheyn knyghtes also brought parlemente halle iuged hanged drawen thrugh prayer grete instaunce lordes iugement foryeuen released perpetuall pryson pand yere rycharde wyttyngdon mayer london iohan wodecoke wyllyam askam shreues london pand ordeyned euery yate london durynge thys parlemet stronge wache men armes archer thrughout euery warde also kynge made v duke one markeys foure erles fyrst erle derby made duke herforde seconde also erle rutlonde made duke awemarle therde erle kent made duke surre fourth ye erle hu tyngdon made duke excestre fyft erle notyngham made duke northfolke erle somerset made markeys dorseet ye lorde spenser made erle gloucestre lorde leuyll raby made erle westmer londe syr thomas percy made erle worcestre syr wyllyam scrope tresourer englod made erle wylteshyre syr iohn montagu erle salysbury whan kynge thus done helde parlemet ryall feest vnto lordes maner people thyder wolde come pand yere deyed syr iohn gaut kynges vncle duke see malyce kyng anone thre worthy lordes comaunded defended kyng reame anone gate theym shyppes dyuerse haues wente ouer see dyuerse londes eche waye ye duke northfolke wente venece deyed who soule chertres made theym enseled maner ryche men thrughout reame moche copelled dyuerse people sette theyr sea therto pand thys done grete couetyse wherfore good hertes reame clene torned away fro kynge euer vtterly dystruccyon ende hym hygh excellente prince kynge thrugh couetous fals counseyll falsly betrayed ala pyte suche kyng myght se pand kynge rycharde sette kyngdome hys ryall londe englonde ferme vnto foure persones whiche syre wyllyam strop erle wyltshyre tresourer englonde syr iohan busshe henry greue syr iohan bagot knyghtes whiche torned theym myscheyf dethe wythin lytell tyme ye shalle fynde afterwarde wryten pand kynge rycharde made grete ordynaunce wente hymselfe ouer see irlond many grete lordes hym wyth grete hoste strenth theyr kyng wyth armes archer moche grete stuffe ryght good ordynaunce longed vnto warre passed ouer see ordeyned made syr edmode langley vncle duke yorke hys lyueteaunte englonde hys absence gouernauce counseyll foure knyghtes taken englond ferme kynge passed see came irlonde wel worthely receyued rebelles ben called wylde irysshmen came downe kynge yolde hym body goodes owne wyll swore vnto hym lyege men dyde hym homage feaute good seruyse thus conquered moost parte irlonde alytyll tyme pand whyle kynge rycharde thus irlonde syr henry bolyngbroke erle derby kyng made duke herforde whyche duke kynge exyled londe comen ayen enlonde chalenge dukedome lancaster ryght trew herytage came downe fraunce londe vnto calays met hym syr thomas arudell archebysshop caunterbury exyled englode hym came erle arudell sone heyre whiche kepyng syr iohn shelly knyght somtyme erle hutindon duke excestre whyche tho castell reygate soutsex stale hym waye came calays keped well worthely tyll two lordes comen calays pand worthy duke syr thomas arundell archebysshop caunterbury shypped hauen calais drewe theyr cours norwarde aryued yorke shyre rauensporne faste wydlyngton came en red fyrste londe two lordes hym theyr nauye moche people reame whan herde comynge knewen anone drewen vnto hym welcomed lordes soo gaaf theym courage manere thynge passed forthe londe gadred moche people pand whan kyng rycharde hede wyste twoo lordes comen ayen stewarde wist knewe anone came halle amonges people brake yerde ryall kynges housholde anone euery man dysparple wente hys waye forsoke theyr mayster souerayne lord lefte hym allone thus kynge rycharde broughte downe destroyed stode hymself allone wythout comforth socoure yf ony good counseyll ony ala pyte ryall kynge anone came worde syre henry bolyngbroke vp stronge powre people squyres bagot escaped frome theym wente ouer see irlonde sethre knyghtes taken theyr hedes smyte thus dyed theyr fals couetoyse pand kynge rycharde taken brought vnto ye duke anone duke put hym fast warde chaunged thrugh oute englonde kynge counseyll yt saye ye noble half noble ferthynge golde pand xiiii yere kyng henryes regne fourth lete make galays warre hoped haue passed grete see forth iherusalem haue ended hys lyf god vysyted hym soone infyrmytees grete sekenesse yt myght well endure whyle feruently taken brought bedde westmynster fayre thambre laye hed asked hys chaberlayll called chambre laye answered sayd iherusalem sayde prophecye sayd yt shold make ende deye iherusale made dyd vnto god dysposed wyll dyed caryed water westmynster barge vnto feuersham then caryed caunterbury londe moche torche lyght brennynge abbaye crechyrche entered buryed besyde saynt thomas caunterburyes shryne thus ended worthy kynge henry mydlente sondaye yere oure lorde mcccc xxi vppon whoos soule god haue mercy amen martyn v pope iohn xiii yere man chosen counseyll constantynoble deposed strof came pea chyrche whiche longe tyme afore desyred necessarye defence fayth myghtyest pope yt euer rychesse grete iuge edefyed townes walles stretes destroyed heresyes dyde moche good thrughe noble prynce sygysmonde gadred moche moneye geten holy londe ayen deth came vppon hym letted hym made counseyll afore deth ye mater decessyd peugenius pope martyn xvii yere eugenius chosen peasyble ye deth martyn man doubted pope soon expulsed frome rome fledde naked also cyted counseyll basylyens deposed dyscharged hym bega stryffe ayen whiche stode deth yt fauoured hym sayde worthe moche louynge contrary sayde ayenst hym someuer taken dygnyte vpon hym afore grete obstynaunce gode fame dyde leue iugement god pcirca annu dm mccccxxi pof kynge henry fyfte kynge henryes sone deth kynge henry fourth regned kyge hery sone borne monmouthe wale worthy kynge gracyous grete conquerour pand fyrste yere hys regne grete loue goodnesse sente ferres langley fader burye kinge rychard secode lete take body erthe ayen dyde brynge westmynster ryal chare couered blacke veluet baners dyuerse armes aboute hors drawynge chare trapped blacke beten dyuerse armes many torche brennynge waye tyll came westmynster lete make hym ryall solempne enteremente buryed hym quene anne wife owne desyre ferther syde saynt edwardes shryne abbaye saynt peter westmynster who soule god haue mercy amen pand yere certayne lollers taken fals herytykes purposed thrugh fals treason haue slayne oure kyng haue destroyed clargye reame myghte haue theyr fals purpose lorde god wolde suffre haste kynge hadde warnynge therof alle theyr fals ordynaunce werkinge came sodenly power saynt iohans withoute smythfelde anone toke certanye lollers fals herytykes broughte kynges presence tolde fals purpose ordynaunce howe wolde haue doo wrought yf myghte haue regned hadde theyr wyll tolde whyche theyr capytayens gouernours ye kynge commaunded theym towre london thanne toke moo theym bothe within cytye wythoute sente newgate bothe counteers thanne broughte examycyon clergye kynges iustyces conuycted theyr fals heresie dampned iustyce theyr fals treason pand theyr iugement sholde drawen frome towr london saynt gelys felde hanged brente galowes pand taken syr roger acton knyghte heresye eke treason ayenste kynge reame came afore clergye conuy te heresye dampned iustyce drawen frome towre london thrughe cyte saynt gelys hanged brente pand seconde yere kynge henryes regne fyfthe helde counseylle alle lordes reame atte westmynster putte hym demaunde prayed besought theyr goodnesse theyr gode counseyll wylle shewe hym touchynge tytle ryghte hadde normande gascoyne guyhen whiche kynge fraunce wythelde wrongfully vntyghte fully whyche hys auncestrees hym hadde trewe tytle conquest ryghte heretage whiche normandye gascoyn guyhen good kynge edwarde wyndesore hys auncestres hym hadde holden theyr lyues tyme lordes gaaf hym counseyl sendde enbassatours vnto kynge fraunce hys counseyll sholde gyue vp vnto hym hys ryght herytage saye normandye gascoyne guyhen whiche predecessours hadde holden afore hym el wold wyne wyth strength swerde shorte tyme helpe almyghty god pand thanne dolphyn fraunce answered oure enbassatours sayde thys manere kynge ouer yonge terder aege comak ony warre ayenste hym lyke yet good warroure doo make suche aconqueste vppon hym somwhat scorne dyspyte sente hym tonne fulle tenes balles bycause wolde haue som playe wyth alle hym lordes wolde come hym better thenne mayntene ony warre pand thenne anone oure lordes werre enbassatours tooke theyr leue came englonde ayen tolde kynge hys counseyll vngoodly answere dolphyn present ye whyche sent kynge pand whan kynge herde theyr wordes answere dolphyn woder sore agreued ryght euyll apayed towarde frensshemen towarde kyng dolphyn thought auenge hym soone god wold sende grace myght anoe lette make tenes balles dolphyn hast myght grete gonstones ye dolphin playe anone ye kynge sente hys lordes helde grete counseyll westmynster tolde vnto answere yt dolphyn worthy prese te sent hym lordes playe kyng lordes accorded yt sholde redy armes wyth ther pow r best araye myght done gete men armes archer yt myght goten stuff longed warre redy wyth theyr retenue mete atte southampton lammasse next folowyng without ony delaye wherfore kyng ordeyned nauye shyppes manre stuffe vytayll ye longed suche warryoure maner ordynauce haue southampton nombere ccc xx saylles felle greate dysease foule myschef iii lordes whyche kynge trusted moche thrugh fals couetyse purposed ymagyned kynges deth thought haue slayne hym bretherne taken ye see whiche thre lordes named thus syre rycharde erle chambrydge broder duke yorke seconde lorde scrop tresourer englonde thyrde syr thomas gray knyght north countre thre lordes afore sayd lucre money hadde made promesse vnto frensshmen haue slayne kynge henry fyfte alle brethern fals trayne sodaynly ware god almyghty helde hys holy honde ouer saued peryllous menye haue done thys receyued frensshemen myllyon golde openly knowen theyr fals treason al thre iuged vnto deth iugemet sholde laadde thrughe hampton withoute northgate heded thus ended theyr lyues thyr false couetyse treason anone done kynge men ye made redy wente shyppes saylled forthe wyth fyften hondred shyppes aryued seyn kydecause vpon ladyes euen assumpcyon normady wyth hys ordynau ce went forth harflet besyeged towne alle aboute londe eke water sent capytayne towne charged hym delyuer towne capytayne sayd yt wolde delyuer hym none wolde hym yelde bad hym best kynge layd hys ordynaunce vnto twone saye gonne engynnes trypgettes shotten caste att walles eke vnto towne caste downe towres towne layd theym vnto erthe played att tenes wyth hys harde gon stone pand within towne whan shold playe theyr songes well awaye ala euer suche tenes balles made cursyd tho warre began tyme euer borne pand morne kyng dyd crye att euery gate towne euery man sholde redy morne erly make assaute vnto ye towe wyllyam boucher iohan graunte wyth xii burgeys worthy men came kynge besought hym hys ryall pryncehode power wythdrawe malyce destruccyon dyd besought hym viii dayes respyce trewes yf ony rescowe myghte come theym el yelde vp towne vnto hym wyth theyr goodes kyng sent forthe capytayne kept remenaunt styll hym ye lorde gaucort capytayn towne went forth royn al hast vnto dolphyn helpe socour none ne man rescowe dolphyn wold abyde thus capytayne come ayen vnto kynge yelded vp towne delyuered hym key bad hym go put frensshmen men woman chyldren stuff hys towne har et wyth englysshe people kynge sente englonde dyde crye euery good towne englonde crafty man wolde come thydes enhabyte hym towne sholde haue house housholde hym heyres euer pand soo tho wete many dyuerse marchauntes crafty men enhabyte theym strength towne welcome pand whan kynge sawe thys towne well stuffed vytayls worthy prince toke leue went calays warde londe frensshme herd comyng thought haue stopped hym way shold passe waye hast myght braken alle brydges ony passage hors man moche myght man passe ouer ryuer nother horse ne foot yf shold haue drowned therfore kynge people wente sought thys waye ferre vp parys warde ther ryall power fraunce assembled redy gyue hym batayll dystroye alle people almyghte god hys guyde saued hym al menye defended hym hys enmyes power purpose thanked god saued hys owne knyght kynge ryghtfull tytle pand kynge holdynge seyenge grete multytude nombre enmyes wythstande way gyue hym batayll kynge wyth meke herte good spyryte lyft vp hondes almyghty god souhht hym hys helpe socoure daye saue trewe seruauntes oure kynge gadred lordes peple bad gode sholde haue fayre daye gracyous vyctorye better theyr enemyes prayed alle make redy vnto batayll wolde rather deed daye felde taken enmyes wold neuer put reame englonde raumsome persone pan duke yorke fell hys knee besought ye kynge aboue wolde grau te hym daye auauntwarde hys batayll kynge grauntyd hym hys askynge sayd gramercy cosyn yorke praied hym make hym redy hadde euery man ordeyne hym stake tree sharpe endes ye stake myght pyght erthe slope theyr enemyes sholde ouercome horsback fals purpose arayed ouer ride enmye sodaynly att fyrste comynge fyrste brunte nyght batayll frensshmen made many grete fyers moche reuyll howtynge showtynge playd kynge hys lordes dyse archer alwaye blanke theyr money wede yt theyrs morne arose daye ganne spynge kynge good auyse lete araye hys batayll wynges charged euery kepe hoole togyder prayed alle good whan redy asked tyme day sayd pryme sayd kynge good tyme englond prayed v therfore good chere lete v goo oure iourney sayde wyth hyghe voys name almyghty god saynt george auaunce baner saynt george thys day thyn helpe pand frensshemen came pryckynge downe wold haue ouer ryden meny god oure archer made ryght sone stomble archer shote neuer arowe amysse perysshed brought vnto ye grou de hors man shote day wager stake made theym toppe ouer terue eche one ouer laye onhepes two hepes lenth hyghe kynge menye men armes archer sthacked soo thycke arowes layd staues ky ge wyth hodes fought maly daye thus god almyghty saynt george brought oure enmyes groude gaf v daye vyctory werre slayne frensshmen ye daye felde agyngcourt moo xi thousand wyth prysoners taken nombred daye frensshme felde moo syr score thousande god daye faughte v came tydynges kynge new batayll frensshmen ordeyned redy stele hym came towardes hym anone oure kynge lette crye euery man sholde doo slee hys prysoners hadde taken anone make theym ayen redy fyghte wyth frensshe men whan saw men kylled downe theyr prysoners dyde wythdrawe brake theyr batayll araye thus kynge worthy conquerour daye vyctory felde agyngcourte pycardye oure kynge retorne ayen batayll see people slayne englysshmen yf ony hurt myght holpen deed felde duke barrye ye duke alausome ye duke braban erle nauerne chyef constable fraunce viii erles archebysshop sauce gode baron hondred mo worthy knyghtes greate alyauce cote armures thousande v hondred enelysshe men deed duke yorke ye erle southfolke englysshmen deed passynge xxvi bodyes thanked god batayll fryday whyche saynt cryspyne crispymanes daye moneth octobre anone kynge commauded bury duke yorke caryed forth wyth hym erle southfolke prysoners duke orlyauce duke burbon erle vendome erle ewe erle rychemonde syr bursygaunt marchall frau ce many worthy lordes taken batayll agyngcourte broughte vnto towne calays ouer see wyth kynge englonde landed douer kente prysoneres saufte thanken bo god almyghty came caunterbury offred saynt thomas shryne rode forthe thrught countre kente nexte waye vnto eltham rested tyll wolde come london mayer london alderman shreues wyth worthy comuners craftes came blacke hethe well worthely arayed welcome kynge dyuer melodyes thanked almyghty god hys gracyous vyctory shewed hym kynge hys prysoners passed forthe theym tyll came saynt thomas waterynge mette hym relygyous men processyon welcomed hym soo kynge came tydynge wyth hys prysoners thrugh cyte london shewed many fayr syght conduytes crosse chepe heuenly araye angells archaugelles patryarkes prophetes virgynes dyuerse melodyes sensynge synginge welcome kynge alle conduytes rennynge wyth wyne kynge passed forthe saynt poules mette wyth hym xiiii bysshopes reuessed mytred sensers welcome kynge songe hys gracyous vyctory tedeum laudamus kynge offred toke hors rode westmynster mayer tooke hys leue kynge rode home ayen pand ye thyrde yere kynge henryes regne fyfth come emperour almayne kynge rome hungrye englonde cyte london mayer alderman wyth shreues worthy craftes london kynges comaundement mette hym blacke hethe best araye coude horsbacke welcomed hym broughte hym vnto london moche honour greate reuerence saynt thomas wateryng mette hym kyng wyth lordes gode araye worthy metynge bytwene emperour kyng henry fyfte kyssed togyder enbraced eche kynge tooke emperour honde came rydynge thrugh cyte london vnto saynt poules alyghted offred alle bysshoppes stode reuesshed wyth sensers theyr hodes sengynge theym tooke theyr horse rode vnto westmynster kynge lodged emperoure hys owne palays rested hym greate whyle alle kynges coste pand soone came duke hollande englonde come se emperoure speke wyth hym wyth kynge hery englode worthely receyued lodged bysshops inne ely kynges coste pand whan emperour welle rested hym seen londe dyuerse partyes knewe commodytes tha processe tyme tooke hys leue kynge yode made knyght garter reteyned wered ye lyueray thanked kynge hys lordes kynge wente ouer see vnto calays aboden longe tyme haue answere frensshe kynge ye laste came plesed hym ryght noughte emperour toke leue ye kynge passed forth goddes name oure kynge came ouer aye englonde hast myght saynt lucas euen came lambythe mondaye nexte came ye parlemete atte westmynster pand yere grete derth corne englond thanked god lasted longe fourth yere kynge henryes regne fyfthe helde hys parleamente atte westmynster begynnynge octobre laste puryfycacyo lady nexte graunted vnto hym mayntene warres spyrytualtee teporalte hoole dyeme anone kynge prayed hys lordes make redy strengthe hym ryght anone lete make newe retenue charged al redy hampton wytson weke next wyth ony delaye kynge made duke bedford protectour defender reame englode hys absence charged hym kepe hys lawes mayntene bothe spyrytuall temporall whan kynge thus sette thynge kynde saynt markes daye toke hys hors atte westmynster came ridynge poules offred tooke leue rode forthe thrugh cyte takenge hys leue maner people well poore ryche prayenge theym generall praye hym rode forth saynt george offrede toke leue mayer chargynge hym kepe well chambre rode forth hampton abode tylle retenue redy come al nauye shyppes wyth hys ordynaunce gadred togyder well stuffed longed suche ryall kynge wyth manere vytayls suche ryall people welle hors man longed suche warryoure saye gonne trypgytes engynes sowes bastyles brydges letge sclynynge ladder malles spade shoueles pyckes pauys bowes arowes bowes strynges tone chestes pypes fulle arowes neded suche worthi warryoure noo thynge seche wha ne tyme come thyder came hym shyppes laden gonne gonpoudre pand whan redy hys retenue come ye kynge lordes wyth alle hys ryall hooste wente shyp tooke see sayled normandye londed touke vpon lammasse daye nexte made xlviii knyghtes att londynge kynge herynge many enmyes vpon see saye ix greate carackes huskes galays shyppes comynge dystroye nauye anone commau ded erle marche chyef chyeftayne many worthy lordes wyth hym men armes archer goo ye see none enemyes defouled hys nauye ne entred vyage ne iourney anone erle toke hys menye went shyp scommed see kepte see costes noo manere enmyes durste rowte vpon see anone kynge sente hys heraudes vnto capytayne touke charged hym delyuer hym hys castell hys towne el wolde neyther leue man ne chylde alyue anone capytayne foure burgeses towne brought keyes kynge besought hym grace kynge delyuered keyes syr iohan kyke e made hym capytayne comaunded hym put frensshmen bothe castell towne besyde castell louers thyder kynge sente erle marchall wyth fayremenye assauted ye towne anone yolden erle brought hym keyes brought kynge kynge tooke hym ayen made hym capytayne castell louers longed therto charged hym delyuer alle frensshme kynge helde forth hys way cane yt stronge towne fayre ryall castell therin anone sent heraudes capytayne charged hym delyuer towne castell el wolde gete theym strenght honde answered sayde toke none kepe ne none wolde delyuere vnto hym anone layde syege vnto towne layde gonne euery syde caste done bothe walles towres slewe moche people theyr house also stretes good duke clarence layde downe walles syde vnto ye bare groande wyth whyle kynge counseylle assauted towne anone duke clarence entred towe slewe downe ryght tyll came kynge spared nother man chylde euer cryed clarence clarence saint george deede walles kynges syde worthy called sprynges yt whiche ye kynge comaunded buryed abbaye canefast wyllyam conquerour who soule god huue mercy amen kynge came towe wyth hys broder duke clarence many worthy lordes wyth moche solemnyte myrthe ye kynge comaunded capytayne delyuer hym castell besought ye kynge gyue hym xiiii dayes respyte yf ony rescowe wolde come yf none wolde come delyuer hym keyes castell comaundement vnder comeposycion ye towne castell bayou townes fortress vyl age nobre xiiii vpon hylle fore castel cane kynge pyght tentes semed towne moche cane tyme came tydynges none resowe wolde come xiiii dayes ende capytayne castell came deliuered keyes castell kynge bayou xiiii townes xv knyghtes bathe syr lowes robert salyn chaynye mougomerye many worthy men kynge comaunded put frensshemen woman man hardy defoule woman ne take noo manere good awaye frome theym let passe pea payne dethe passed oute towne one daye moo xv hondred woman kynge lete stuffe towne castell englysshemen ordeyned twoo capytayns one ye towne castell pand charged theym vppon theyr lyues kepe well towne castell oure kyng wente then gate valeys newelyn layde asyege chyrburgh seyge layde duke gloucestre wyth stronge power myghty processe tyme made ther capytayne towne pand tyme good eerle warwyk layed seyge vnto donnfronte gate put therin capteyne speke eerle marche kynge ordeyned tho scomme see kepe costes englonde manere enmyes wynde rose vppon theym wende haue loste thorough grace almaghty god good gouernaunce rodden afore yle wyght storme ther loste two carackes twoo balyngers wyth marchaundyse grete goodes al people within theym caracke broke vp hampton threwe maste ouer walles towne saynt barthelomeus daye whan storme cessed thys worthy erle marche toke shyppes wyth hys menye wente see londed normandye hogges roden forth wardes ye kynge pand euer came frensshemen fledde came theym anthony pygge folowed hooste alle waye tyll came grete water dradde haue drowned drenched water closed theym soo myghte noo gete oute pbut laste god almyghty thys anthony pygge broughte theym alle saufte oute caughte theym gyde knewe countree aboute brought theym thorough quycke sande forthe ile also toke many prysoners waye warde kynge theyr iourneye men vnto castel cane kynge welcomed hym toke hys iourney atte argentun anone tho yolden kynge theyr lyues wente theyr waye oure kynge remeued vnto stronge towne tho called cese fayer mynster yelde vp anone vnto kynge thanne kynge wente then lausome wanne towne brydge kynge sent erle warwyk towne called belesme wyth grete stronge power anone yelde put al kynges grace hys mercy dyde many stronge townes castels tho partyes then wente vernyll perche anone yolden vnto kynge bothe towne castell bodyes godes kynges good grace kynge gate conquered townes castelles pyle strengthes abbays vnto cyte rone pand fyfth yere kynge henryes regne fyfth syr iohan oldcastell ye lorde cobham arested heresie broughte vnto towre london anone afte brake towre wente wale kepte hym longe tyme att last lord powys toke hym stode att grete defence longe tyme soore wounded wolde taken soo lorde powys men brought hym wale vnto london agayne whyrlcole soo brought westmynster examined certayne pointes put vppon hym sayd naye conuyte ye clargye hys heresye dampned iustyces vnto dethe treason ladde toure ayen layde hurdell drawen thrugh cytye saynt gelys felde made newe payre galowes stronge coler yren hym hanged brete galowes al leudenesse fals opynyons vi yere kynge henrye fyfth sente hys vncle syr thomas beauforde duke excestre fayre menye armes archer cyte rone dyspleyed baner sente herodes vnto towne badde theym yelde cyte vnto kynge theyr lyege lorde sayde tooke none kepe ne none sholde haue yf dere bought meued theyr hondes answere wolde none gyue gonne pand duke toke gode semet ye grounde anone yssued cytee grette menye men armes bothe horsbacke foote anone menye mette wyth ouer trewe greate hepe take slayne xxx persones full ryght good mennys bodyes remenaunt fledde aien towne duke wente vnto pountlarge vnto kynge tolde hym al spedde howe lyked grounde pand anone duke gone caste downe subarbes aboute cyte vnto harde grounde bycause kyng sholde noo refusynge vpon frydaye lammasdaye thanne nexte folowynge onre kynge hoste came rone anone sete hys syege rounde cytye anone lete laye hys ordynaunce vnto towne kynge wyth hys lordes logded wythin chartre house grete strengthe aboute theym eest partye cytee duke clarence lodged hym strengthe power att weste ende waste abbaye proce chanx duke exchestre menye northe syde porte beauuesyn bytwene duke clarence duke excestre erle marchall lodged wyth moche people stronge power castell gate pand thanne erle ormonde lorde haryngton also lorde talbott wyth theyr retenue companye next hym pand thanne syr iohan cornewayle manye othere noble knyghtes squyres name wyth theyr retenue laye wyth noble duke clarence pand thanne frome duke excestre towardes kynge lodged lorde roos lorde wylleby wyth lorde phehewe syre wyllyam porter knight theyr retenue porte saynt hyllary thane erle mortaye retenne lodged abbaye saynte katherynes pand erle salesbury wyth hys retenue laye syde saynt katherynes syr iohan graye knyght lodged att abbaye called mounte du saynt mychel syr phylyp leche knyght kynges tresourer lodged bytwene water seyn abbaye kept warde vnder hylle baron carowe lodged vnder water syde kepe passage ienyco squyre laye nexte hym water syde two squyres kept manly water seyn fought theyr enmyes oft tymes syde seyn laye ye erle hontyngdon master neuyll erles sone westmer london syr gylbert vm reuyll erle keme syr rycharde erle arundell lorde feryers wyth theyr retenue porte du poute eche lordes stronge ordynauce kynge dyde make poutlarge ouer water seyn stronge amyghty chayne iron put yt thrught grete pylis fast pyght grounde wente ouer ryuer seyn vessell myght passe yt kynde aboue chayn kynge lete make brydge ouer water seyn man hors caryage myght go fro tymes wha nede came ye erle warwyke goten doufronte vnto kynge henry englonde anone kynge sent erle warwyk cawdebeke seyge yt whan came towne sente heraudes vnto capytayne badde hym yelde vp towne vpon payne dethe anone layde sege capytayne besought erle myght come vnto hys presence pleased hym speke wyth hym soo good erle grauted hym come came oute foure burgeys came wyth hym entreated soo wyth erle towne vnder composycyon done cyte rome dyde erle graunted consented tho vpoon thys condycyon kynges nauye englonde wyth hys ordynaunce myghte passe theym saufte ony manere lette dysturbaunce composycyon sete theyr seales shyppes passed vp saufte came cytee rone hondred shyppes caste theyr ankers thanne thys cyte besyeged bothe londe water whan done shyppes comen vp came erle warwyke ayen kyng lodged hym bytwene abbaye saynt katherynes kyng tyll abbaye enteraced yolden vnto kynge thanne remeued hym then lodged hym porte martenuylye tho erle salysbury commaunded kynge make hym redy ryde came hasty tydynges made hym abyde soo retorned ayen lodged hym besyde good erle huntyngdon tylle syege ended pand thenne came good duke gloucestre kynges brother syege chyrbourghe whiche hadde goten stuffid agayne vnto kynges behoue profyte vnto crowne englond whan comen kynge rone lodged greate ordynaunce porte saynt hyllary nerer towne hys enmyes thenne ony laye xl roddes lenthe within shote quarell wyth hym laye erle southfolke lorde bergeyeney wyth hys retenue stronge ordynaunce manly proudly faughte euery day wyth theyr enmyes euer whan yssued cyte pand thanne came pryoure kylmayne irlonde ouer see kynge wyth fayr meny armes theyr owne countree gyse somme xvi hondred good mennys bodyes kyng welcomed theym made theym goode pand thanne came thydynges vnto kynge kynge frauce dolphyn duke burgoyne wolde come downe rescowe cyte rone stronge power manere nacyons breke syege casteth hym entre northe syde hooste cause beste entrynge moost playne kynge assyned pryoure kylmayne wyth power lodged hym northe syde hoste stoppe theyr passage foreste lyon ordynaunce full gladde went forthe haste kepte grounde place kyng counseyll assygned quyte good warryours vnto thyer kynge pnow wyll tell whyche chyef capytayns gouernoure cytee rome monsyr uy boteler cheyf capytayne bothe cyte castell mon syre teymygan capytayne porte canx mon syr de al roche capytayne dysners mon syr anthony lyuetenaut mon syr guy botyler henry chantfyen capytayne porte dela pounte iohan materuas capytayne porte de la castell mon syr de preant capytayne porte saynt hyllary bastarde tyne capytayn ye porte martenuylle graunt iakes worthy warryoure capytayne al warre wy gouernour outwarde horsbacke foot men armes whan yssued cytee porte arayed al sholde encountre menye eche capytayns ladde fyue thousande men armes moo fyrste comynge kynge theyr nombred heroudes thre hundred thousande wome chyldren yonge olde amonge many man full man hondes preued whan yssued cytee horsbacke foot came neuer att one gate allone thre foure gate atte euery gate two thre thousande good mennys bodyes armed manfully encoutred englyssme moche people slayne dyuerse tymes wyth gonne quarelles ordynaunce syege dured xx wekes euery towne trusted haue rescowed cam none att laste kepte towne soo lange deyed many thousades within towne defaute mete men chyldren eten theyr horse dogges cattes towne often tymes men armes drofe pore people att gate towne spendynge vytaylles anone englysshmen drofe theym towne ayen soo laste capytayne towne sawe myschyef rescowed also scarsyte vytaylle people deyed soo defaute meete euery daye many thousandes also sawe yonge chyldren lye souke theyr moders pappes deed pthan anone sente kynge besechynge hym hys grace mercye broughte keyes towne vnto kynge delyuered towne hym al soudyours voyed towne theyr horse harnes comunes towne abyde dwelle styll towne yerely paye hym hys successours alle manere customes see fermes katerenes kyng entred towne rested hym castell tyll ye wne sette rule gouernaunce phow kynge englond made enheyrytoure regente frauce wedded quene katheryne anone rone goten depe manye townes basse normandye gaf ouer without stroke syege whan vnderstode kynge goten rone also yere pea made sworne bytwene duke bugoyne dolphyn whiche sworne goddes body sholde loue assysse eche ayenst theyr enemyes contrary othe duke iohn burgoyne slayne pyteously murdred presence dolphyn wherfore frensshmen gretly deuydeb necessyte laboured haue treatye wyth kynge englonde kynge englonde wanne dayely townes castels fortress palso thys yere quene iane arested brought vnto castell lede kent one rere radulfe doctour dyuynyte confessour whyche afterwarde slayne persoone toure fallynge wordes debate warde quene iane delyuered pand vii yere kynge frau ce englonde accorded kynge henry made heyre regent fraunce wedded dame katheryne doughter fraunce troyes champayne trynyte sondaye made menne phylyp newe made duke burgoyne whiche sworne kynge henry auenge hys faders deth become englyssh pand thanne kynge wyth hys newe wyfe wente parys ryall receyued then wente wyth lordes duke bourgoyn many lordes fraunce layd syege dyuerse townes castels helde dolphyns partye wanne towne milon helde longe tyme therin good defender viii yere kyng quene came ouer see londed landelmasse daye morne att douer xiiii daye feuerer kynge came london ye xxi daye monthe quene came xxiiii crowned westmynster palso yere anone ester kyng helde palement westmynster whiche parlemente ordeyned golde englysshe coyn sholde weyed none receyued weyght nd anone wytsontyde kynge saylled calays passed forth frauce xxii daye marche kyng came ouer duke clarence slayne fraunce dyuerse lordes taken prysoners erle huntyngdon erle somerset dyuerse bycause wold taken none archer thoughte haue ouercome frensshemen themself without archer yet whan slayne archer came rescowed ye body duke whiche wolde haue caryed god haue mercye soule valyaunte man yere bytwene crystmasse cadelmasse towne mylon yolden vnto kynge pin ii yere saynt nycholas daye decembre borne henry kynges fyrste begoten sone wyndesore who god faders font stone syr henry bysshop wynchestre iohn duke bedford duchesse holonde godmoder henry chychelay archebysshop cauterbury god fader confermynge pand x yere ye cyte mew bry goten whiche ben longe besyeged yere quene shypped hampon sayled ouer kynge fraunce worshypfully receyued kynge also kyng fraynce hyr fader hyr moder thus kynge henry wanne faste fraunce helde grete astate sate greate feest parys crowned ye quene also whiche hadde seen alle people resorted vnto courte kynge fraunce helde none astate ne rule lefte almoost allone palso yere weder toke sete vpon poules steple london yere monethe august kynge waxed seke boy devyncynt whan sawe sholde deye made hys testamet ordeyned many noble thynges hys soule deuoutly receyued ryghtes holy chyrche soo ferre whanne anoynted sayde seruyse preest ye verse spalme miserere mei deus benigne fac dne bona voluntate tuasyon vt edificentur mury iherusalem badde tarye sayd thus good lorde thou knowest myn entente hathe ben yet yf myght lyue redyfye walles iherusalem thanne preest proceded forth made anende anone thys mooste noble prynce dyctoryous kynge floure hys tyme crysten chyualrye whome worlde doubted gaaf hys soule handes god deyed made en de naturall lyfe att sayde boy de vyncent besyde parys ye xxxvi yere hys aege vppon whoos sowle god haue mercy amen pthan body enbamed cyred layd ryall chare ymage lyke hym layde vpvon corp open wyth dyuerse baners horse couered rychely armes englonde fraunce also olde armes saynt edwarde saynt edmonde grete multytude torch whome wente kynge scotlonde many lordes whyche accompanyed body tyll came vnto westmynster london englonde euery towne waye solempnely dyryge eue masse morne moche almes gyuen poore peple ye waye vii daye nouembre ye corp brought thrugh london wyth grete reuerece solempnyte westmynster nowe lyeth worshypfully buryed layd tombe ryal ymage lyke hyself syluer gylde made att cost quene katheryne thus ended entered buryed noble kyng ry ye fyfth vpon whoos soule al cryste soules god haue mercy ame pof ye lawe kynge hery ye fyfth ordeyned kyng rycharde hymself dethe noted kynge henry fyfth noble prynce kynge crowned hys yo gth wylde recheles spared noo thynge hys lust ne desyres accoplesshed lykyng soone crowned enoynted sacred anone sodaynly chaunged newe man set entent lyue vertuously mayntenynge holy chyrche destroyenge heretykes kepynge iustyce defendynge reame subgettes pand moche hys fader deposed hys labour good kyng rycharde pyteously made hym deye offence done hym ayenst legaunce sent rome assoyled therof whiche offece holy fader ye pope enyoyned hym make hym prayed perpetually lyke done take hym naturall lyf therfore shold fyside four taper brene perpetually body extynccon bodely lyf soule may euer remembred lyf heue spyrytual lyfe also sholde euery weke ye daye come aaboute hys deth haue solempne masse requie ye eue afore dyryge wyth ix lesson doole poore peple alwaye daye xi shellynges vii pen deled peny mele one yere annyuersary termete holden ye honest wyse bedeled ye daye xx poude pen poore people euery monke xx shellynge whyche alle thynhes performed thys noble kynge fader kyng henry fourth fader performed durynge hys lyf whome sayd god dyd touche hym lepreor deyed pand also thys noble prynce lette calle ye abbottes pryours saynte benet order englond chapytre hous westmynster reformacyon theyr order wherin comunycacyon also wyth bysshops spyrytualte ferre forth doubted sore wold haue temporaltes myddyll masse fyrste laste masse shall assygned hym apperyeth verse folowynge henrici misse quinti sunt hic tabulate que successiue sunt per monachos celebrate pde dmca prima sit assumpre de festo no flode suppose suche bestes swame ylodes aboute fyrste nexte soo forthe el sayllynge ylondes broughte wyth suche beestes loue hutynge angel god almyghtes comaudemet brought suche bestes ylo de aboute ye erthe brought ye fyrste fulfylled tho goddes comaudemete ye comaun ded ye erthe brynge forth gras quicke bestes phere endeth ye descrypcyo brytayne whiche coteyned englode wale scotlonde also bycause irlode vnd ye rule englo de olde tyme hathe cotynued therfore haue sette ye descrypcyo aft ye sayd brytayne whiche haue take poly cronycon also enprynted one somtyme sco e mayster saynt albons vpon whose soule god haue mercy amen enprynted londo powlys chyrche yarde west dore powly besyde lorde london palays iulyan notary yere lorde god mcccccxv
